ākampakāni śirasaś ca mahā-kavīnāṃ teṣāṃ samuccayam anargham ahaṃ vidhāsye ।। utsṛṣṭāmbara-dṛṣṭa-vigraha-bharā yasya smarāgresarā mārā māra-vadhū-stanāś ca na dadhuḥ kṣobhaṃ sa vo avyāj jinaḥ ।। sa trailokya-guruḥ sudustara-bhavākūpāra-pāraṅgato māra-vyūha-jaya-pragalbha-subhaṭaḥ śāstā tava stān mude ।। yas tu kṣāntyā śamayati śataṃ manmathādīna-rātīn kalyāṇaṃ vo diśatu sa muni-grāmaṇīr arka-bandhuḥ ।।
saṅgha-śriyaḥ । durvāra-māra-parivāra-balāvalepakalpānta-saṃtata-payaḥ-prasarair ahāryaḥ ।। saṃsāra-bhitti-bhiduro bhava-kanda-kandukandarpa-darpa-dalana-vyasanī munīndraḥ ।। te maulau bhavatāṃ milantu jagatī-rājyābhiṣekocitasrag-bhedā abhaya-pradāna-caraṇa-preṅkhan-nakhāgrāṃśavaḥ ।।
deyāt tubhyaṃ avārtha-vīrya-viṭapaḥ kṣānti-prasūnodgamaḥ succhāyaḥ ṣaḍ-abhijña-kalpa-viṭapī-saṃbodha-bījaṃ phalam ।। etau śrīdhara-nandinaḥ । yas tv enaṃ sabalaṃ ca jetum abhitas tat-kampa-mātraṃ bhruvornārebhe sugatas tu tad-guṇa-kathā stambhāya naḥ kevalam ।। kumudākara-mateḥ ।।
ke apy utkarṣaṃ stuvanti smaram api jayatas tad vadāmaḥ kim asmin yo bhasmāsīt kaṭākṣa-jvalana-kaṇikayā drāg umā-kāmukasya ।। āsīd adbhuta-maulir atra-militāṃ vyāttānana-cchāyikām ālokyātmana eva māra-sumaṭaḥ paryasta-dhairyodayaḥ ।। āśliṣyan-madhu-lampaṭāli-nivahasyoccair mithaś cumbanair vyākoṣaḥ kusumāñjalir diśatu vaḥ śreyo nijāyārpitaḥ ।। sukhaṃ tad vaḥ śāstur diśatu śivam ajñāna-rajanīvyavacchedodgacchan mahima-ghana-saṃdhyātapa iva ।।
mārasyāpi śarair abhedya-hṛd iti śraddhābhara-prahvayā pāyād vaḥ sphuṭa-bāṣpa-kampa-pulakaṃ ratyā jino vanditaḥ ।। vandārutridaśaudharatramukuṭotsarpat-prabhā-pallavapratyunmīlad-apūrva-cīvara-paṭaḥ śākyo muniḥ pātu vaḥ ।। vasu-kalpasya । itīvainān nūnaṃ ya iha sumano astratvam anayat sa vaḥ śāstā śastraṃ diśatu daśa-diṅ-māra-vijayī ।।
।। madhūdrāṇāṃ nidrābhiduram apamudrādbhutamudaś cakorān bibhrāṇaṃ sarasiruha-pāṇer avatu vaḥ ।। buddhākara-guptasya । jayati sita-gabhasti-stoma-śubhrānana-śrīḥ sahaja-guru-dayārdrālokano lokanāthaḥ ।।
śrīmat-potalake gabhīra-vivṛti-dhvāna-pratidhvānite sāndra-svāṃśu-caya-śriyā valayito lokeśvaraḥ pātu vaḥ ।। tṛṣārtānām īṣad vitataṃ adharāntaḥ prati gatipraṇālībhiḥ pañcābhavad iti kiṃ anyad bhuja-karāt ।। ravim iva dhṛtāmitābhaṃ kavim iva surasārtha-viracita-stotram । madhum iva saṃbhṛta-karuṇaṃ vidhum iva nāthaṃ kha-sarpaṇaṃ vande ।।
udarasyedam aṇutvaṃ sahaja-gurutvaṃ yadi nedaṃ hṛdayasya । svārthe katham alasatvaṃ katham anusatvaṃ hita-karaṇe matir asya ।। ity unnīya vidhor abhīti-vihasad yat saṃnidhiṃ sādhvagān nūnaṃ nīrajam astu vaḥ śiva-dive tad lokanāthānanam ।। maharṣer yasyendu-dyuti-ghaṭita-mūrter iva sa vaḥ klamaṃ bhindyād dadyāt praśama-sukha-pīyūṣa-laharīm ।।
।। iti lokeśvara-vrajyā ।। ।। niryat-pāda-nakhonmukhāṃśu-visara-srag-danturaḥ smaryatāṃ mañjuśrīḥ sura-mukta-mañjari-śikhā-varṣair ivābhyarcitaḥ ।। trāsa-tyakta-sva-parṇāstṛta-sura-ghṛṇayevālasat-pāda-vṛndas tāraugha-pluṣṭa-bhānur jagad avatu naṭad-bhairavātmā kumāraḥ ।।
nānā-vidhaṃ sura-vadhūbhir itīkṣito vaḥ pāyāc ciraṃ sugata-vaṃśa-dharaḥ kumāraḥ ।। yo vandamānam abhiṣiñcati dharma-rājye jāgartu vo hita-sukhāya sa mañju-vajraḥ ।। mamābhyarṇe dhārṣṭyāc carati punar indīvaram iti krudhevedaṃ prāntāruṇam avatu vo locana-yugam ।। ।।
trīn kālān iva vīkṣituṃ vahati yo visphūrjad-akṣṇāṃ trayaṃ sa traiguṇya-paricchedo vijayate devas triśūlāyudhaḥ ।। vasukalpa-dattasya ।। namronnamra-bhujaṅga-puṅgava-guṇa-vyākṛṣṭa-bāṇāsanakṣiptāstrasya puradruho vijayate saṃdhāna-sīmāśramaḥ ।। murāreḥ ।
yo bimba-pratipūraṇāya vidhṛto niṣpīḍya saṃdaṃśikāyantre śaiva-lalāṭa-locana-śikhā-jvālābhir ābarhyate ।। ity āhur militāḥ parasparam amūr yasmin praśāntiṃ gate kapāntāra-bhaṭī-naṭasya bhavatāt tad vaḥ śriye tāṇḍavam ।। itthaṃ saṃkucad-ambajānukaraṇa-vyājopanītāñjaleḥ śambhor vañcita-pārvatī-kamucitam saṃdhyārcanaṃ pātu vaḥ ।। kopas te mayi niṣphalaḥ priyatame sthāṇau phalaṃ kiṃ bhaved itthaṃ nirvacanīkṛto dayitayā śambhuḥ śivāyās tu vaḥ ।।
naman janmany asminn aham atanur agre apy anatibhāṅ maheśa kṣantavyaṃ tad idam aparādha-dvayam api ।। muñjasya । maināko api gabhīra-nīra-viluṭhan pāṭhīna-pṛṣṭhocchalac chaivālāṅkura-koṭi-koṭara-kuṭī-kuḍyāntare nirvṛtaḥ ।। yasya sphāra-phaṇā-maṇau nilayanāt tiryak-kalaṅkākṛtiḥ śeṣaḥ so apy agamad yad-aṅgada-padaṃ tasmai namaḥ śambhave ।।
vallaṇasya । ujjṛmbhā babhru-netra-dyutim asakṛd-asṛk-tṛṣṇayālokayantyaḥ pāntu tvāṃ nāga-nāla-grathita-śava-śiraḥ-śreṇayo bhairavasya ।। daṃṣṭrācandra-prabhābhiḥ prakaṭita-subṛhattālu-pātāla-mūlaṃ śambhor vaktraṃ suvaktra-tritaya-bhaya-karaṃ hantv adhaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ vaḥ ।। śreyāṃsi vo diśatu tāṇḍavitasya śambhor ambhodharāvali-ghana-dhvanir aṭṭahāsaḥ ।।
saṅghamitrasya । pāyād vo ghana-tāṇḍava-vyatikara-prāg-bhāra-kheda-skhaladbhogīndra-ślatha-piṅgalotkaṭa-jaṭājūṭaṃ śiro dhūrjaṭeḥ ।। gaurī-pādānataḥ śambhur jayatv ekādaśaḥ svayam ।। pāntu tvām akaṭhora-ketaka-śikhā-saṃdigdha-mugdhendavo bhūteśasya bhugaṅga-valli-valaya-sraṅ-naddha-jūṭā jaṭāḥ ।।
sa jayati gāṅga-jalaughaḥ śambhor uttuṅga-mauli-viniviṣṭaḥ । majjati punar unmajjati candra-kalā yatra śapharīva ।। sravan-mandākinyāḥ prati-divasa-siktena payasā kapālenonmuktaḥ sphaṭika-dhavalenāṅkura iva ।। kasyacit ।
avocad yaṃ paśyedty avatu sa śivaḥ sā ca girijā sa ca krīḍā-candro daśana-kiraṇāpūrita-kalaḥ ।। vararuceḥ । trailokya-nagarārambhamūla-stambhāya śambhave ।। kasyacit ।
āliṅgan yo avadhūtas tripura-yuvatibhiḥ sāśru-netrotpalābhiḥ kāmīvārdrāparādhaḥ sa dahatu duritaṃ śāmbhavo vaḥ śarāgniḥ ।। yeṣām ucchalatāṃ javena jhagiti vyūheṣu bhūmībhṛtām uḍḍīneṣu viḍaujasā punar asau dambholir ālokitaḥ ।। majja-prāye aṅga-bhāge jhagiti rati-pater jājvalan projjvala-śrīr aśreyo vyasyatād vastrinayana-nayanopāntavānto hutāśaḥ ।। dhatte atyadbhuta-vismayena dharayā dhūtasya kānta-tviṣo lolat-kuntala-kuṇḍalasya śirasaḥ śobhāṃ sa vo dhūrjaṭiḥ ।।
mṛdur lekhākoṇe raya-vaśa-vilolasya śaśinaḥ punīyād dīrghaṃ svo hara-śirasi gaṅgā-kala-kalaḥ ।। viśvaṃ srakṣyati rakṣati kṣitim apām īśiṣyate śiṣyate nāgau rāgiṣu raṃsyate syati jagan nirvekṣyati dyām iti ।। bhojadevasya । saṃdhyevārdra-mṛṇāla-komala-tanor indoḥ sahasthāyinī pāyād vas taruṇāruṇāṃśu-kapiśā śambhor jaṭā-saṃhatiḥ ।।
saṃtrāsān niḥsarantyāpy avirata-visarad-dakṣiṇārdhānu-bandhād atyaktāyādri-putryā tirpurahara-jagat-kleśa-hantre namas te ।। ātmany ātmānam eva vyapagata-karaṇaṃ paśyatas tattva-dṛṣṭyā śambhor vaḥ pātu śūnya-kṣaṇa-ghaṭita-laya-brahma-lagnaḥ samādhiḥ ।। nyañcadbhūtsarpad-agni-skhalad-akhila-giritvaṅgad-uttāla-maulisphūrjac-candrāṃśu-niryan-nayana-rucira-sajjāhnavī-nirjharaḥ vaḥ ।। mātraivaṃ prahite guhe vighaṭayaty ākṛṣya saṃdhyāñjaliṃ śambhor bhagna-samādhi-ruddha-rabhaso hāsyodgamaḥ pātu vaḥ ।।
yogeśvarasya । gaurīṃ nartayataḥ sva-vaktra-murajenāmbhodhara-dhvāninā śambhor vaḥ sukhayantu lambhita-layacchedāhatās tālikāḥ ।। tasyaiva । ālokya tripurāvarodhana-vadhū-vargasya dhūma-dhvajaṃ hasta-srasta-śarāsano vijayate devo dayārdrekṣaṇaḥ ।।
vṛṣaḥ śāṭhyaṃ kṛtvā vilikhati khurāgreṇa nayanaṃ yadā śambhuś cumbaty acala-duhitur vaktra-kamalam ।। muṇḍālī-kuhara-prasarpad-anilāsphāla-pramukta-dhvaniḥ prāvṛṭ-kāla ivoditaḥ śiva-śiro-meghaḥ śivāyāstu vaḥ ।। gaurī-mukha-tiraskāralajjayeva na vardhate ।। mauli-svīkṛta-jāhnavīka iti ca prāptābhyasūyaṃ haraḥ pārvatyā sabhayaṃ bhujaṅga-valayīty ālokitaḥ pātu vaḥ ।।
phaṇini śikhi-graha-kupite śikhini ca tad-deha-valayitākulite । avatād vo hara-guhayor ubhaya-paritrāṇa-kātaratā ।। daityādhīśāṅganānāṃ jaghana-parisare lākṣika-kṣauma-lakṣmīr aśreyāṃsi kṣiṇotu tripura-hara-śarodgāra-janmānalo vaḥ ।। maṅgalasya ।
saptāmbhonidhi-janma-caṇḍa-laharī-majjan-nabho-maṇḍalatrāsa-trasta-surāṅganā-kalakala-vrīḍā-vilakṣo haraḥ ।। purāriḥ saṃvṛṇvan vigalad-upasaṃvyānam ajine punītād vaḥ smera-kṣiti-dhara-sutāpāṅga-viṣayaḥ ।। yaḥ śaktyā samalaṃkṛto api śaśinaṃ śrī-śailajāṃ svardhunīṃ dhatte kautuka-rāja-nīti-nipuṇaḥ pāyāt sa vaḥ śaṅkaraḥ ।। ।।
avyād vo hata-dundubhi-svana-ghana-dhvānātiriktas tayor anyonya-pracalāsthit-pañjara-raṇat-kaṅkāla-janmā ravaḥ ।। yogeśvarasya । rakṣatu vaḥ stana-yugalaṃ hari-kari-kumbhānukāri giri-guhituḥ । śaṅkara-dṛḍha-kaṇṭha-graha-pīḍana-bhasmāṅga-rāga-vicchuritam ।।
pātāla-pratimalla-galla-vivara-prakṣipta-saptārṇavaṃ vande nandita-nīlakaṇṭha-pariṣad-vyakta-rddhi vaḥ krīḍitam ।। brahmann unnaya dūram ātma-sadanaṃ devasya me nṛtyataḥ śambhoḥ saṃkaṭam etad ity avatu vaḥ protsāraṇā nandinaḥ ।। romāñcaḥ katham eṣa devi bhagavan gaṅgāmbhasāṃ śīkarar itthaṃ bhartari bhāva-gopana-parā gaurī ciraṃ pātu vaḥ ।। kālaḥ kṛttiṃ nibadhnāty upanayati kare kāla-rātriḥ kapālaṃ śambhor nṛtyāvatāre pariṣad iti pṛthag vyāpṛtā vaḥ punātu ।।
ity uktvā nīyamānaḥ sukhayatu vṛṣabhaḥ pārvatī-pāda-mūle paśyann akṣair vilakṣaṃ valita-gala-calat-kambalaṃ tryambakaṃ vaḥ ।। abhinandasya । amba dviguṇa-gambhīre bhāgīrathi namo astu te ।। udyātān apahāya vigraham iha srotaḥ-pratīpān api srotas tīvrataratvarā gamayati drāg brahmalokaṃ janān ।।
premollāsāj jayati madhuraṃ sasmitābhir vadhūbhir gaurī-mātuḥ kim api kim api vyāhṛtaṃ karṇa-mūle ।। pratyutsarpad-vimala-kiraṇair yais tirodhānam indor devyāḥ sthāṇau caraṇa-patite te nakhāḥ pāntu viśvam ।। dakṣasya । kintu prema-stimita-madhura-snigdha-mugdhā na dṛṣṭir dṛṣṭety antaḥkaraṇam asakṛt tāmyati tryambakasya ।।
bhagīrathasya । yasyoddaṇḍita-śuṇḍa-puṣkara-marud-vyākṛṣṭa-sṛṣṭaṃ muhus tārā-cakraṃ udakta-śīkara-pṛṣal-līlām ivābhyasyati ।। gaṇḍoḍḍīnāli-mālā-mukharita-kakubhas tāṇḍave śūla-pāṇer vaināyakyaś ciraṃ vo vadana-vidhutayaḥ pāntu cītkāra-vatyaḥ ।। bhavabhūteḥ ।
jagat tat taj jātaṃ sakala-nara-nārī-mayam iti pratītiṃ kurvāṇo jayati śikhi-bhartur gaja-mukhaḥ ।। bhava-jaladhi-jalāvalamba-yaṣṭir mahiṣa-mahāsura-śaila-vajra-dhārā । hara-hṛdaya-taḍāga-rāja-haṃsī diśatu śivaṃ jagataś ciram ।। śūlāhata-mahiṣāsura-rudhira-cchuritādharāmbarā gaurī ।
puṣpavatīva sa-lajjā hasita-hara-nirīkṣitā jayati ।। unmāda-smita-roṣa-lajjitam asau gauryā kathaṃcic cirād vṛddha-strī-vacanāt priye vinihitaḥ puṣpāñjaliḥ pātu vaḥ ।। bhāsasya । śikhipatir atidurlaḍitaḥ pitror abhilaṣati madhyam adhiśayitum ।
tāv apy eka-śarīrāv iti viṣamāśaś ciraṃ jayati ।। keyaṃ ko ayaṃ kiṃ etad yuvatir atha pumān vastu kiṃ syāt tṛtīyaṃ śambhoḥ saṃvīkṣya rūpād apasarati guhaḥ śaṅkitaḥ pātu yuṣmān ।। sadyaḥ sītkāra-kārī jala-jaḍima-raṇa-hanta-paṅktir guho vaḥ kampī pāyād apāyāj jvalita-śikhi-śikhe cakṣuṣi nyasta-hastaḥ ।। bāṇasya ।
raktāmbhoja-dhiyā ca locana-puṭaṃ lālāṭam udghāṭayan pāyād vaḥ pitur aṅka-bhāk śiśu-jana-krīḍonmukhaḥ ṣaṇ-mukhaḥ ।। balabhadrasya । calad-barha-cchatra-śriyam iva dadhāno atirucirām avighnaṃ herambo jagad-agha-vighātaṃ ghaṭayatu ।। ābhāti yo daśana-śūnya-mukhaika-deśadehārdha-hārita-vadhūka ivaka-dantaḥ ।।
ekaṃ trīṇi navāṣṭa sapta ṣaḍ-ativyastāsta-saṃkhyā-kramā vācaḥ śaktidharasya śaiśava-kalāḥ kurvantu vo maṅgalam ।। antarhāsa-pināki-pāṇi-yugala-sphālollasac-cetasas tan-mūrdhekṣaṇa-tarpitasya hasitaṃ pāyāt kumārasya vaḥ ।। ity antaḥparibhāvayan bhagavato dīrghaṃ dhiyaḥ kauśalaṃ kūṣmāṇḍo dhṛti-saṃbhṛtām anudinaṃ puṣṇāti tunda-śriyam ।। ity evaṃ barhināthe kathayati sahasā bhartṛ-bhikṣā vibhūṣā vaiguṇyodvega-janmā jagad avatu ciraṃ hāravo bhṛṅgirīṭeḥ ।।
ity ādau paricintitaṃ pratimuhus tad-bhṛṅgi-kūṣmāṇḍayor anyonya-pratikūlam īśa-śivayoḥ pāṇigrahe pātu vaḥ ।। tvāṃ pātu mañjarita-pallava-karṇapūralobha-bhramad-bhramara-vibhrama-bhṛt-kaṭākṣaḥ ।। gaurīṃ hasta-yugena ṣaṇ-mukha-vaco roddhuṃ nirīkṣyākṣamāṃ vailakṣyāc caturāsya-niṣphala-parāvṛttiś ciraṃ pātu vaḥ ।। bhartur bhūta-gaṇāya gotra-jaratī-nirdiṣṭa-mantrākṣarā rakṣatv adri-sutā vivāha-samaye prītā ca bhītā ca vaḥ ।।
rājaśekharasya । ity anyonya-viruddha-ceṣṭitam idaṃ paśyan nija-svāmino bhṛṅgī sāndra-śirāvanaddha-paruṣaṃ dhatte asthi-śeṣaṃ vapuḥ ।। ।। iti śiva-gaṇa-vrajyā ।। ।।
krīḍā-kroḍa-tanor navendu-viśade daṃṣṭrāṅkure yasya bhūr bhāti sma pralayābdhi-palvala-talotkhātaika-mustākṛtiḥ ।। vākpatirājasya । yat-saṃskāra-kalānuvartana-vaśād velā-chalenāmbhasāṃ yātāyātam ayantritaṃ jala-nidher nādyāpi viśrāmyati ।। yābhyām ardha-vibodha-mugdha-madhura-śrīr ardha-nidrāyito nābhī-palvala-puṇḍarīka-mukulaḥ kamboḥ sapatnī-kṛtaḥ ।।
kim adhikaraṇā kīdṛk kasya vyavasthitir ity asāvudaram aviśad draṣṭuṃ tasmai jagan-nidhaye namaḥ ।। murārer etau । devi tvaṃ parihāsa-keli-kalahe anantā tvam evety asau smero vallava-sundarīm avanamac chauriḥ śriyaḥ vaḥ kriyāt ।। vākpatirājasya ।
mugdhe ahaṃ madhusūdano vraja latāṃ tām eva puṣpāsavām itthaṃ nirvacanīkṛto dayitayā hrīṇo hariḥ pātu vaḥ ।। śubhaṅkarasya । mlāyantyā vana-mālayā parigataḥ śrānto api ramyākṛtir gopa-strī-nayanotsavo vitaratu śreyāṃsi vaḥ keśavaḥ ।। kasyacit ।।
niryāto vadanena kukṣi-vasateḥ patyus talād arṇasāṃ śaṅkho apatya-paramparāvṛta iva śreyāṃsi puṇātu vaḥ ।। sa jayaty ādi-varāho daṃṣṭrāniṣpiṣṭa-kula-giri-kaseruḥ । yasya puraḥ sura-kariṇaḥ sāṅkura-māṣopamā jātāḥ ।। yair vyāvṛtya patadbhir aurva-śikhinas tejo-jaṭālaṃ vapuḥ pānādhmāna-vaśād arocaka-rujaś cakre cirasyāspadam ।।
dvijasya śamino mama tribhuvanaṃ tad ity āśayo harer jayati nihnutaḥ prakaṭitaś ca vakroktibhiḥ ।। ity ākūta-juṣaḥ śriyaṃ jala-nidher ardhotthitāṃ paśyato vācontaḥ-sphuritā bahir vikṛtibhir vyaktā hareḥ pātu vaḥ ।। punātu bhavato harer amara-vairi-nāthorasi kvaṇatkaraja-pañjara-krakaca-kāṣa-janmānalaḥ ।। vākpater etau ।
nakṣatra-karbura-viyat-pratirodhi-nindadunnidra-kairava-taḍāgam uro murāreḥ ।। sa tu vinihita-grīvākāṇḍaḥ kaṭāha-puṭāntare svapiti bhagavān kūrmo nidrābharālasa-locanaḥ ।। lāvaṇyasya mahā-nidhī rasikatāṃ lakṣmī-dṛśos tanvatī yuṣmākaṃ kurutāṃ bhavārti-śamanaṃ netre tanur vā hareḥ ।। yasminn uddharati śrutīḥ pṛthutarād oṅkāra-sāra-dhvaner madhye-sindhu viyan-mayo jala-mayaḥ stambhas tv abhūd ambare ।।
gātrāpavṛtti-bhara-kharvita-śeṣam avyād avyāhataṃ murajitaḥ kṛtaka-prasuptam ।। na dṛṣṭo bhāṇḍīre taṭa-bhuvi na govardhana-girer na kālindyāḥ kūle na ca nicula-kuñje muraripuḥ ।। vyaktaḥ stambhān naraharir abhūd dānavaṃ dārayiṣyann ity uktasya smitam udayate devakī-nandanasya ।। śatānandasya ।
pātrāvāpti-samutsukena balinā sānandam ālokitaṃ pāyād vaḥ krama-vardhamāna-mahimāścaryaṃ murārer vapuḥ ।। bhūyas tat-kāla-kānti-dviguṇita-surata-prītinā śauriṇā vaḥ śayyām ālambya nītaṃ vapur alasa-lasad-bāhu lakṣmyāḥ punātu ।। itthaṃ yad-vadana-stana-dvaya-valad-romāvalīṣu bhramaḥ kṣīrābdher mathane abhavad-diviṣadāṃ lakṣmīr asāv astu vaḥ ।। kasyacit ।।
sisīdhu mu-mu-muñca me pa-pa-pa-pāna-pātre sthitaḥ mada-skhalitam ālapan hala-dharaḥ śriyaḥ vaḥ kriyāt ।। puruṣottama-devasya । cāpaṃ cāpaṃ na khaḍgaṃ tvaritataram aho karkaśatvaṃ nakhānām itthaṃ daityādhirājaṃ nija-nakha-kuliśair jaghnivān yas sa vo avyāt ।। śrī-vyāsa-pādānām ।
darpa-sphūrjan-mahokṣa-dvaya-samara-rasābaddha-dīrghānurāgaḥ krīḍā-gopāla-mūrtir muraripur avatād ātta-gorakṣa-līlaḥ ।। śrī-sonnokasya । vicintya yeṣāṃ caritaṃ surārayaḥ priyā-nakhebhyo api rateṣu bibhyati ।। itthaṃ vyāhṛta-pūrva-janma-viraho yo rādhayā vīkṣitaḥ serṣyaṃ śaṅkitayā sa vaḥ sukhayatu svapnāyamāno hariḥ ।।
śubhāṅkasya ।; skmsauka pvpadyā ) ye ca dhyānānubandha-cchala-mukula-dṛśā vedhasā naiva dṛṣṭās te lakṣmīṃ narmayanto nidhuvana-vidhayaḥ pāntu vo mādhavasya ।। nāgāṅgaṃ moktum icchoḥ śayanaṃ uru-phaṇā-cakravālopadhānaṃ nidrā-cchedābhitāmrā ciram avatu harer dṛṣṭir ākekarā vaḥ ।। prāptāḥ pātāla-paṅke na luṭhanaratayaḥ potramātropayukte yenoddhāre dharitryāḥ sa jayati vibhutā-vighniteccho varāhaḥ ।।
vākpatirājasya । tvaṅgan-niṣṭhura-pṛṣṭha-roma-khacita-brahmāṇḍa-bhāṇḍa-sthite yasyotsphāla-kutūhalena katham apy aṅgeṣu jīrṇāyitam ।। raghunandasya । ye rādhā-smṛti-sākṣiṇaḥ kamalayā sāsūyam ākarṇitā gāḍhāntar-davathoḥ pratapta-saralāḥ śvāsā hareḥ pāntu vaḥ ।।
itthaṃ nābhi-vinirgatena sa-śiraḥ-kampādbhutaṃ vedhasā yasyāntaś ca bahiś ca dṛṣṭam akhilaṃ trailokyam avyāt sa vaḥ ।। vākpati-rājasya । ity uktvā phaṇa-bhṛt phaṇāmaṇi-gatāṃ svām eva matvā tanuṃ nidrā-ccheda-karaṃ harer avatu vo lakṣmyā vilakṣa-smitam ।। ity anya-vyapadeśa-gupta-hṛdayaḥ kurvan viviktaṃ vrajaṃ devaḥ kāraṇa-nanda-sūnur aśivaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ sa muṣṇātu vaḥ ।।
bhītānandita-vismitena viṣamaṃ nandena cālokitaḥ pāyād vaḥ kara-padma-susthita-mahā-śailaḥ salīlo hariḥ ।। sohnokasya । vyāvalgad-valavad dhiraṇyakaśipu-kroḍa-sthalī-pāṭanaspaṣṭa-prasphuṭad-asthi-pañjara-rava-krūrā nakhāḥ pāntu vaḥ ।। dor-daṇḍo asau jayati jayinaḥ śārṅgiṇo mandarādrigrāva-śreṇinikaṣamasṛṇa-kṣuṇṇakeyūra-patraḥ ।।
bhagīrathasya । harer apara-keśari-kṣubhita-cetasaḥ pātu vaḥ saroṣa-lalitādhara-bhrukuṭi-bhaṅga-bhīmaṃ mukham ।। ity uktasya yaśodayā murāripor avyāj jaganti sphuradbimboṣṭha-dvaya-gāḍha-pīḍana-vaśād avyakta-bhāvaṃ smitam ।। yasyodara-sthita-jagat-traya-bīja-kośanirgacchad-aṅkura-śikheva vibhāti daṃṣṭrā ।।
dvīpāḥ patrāṇi meghā madhupakulam abhūt tārakā-garbha-dhūlir yasyaitan-nābhi-padmaṃ bhuvanam iti sa vaḥ śarma devo dadhātu ।। halāyudhasya । asita-sicaya-prānta-bhrāntyā muhur muhur utkṣipan jayati janita-vrīḍā-namra-priyā-hasito hariḥ ।। iti viṣṇu-vrajyā ।।
।। so avyād uttapta-kārtasvara-sarala-śara-spardhibhir dhāma-daṇḍair uddaṇḍaiḥ prāpayan vaḥ pracuratama-tamaḥ-stomam astaṃ samastam ।। śuka-tuṇḍa-cchavi savituś caṇḍa-rucaḥ puṇḍarīka-vana-bandhoḥ । maṇḍalam uditaṃ vande kuṇḍalam ākhaṇḍalāśāyāḥ ।।
vidyāyāḥ ।। saṃsāra-sāgara-samutkramiyogisārthaprasthāna-pūrṇa-kalasāya namaḥ savitre ।। varāha-mihirasya ।। arkālokaḥ kriyād vo mudaṃ udaya-śiraś cakravālālavālād udyad-bāla-pravāla-pratima-rucir ahaḥ-pādapa-prāk-pravālaḥ ।।
mayūrasya । ।। iti sūrya-vrajyā ।। ।। apy ete sahakāra-saurabha-muco vācālitāḥ kokilair āyānti priya-viprayukta-yuvatī-marma-cchido vāsarāḥ ।।
saṅgha-śrīyaḥ । paśyaite taravo api sundari jarat-patra-vyayānantarodbhinna-pāṭala-koṭi-saṃpuṭa-dala-prādurbhavat-kuḍmalāḥ ।। malaya-mahī-dhara-pavanaḥ kala-kaṇṭha-kala-dhvanir nikuñja-latāḥ । utkalikā utkalikāś cetasi janayanti lokasya ।।
āmṛṣṭo muhur īkṣito muhur abhighrāto muhur loṭhitaḥ pratyaṅgaṃ ca muhuḥ kṛto mṛgadṛśā kiṃ kiṃ na cūtāṅkuraḥ ।। kvāpi kvāpi madākulākulatayā kāntāparādha-grahagranthi-ccheda-samudyataṃ ca hṛdayaṃ dolāyate subhruvām ।। eteṣām api paśya kiṃśukataroḥ patrair abhinna-tviṣāṃ puṣpa-bhrāntibhir āpatanti sahasā cañcūṣu bhṛṅgāṅganāḥ ।। rājaśekharasya ।
yāḥ kṛcchrād abhilaṅghya lubdhaka-bhayāt tair eva reṇūtkarair dhārā-vāhibhir asti lupta-padavī-niḥśaṅkam eṇī-kulam ।। dalati kalikā cautī nāsmin tathā mṛga-cakṣuṣāṃ atha ca hṛdaye māna-granthiḥ svayaṃ śithilāyate ।। ity āśokī jagati sakale vallarī cīrikeva prāptārambhe kusuma-samaye kāla-devena dattā ।। candraṃ sundarayanti mukta-tuhina-prāvārayā jyotsnayā vardhante ca vivardhayanti ca muhus te amī smaraṃ vāsarāḥ ।।
śiñjal-lola-bhramara-valayaḥ kānanālī-vadhūnāṃ sadyaḥ kunda-smita-bṛhatikāḥ pūrṇa-pātrī-karoti ।। prārabdhe timire vasanta-samaya-kṣoṇīpater bhrāmyataḥ prasnigdhā parito dhṛteva kalikā-dīpāvaliś campakaiḥ ।। atha ca savituḥ śītollāsaṃ lunanti marīcayo na ca jaṭharatām ālambante klamodaya-dāyinīm ।। bhṛṅgā-laṅghita-koṭi kiṃśukam idaṃ kiṃcid vivṛntāyate māñjiṣṭhair mukulaiś ca pāṭalitaror anyaiva kācil lipiḥ ।।
rājaśekharasya । kiṃ ca trīṇi jaganti jiṣṇu-divasair dvitrair manojanmano devasyāpi cirojjhitaṃ yadi bhaved abhyāsa-vaśyaṃ dhanuḥ ।। kiṃ ca svāśraya-saṃbhṛta-prathimasu cchāyātapāṅgeṣv ayaṃ lokaḥ stoka-raso adya na kvacid api svacchandam ānandati ।। gambhīra-krama-pañcamonmada-pika-dhvānocchalad-gītayaḥ pratyujjīvita-manmathotsava iva krīḍanty amū bhūruhaḥ ।।
prāg eva jaitram astraṃ sahakāra-latā smarasya cāpabhṛtaḥ । kiṃ punar analpa-nipatita-madhukara-viṣa-kalka-lepena ।। eṣo ahaṃ muditāli-kokila-kulaṃ kurvan vanaṃ prāptavān yuṣmābhiḥ priya-kāminī-parigataiḥ sthātavyam asmād iti ।। yeṣām akṣi-nibhena bhānti bhagavad-bhūteśa-netrānalajvālā-jāla-karāli-tāsamaśarāṅgāra-sphuliṅgā iva ।।
kiṃśuka-kalikāntar-gata-candra-kalā-sphardhi keśaraṃ bhāti । rakta-nicolaka-pihitaṃ dhanur iva jatu-mudritaṃ vitanoḥ ।। kiṃ cānyat kusumāyudho adya bhagavān dhatte sa-garvaṃ dhanur jyām unmārṣṭi ca pañcabhiś ca viśikhair jetuṃ jagad vāñchati ।। tenāliṅgita-mātra eva vidhivat prādur-bhavan nirbharakrīḍā-kūta-kaṣāyitena manasā loko ayam unmādyate ।।
kiṃ cāṣāḍha-girer anaṅga-vijaya-prastāvanā-paṇḍitaḥ svairaṃ sarpati bāla-candana-latā-līlā-sakho mārutaḥ ।। saṃtāpārthaṃ katham itarathā pāntha-sīmantinīnāṃ puṣpa-vyājād visṛjati śikhā-śreṇim udgāḍha-śoṇām ।। sarvāṅgīṇo bakula-rajasā piñjareṇoparāgaḥ straiṇo yūnāṃ bhavatu rataye veśa-sarvābhisāraḥ ।। sīmantinyaḥ kusuma-dhanuṣā baddha-sakhyasya māsaḥ snigdha-smerair mukham adhiguṇaṃ dṛṣṭipātaiḥ pibanti ।।
śikī-mukhair adya manojña-pakṣair viṣopalepād iva kajjalābhaiḥ । nitānta-pūrṇā mucakundakoṣā vibhānti tūṇā iva manmathasya ।। snehaṃ sravanti taravaḥ pañcāpi kṣipati mārgaṇān madanaḥ । parimukta-kaṇṭha-rodhaḥ para-puṣṭaḥ kṣarati mādhuryam ।।
saṃkucitā iva pūrvaṃ durvāra-tuṣāra-janita-jaḍi-mānaḥ । saṃpraty uparamati hime kramaśo divasāḥ prasāra-juṣaḥ ।। duḥśliṣṭa-durlakṣya-palāśa-saṃdhīny āpāṭalāgrāṇi harinti mūle । kuśeśayānāṃ śukaśāvabhāṃsi prādurbabhūvur navakuḍmalāni ।।
parimalita-haridrān saṃprati drāviḍīnāṃ nava-nakha-pada-tiktān ātapaḥ svedabindūn ।। eko loke kathayati narasyeṣṭa-jāte nisargaṃ nāryāḥ puṃsi sthitim anuguṇāṃ śaṃsati spaṣṭam anyā ।। tataḥ strīṇāṃ hanta kṣamam adhara-kāntiṃ kalayituṃ samantān niryāti sphuṭa-subhaga-rāgaṃ kisalayam ।। re saṃpraty apavitram atra pathikāḥ sārambham ujjṛmbhate cūto dūta ivāntakasya kalikā-jāla-sphurat-pallavaḥ ।।
ito asty eṣa śrīmān aviralam idānīṃ mukulitaḥ prayacchaty unmādān ahaha sahakāra-druma-yuvā ।। kasyacit । aṅkurite pallavite korakite vikasite ca sahakare । aṅkuritaḥ pallavitaḥ korakito vikasitaś ca madano asau ।।
ācinvanti kadambakāni madhunaḥ pāṇḍūni mattālayaḥ strīṇāṃ pīna-ghana-staneṣu kaṇavān svedaḥ karoty āspadam ।। sapadi sakhībhir nibhṛtaṃ virahavatīs trātum atra bhajyante । sahakāra-mañjarīṇāṃ śikhodgama-granthayaḥ prathame ।। ।। iti vasanta-vrajyā ।।
।। grīṣma-vrajyā ।। gurvī vallabhatā jaḍair adhigatā doṣākaraḥ sevyate hā kālaḥ kim ayaṃ kalir na hi na hi prāptaḥ sa gharmāgamaḥ ।। nidāghārka-proṣa-glapita-mahimānaṃ mṛga-dṛśāṃ pariṣvaṅgo anaṅgaṃ punar api śanair aṅkurayati ।।
maṅgalārjunasya । pravṛddha-tāpo divaso atimātram atyartham eva kṣaṇadā ca tanvī । ubhau virodha-kriyayā vibhinnau jāyāpatī sānuśayāv iva staḥ ।। śuṣyac-chrotasi tapta-bhūmi-rajasi jvālāyamānāmbhasi jyeṣṭhe māsi kharārka-tejasi kathaṃ pāntha vrajan jīvasi ।।
idānīṃ nīhāra-stimita-pavana-prīti-janitāṃ niśā-śeṣo nidrāṃ nudati paṭa-dhūmyāṭa-mukharaḥ ।। vāyuḥ sañcāriṇa iva likhaty ānane dig-vadhūnāṃ dhūmodgārair aguru-pavanaiḥ sāntarān patra-bhaṅgān ।। autsukyaṃ janayanti pāntha-pariṣad-gharmāmbu-bindūtkaravyākṣepa-kṣama-manda-manda-maruto mārga-sthalī-pādapāḥ ।। jaṅghā-kuñcana-labdha-nīḍa-niviḍāvaṣṭambha-kaṣṭojjhitakṣepīyaḥ-pavanābhighāta-rabhasotkṣepair ahaḥ pakṣibhiḥ ।।
tṛṣṇārtaḥ śuka-śāvako api sutanoḥ pīna-stanāsaṅginīṃ muktāhāra-latāṃ tad-aṅka-vasatis toyāśayā pāsyati ।। amī mandārāṇāṃ dava-dahana-saṃdehita-dhiyo na ḍaukante pātuḥ jhaṭiti makarandaṃ madhulihaḥ ।। muhūrtaṃ viśrāntaṃ sarasa-kadalī-kānana-taṭe priyā-kaṇṭhāśleṣe niviśati padaṃ śaityam adhunā ।। pātho-bindubhir akṣi-sandhiṣu śanaiḥ saṃsicyamānaḥ sukhaṃ magno vāriṇi dūra-niḥsahatayā nidrāyate sairibhaḥ ।।
uttāmyat-tālavaś ca pratapati taraṇāvāṃśavīṃ tāpa-tandrīṃ adri-droṇī-kuṭīre kuhariṇi hariṇārātayo yāpayanti ।। dṛṣṭir dhāvati dhātakīvanam asṛktarṣeṇa tārakṣavī kaṇṭhād bibhrati viṣkirāḥ śaraśamī-nīḍeṣu nāḍindhamān ।। subhaga-salilāvagāhāḥ pāṭali-saṃsarga-surabhi-vana-vātāḥ । pracchāya-sulabha-nidrā divasāḥ pariṇāma-ramaṇīyāḥ ।।
ādhārāḥ pluta-bāla-śaivala-dala-cchedāvakīrṇormayaḥ pīyante hala-mukta-magna-mahiṣa-prakṣobha-paryāvilāḥ ।। vahnir nīḍi-kiliñja-sañcaya-samutsiktaś caran kānane prasnigdhān iha viṣkirāṇḍakalalān ājyāśayā lumpati ।। kliṣṭa-krauñcam adhārtarāṣṭram apatat-koyaṣṭi niṣṭīṭibhaṃ sīdat-sāra-sama-prasakta-kuraraṃ kālena jātaṃ saraḥ ।। kāntaṃ karṇāvabhiniviśate komalāgraṃ śirīṣaṃ strīṇām aṅge vibhajati tapas tatra tatrātma-cihnam ।।
śuka-patra-harita-komala-kusuma-śatānāṃ śirīṣa-yaṣṭīnām । talam āśrayati dinātapa-bhayena paripiṇḍitaṃ śaityam ।। bhavanti ca himopamāḥ stana-bhuvo yad eṇī-dṛśāṃ śucer upari saṃsthito rati-pateḥ prasādo guruḥ ।। śucāv eṇākṣīṇāṃ malayaja-rasārdrāś ca tanavo vinā tantraṃ mantraṃ rati-ramaṇa-mṛtyuñjaya-vidhiḥ ।।
api pariṇamayitrī rāja-rambhā-phalānāṃ dina-pariṇati-ramyā vartate grīṣma-lakṣmīḥ ।। kiṃ cottapta-viyat-kapāla-phalake kaṅkāla-śeṣa-śriyaṃ candraṃ marmarayanti parpaṭakara-krūrā raver aṃśavaḥ ।। ।। iti grīṣma-vrajyā ।। ।।
unmīlat-kuṭaja-prahāsiṣu girer ālambya sānūn itaḥ prāg-bhāreṣu śikhaṇḍi-tāṇḍava-vidhau meghair vitānāyyate ।। upari-vighaṭamāna-prauḍha-tāpiñja-nīlaḥ śrayati śikharam adrer nūtanas toya-vāhaḥ ।। udyat-kunda-latānta-ketaka-bhṛtaḥ kacchāḥ saric-chrotasāṃ āvir-gandha-śilīndhra-lodhra-kusuma-smerā vanānāṃ gatiḥ ।। dhārā-sikta-vasundharā-surabhayaḥ prāptās ta ete adhunā gharmāmbho-vigamāgama-vyatikara-śrī-vāhino vāsarāḥ ।।
dhūtvā dhāvati kṛṣṇa-kīṭa-paṭala-śreṇīṃ śikhaṇḍī śiraḥ dūrād eva vanāntare viṣa-dhara-grāsābhilāṣāturaḥ ।। dhārā-klinna-kadamba-saṃbhṛta-sudhāmododvahāḥ proṣitair niḥsaṃpāta-visāri-dardura-ravā nītāḥ kathaṃ rātrayaḥ ।। tīrāṇy adya pipīlikā-samudayāvarjaj-jaṭā-lolupavyāptāny unmada-kukkubhāni saritāṃ kurvanti lolaṃ manaḥ ।। eṣa sphāra-mṛdaṅga-nāda-madhurair ambho-mucām āravaiḥ barha-śreṇi-kṛtātapatra-racano hṛṣṭaḥ śikhī nṛtyati ।।
nidrā-mudrita-locane pratigṛhaṃ mūkāyamāne jane nirdvandvoccarad-ucca-dardura-ravaiḥ kolāhalinyo niśāḥ ।। aṭṭeṣu kāṇḍa-paṭa-vārita-śīkareṣu dhanyāḥ pibanti mukha-tāmarasaṃ vadhūnām ।। kiṃ cānyat kalikormi-medura-mukhī jātā kadamba-cchaviś chidyante kiyatā kṣaṇena śikhināṃ mauna-vrata-granthayaḥ ।। ḍimbhā daṇḍaka-pāṇayaḥ pratidiśaṃ paṅka-cchaṭā-carcitāś cubhrūś cubhrur iti bhramanti rabhasād udyāyi-matsyotsukāḥ ।।
martyāvatīrṇasya viḍojaso ayaṃ nīlāṃśuka-cchatram ivāmbuvāhaḥ ।। etāḥ ketaka-bheda-vāsita-puro-vātāḥ patad-vārayo na pratyemi janasya yad virahiṇo yāsyanti soḍhuṃ niśāḥ ।। utsaṅge kakubho nidhāya rasitair ambhomucāṃ ghorayan manye mudrita-candra-sūrya-nayanaṃ vyomāpi nidrāyate ।। dorbhyām āliṅgyamānā jaladhara-samaye patra-ṣaṇḍe niśāyāṃ dhanyāḥ śṛṇvanti suptāḥ stana-yuga-bharitoraḥ-sthalāḥ kāminīnām ।।
apagata-rajo-vikārā ghana-paṭalākrānta-tārakālokā । lamba-payodhara-bhārā prāvṛd iyaṃ vṛddha-vaniteva ।। uddeśa-sphurad-indra-cāpa-valaya-jvālāpadeśād aho dahyante katham anyathārdha-malināṅgāra-dyutas toyadāḥ ।। meghenopakṛtaṃ yad āśu vihitā tasyāgaso niṣkṛtiḥ svairiṇyāḥ priya-veśma-vartma diśatā vidyud-vilāsair muhuḥ ।।
piṣṭānāṃ prasabhaṃ ghanāghana-ghaṭā-saṃghaṭṭato vidyutāṃ cūrṇābhāḥ paritaḥ patanti taralāḥ khadyotaka-śreṇayaḥ ।। kvāmagnaṃ sthalam asti nāma tad ibhīvoddāma-saudāminīnetronmeṣa-vilokitākhila-bhuvo varṣanti naktaṃ ghanāḥ ।। paśyanto nija-kaṇṭha-kāṇḍa-malināṃ kādambinīm unnatagrīvābhyarṇa-milat-kalāpa-viṭapā nṛtyanti kekā-bhṛtaḥ ।। sphural-loma-śyāma-cchagala-śiśi-karṇa-pratisamacchadāgrābhis tvagbhir valayita-karīrās tala-bhuvaḥ ।।
ete kuñcita-jānavo nava-jale nirvānti gharmāhatā bhūyaḥ pakṣa-puṭābhipāta-rabhasotsarpat-kaṇāḥ patriṇaḥ ।। majjānam api vilimpati nākṛta-puṇyasya varṣati payode । nirgama-keli-samutsuka-śiśi-vāraṇa-gāḍha-parirambhaḥ ।। antar me dayitā-mukhaṃ tava śaśī vṛttiḥ samaivāvayos tat kiṃ mām aniśaṃ sakhe jaladhara tvaṃ dagdhum evodyataḥ ।।
kasyacit । bhuvaḥ kim etā divam utpatanti divo athavā bhū-talam āviśanti । calāḥ sthirā veti vitarkayantyo dhārāḥ karāgrair abalāḥ spṛśanti ।। pānthaḥ sva-śāsana-vilaṅghana-jāta-kopakāmājñayā priyatamām iva nīyate sma ।।
nartiṣyanti tavodaye adya jalada vyālola-puccha-cchadacchatra-cchādita-maulayo diśi diśi krīḍālasāḥ kekinaḥ ।। gāyati hi nīlakaṇṭho nṛtyati gaurī taḍit tarala-tārā । āsphālayati mṛdaṅgaṃ tad-anu ghano ayaṃ mahā-kālaḥ ।। alakeṣu cūrṇa-bhāsaḥ sveda-lavābhān kapola-phalakeṣu ।
nava-ghana-kautukinīnāṃ vārikaṇān paśyati kṛtārthaḥ ।। kāle vāri-dharāṇām apatitayā naiva śakyate sthātum । utkaṇṭhitāsi tarale na hi na hi sakhi picchilaḥ panthāḥ ।। asita-bhujaga-śiśu-veṣṭitam abhinavam ābhāti ketakī-kusumam ।
āyasa-valayākaṅkṛta-viṣāṇam iva dantinaḥ patitam ।। stambeṣu ketakīnāṃ yathottaraṃ vāmanair dalair adya । vidalanti meṣa-tarṇaka-puccha-cchavi-keśarāḥ sūcyaḥ ।। preṅkhad-vidyut-patākāvali-rucira-dhanuḥ-khaṇḍa-khaṭvāṅga-dhārī saṃprāptaḥ proṣita-strī-pratibhaya-janakaḥ kāla-kāpāliko ayam ।।
pūrṇa-śrotasi śānta-cātaka-tṛṣi vyāmugdha-candra-tviṣi prāṇān pāntha kathaṃ dadhāsi nivasann etādṛśi prāvṛṣi ।। kva saṃpraty uṣṇāṃśur gata iti samanveṣaṇa-parās taḍid-dīpālokair diśi diśi carantīva jaladāḥ ।। khadyotonnamitopakaṇṭha-taravaḥ puṣṇanti gambhīratām āsārodakamatta-kīṭa-paṭalī-kvāṇottarā rātrayaḥ ।। spṛṣṭāḥ koṭara-nirgatārdha-tanubhiḥ pātuṃ payodānilaṃ niryad-vaṃśa-karīra-koṭaya iva kṣoṇī-bhṛto bhogibhiḥ ।।
hṛl-lekhaṃ janayanty anūpa-saritāṃ uttuṇḍa-gaṇḍūpadotkīrṇodgīrṇā mṛd-arbuda-sthapuṭita-prāntās taṭī-bhūmayaḥ ।। kulīrair bhrāmyadbhir gaṇayitum iva vyāpṛta-karāḥ manaḥ krīṇantīva prakaṭa-vibhavāḥ palvala-bhuvaḥ ।। vindhyādri-mahā-liṅgaṃ snapayati paryanya-dhārmikaḥ śucibhiḥ । jaladendranīla-gaḍḍūśatojjhitaiḥ saṃprati payobhiḥ ।।
pibati vyoma-kaṭāhe saṃsakta-calat-taḍil-latā-rasanaḥ । megha-mahā-mārjāraḥ saṃprati candrātapa-kṣīram ।। ardhodgatena kadalī mṛdu-tāmra-talena garbha-koṣeṇa । pibati nidāgha-jvaritā ghana-dhārāṃ kara-puṭenaiva ।।
saṃlakṣyate vyoma vaṭa-drumābham ambhodhara-śyāma-dala-prakāśam ।। pāṇḍicchāyaḥ stana-parisaro yūthikā-kaṇṭha-sūtrair ity ākalpaḥ prakṛti-lalito vallabhaḥ sundarīṇām ।। dṛṣṭe svābhāvika-tanu-guṇe durdina-svairiṇīnāṃ dhanyo veṣāntara-viracanaṃ pratyudāste kṛtārthaḥ ।। ahar vā rātrir vā dvayam api vilupta-pravicayaṃ ghanair baddha-vyūhaiḥ kim idam iti ghoraṃ vyavasitam ।।
phullad-dhārā-kadambas tava kavalayitā yāvad ete na dṛṣṭā nirmukta-vyāla-nīla-dyuti-nava-jalada-vyākulā vindhya-pādāḥ ।। yogeśvarasya । antar-vinyasta-vīrut-tṛṇa-maya-puruṣa-trāsa-vighnaṃ kathaṃcit kāpotaṃ kodravāṇāṃ kavalayati kaṇān kṣetra-koṇaika-deśe ।। sa mādhyandātyūhaś cala-vipula-kaṇṭhaḥ prasarati kramodañcat-tāraḥ krama-vaśa-naman manda-madhuraḥ ।।
।। iti prāvṛḍ-vrajyā ।। ।। prasādayantī sa-kalaṅkam induṃ tāpaṃ raver abhyadhikaṃ cakāra ।। dhiṅ māṃ tathāpi galitoru-payodharatvād ity uccakaiḥ śarad iyaṃ vahatīva tāpam ।।
yeṣv abhyāgata-khañjarīṭa-śabalās toyāpasāra-kramastoka-stoka-taraṅgitānta-pulināḥ karṣanti nadyo manaḥ ।। maṅgalyaṃ ca kalaṅka-pallava-sakhaṃ smerānanā śarvarī jyotsnā-tarpaṇa-gauram indu-kalaśaṃ vyomāṅgane nyasyati ।। vidadhati na ced utkaṇṭhārdraṃ śaran maṇi-nūpuradhvanita-madhurottāla-snigdhair manaḥ kvaṇitormibhiḥ ।। niśāntāḥ prīṇanti pramada-kurarodgīta-rabhaso nabhasvad-vyādhūta-sphuṭa-kumuda-gandha-pluta-diśaḥ ।।
sthire yūnāṃ māna-graha-paribhave mūrcchati ghano dvirephācāryāṇāṃ madhu-mada-paṭīyān kalakalaḥ ।। cirāc cillas tiryak-tvaritataram āhāra-nipuṇo nipatyaivākasmāc cala-caraṇa-mūrdhaṃ prapatati ।। harṣāśrūrmi-stimita-nayana-nyasta-sotkaṇṭha-dṛṣṭeḥ kaṃcit kālaṃ naṭati nikaṭe khañjarīṭaḥ priyāyāḥ ।। manovinodasyāmī ।
kūjat-kādambarājī-pihita-parisarāḥ śāradīnāṃ nadīnāṃ tīrāntā mañju-guñjan-mada-kalakuraba-śreṇayaḥ prīṇayanti ।। toyaṃ prasīdati muner iva dharma-cintā kāmī daridra iva śoṣam upaiti paṅkaḥ ।। āpāṇḍu-pīvara-payodharam udvahantī kācid vadhūr virahiṇīva śarad vibhāti ।। citāś citrākārair niśi vikacana-kṣatra-kumudair nabhastaḥ syandante sarita iva dīrghā daśa diśaḥ ।।
grāmānteṣu navīna-sasya-hariteṣūddāma-candrātapasmerāsu kṣaṇadāsu dhena-dhavalī-vargaḥ parikrāmati ।। go-rocanā-harita-babhru bahiḥ palāśam āmodate kumudam ambhasi palvalasya ।। vyakta-vyāghra-padāṅka-paṅkti-nicitonmudrārdra-paṅkodarās saṃtrāsaṃ janayanti kuñja-saritaḥ kācābhahnīlodakāḥ ।। kedārebhyaḥ praṇālaiḥ praviśati śapharī-paṅktir ādhāram ārād acchaḥ kaccheṣu paṅkaḥ sukhayati saritām ātapād ukṣa-pālam ।।
nadyaḥ pratyagra-tīropanati-sarabhasaiḥ khañjanaiḥ sāñjanākṣā haṃsāḥ kaṃsāri-deha-tviṣi gagana-tale śaṅkha-śobhāṃ vahanti ।। te saṃpraty akaṭhora-vāraṇa-vadhūdantāṅkura-spardhino niryātāḥ kamalākareṣu bisinī-kandāgrima-granthayaḥ ।। kapotaiḥ potārthaṃ kṛta-niviḍa-nīḍā viṭapinaḥ śivābhir valmīkāḥ khara-nakhara-khātodara-mṛdaḥ ।। vātodastaiḥ śaśadhara-kalā-komalair indra-tūlair līlottaṃsaṃ racayitum alaṃ kanyakāḥ kautukinyaḥ ।।
yā sīmante maṇibhir aruṇaiḥ sā cchavir bandhu-jīvair veśaḥ śobhāṃ diśati paramām ārtavaḥ śāli-gopyāḥ ।। adyānandaṃ dadhati vicarac-cakravākopacañcugrāsa-trāsa-pracala-śaphara-smera-nīrās taṭinyaḥ ।। nimnāvaśiṣṭa-salilāni mano haranti rodhāṃsi haṃsa-pada-mudrita-kardamāni ।। dūrībhavanti saritāṃ taṭa-kānanāni pūrva-pravāha-mahimānam udāharanti ।।
tṛṇa-rāja-pāka-saurabha-sugandhayaḥ pariṇatāśavo divasāḥ । ādya-kulopanimantraṇa-suhita-dvija-duḥsahoṣmāṇaḥ ।। āḍhyān nivāpalambho niketa-gāmī ca picchilaḥ panthāḥ । dvayam ākulayati cetaḥ skandhāvāra-dvijātīnām ।।
।। iti śarad-vrajyā ।। ।। nidrā-vyājāj jaḍima-vidhurā yatra gāḍhe api mantau vāmāḥ kaṇṭha-graham aśithilaṃ preyasām ādriyante ।। vṛnte karkaśa-kīra-piccha-haribhiḥ sthūlaiḥ phalair bandhurāḥ saṃpraty utsukayanti kasya na manaḥ pūga-drumāṇāṃ chaṭāḥ ।।
kumudvatyāḥ koṣe madhu śiśira-miśraṃ madhuliho lihanti pratyūṣe virasa-virasaṃ manda-rucayaḥ ।। prātaḥ kunda-samṛddhi-darśana-rasa-prīti-prakarṣollasanmālākāra-vadhū-kapola-pulaka-sthairya-kṣamo mārutaḥ ।। prātaḥ pṛṣṭhāvagāḍha-prathama-ravi-rucir grāma-sīmopaśalye śete siddhārtha-puṣpa-cchadana-cita-hima-klinna-pakṣmā mahokṣaḥ ।। kaṭu-madhurāṇy āmodaiḥ parṇair utkīrṇa-patra-bhaṅgāni ।
damanaka-vanāni saṃprati kāṇḍair ekānta-pāṇḍūni ।। pariharati suṣuptaṃ hālika-dvandvam ārāt stana-kalaśa-mahoṣmābaddha-rekhas tuṣāraḥ ।। hastāropita-dātra-rajju-laguḍair vṛddhair avṛddhaiḥ saha tyaktvā śāli-cikartiṣām ita ito dhāvanty amī pāmarāḥ ।। pārśvau kampa-jaḍau pidhāya kaphaṇi-dvandvena romāñcitā prātar no na ca sāyam adya jaratī gehodaraṃ muñcati ।।
bāhu-kṣepāt stana-parisarād asta-līlāṃśukābhiḥ ghoṣa-strībhir divasa-viratau bhāti nirviśyamānaḥ ।। grāmās tuṣāra-bhara-bandhura-gomayāgnidhūmāvalī-valaya-mekhalino haranti ।। mūle harinti kiṃcit pārśve pītāni lohitāny agre । madhura-surabhīṇi saṃpraty agāḍha-pākāni badarāṇi ।।
ity ālokya ciraṃ dṛśā kṛpaṇayā dūrāgatena stutaḥ pānthenaika-palāla-muṣṭi-rucinā garvāyate hālikaḥ ।। ।। nāryaḥ kunda-caturthikā-mahasam ārambhābhiṣeke yathā hūtānaṅgam ulūlu-kākala-ravaiḥ prīṇanti yūnāṃ manaḥ ।। prādurbhāvaṃ tirayati raver adhvagānām idānīṃ sarvāṅgīṇaṃ diśati palitaṃ lomalagnā himānī ।।
rātriṃ sarvāṃ hutavaha-pariṣvaṅga-bhājo api manye jāḍyābaddhān tvarayitum ayaṃ drāṅ na śaknoti pādān ।। vārāṃ pūrṇā iva sacakitā vāra-pārīṇa-dṛṣṭer dūrottānā api śikhariṇāṃ nirjhara-droṇi-mārgāḥ ।। kṣīyante suratāntare api na dṛśāṃ pātrīkṛtāṃ kāmibhiḥ saubhāgyāpagamād ivendu-mahasāṃ lāvaṇya-śūnyāḥ śriyaḥ ।। pratyāsīdati vallabhe jalaruhāṃ kṣāmāyamāṇa-dyutau bāṣpān ujjhati vāri vāri-ruhiṇī-nāśād ivopārjitān ।।
asmākaṃ tu vidīrṇa-daṇḍita-paṭī-pracchāditodghāṭitakroḍa-svīkṛta-jānu-vepathumatāṃ cetaḥ paraṃ sīdati ।। śītārti-vyasanāturaḥ punar ayaṃ dīno janaḥ kūrvavat svāny aṅgāni śarīra eva hi nije nihnotum ākāṅkṣati ।। udañcad-dor-vallī-valita-valayābhir yuvatibhir gṛhīta-protkṣipta-bhramita-masṛṇodīrṇa-musalāḥ ।। vāyur vyasta-śaṇas tuṣāra-kaṇavān abhyeti kampa-pradaḥ pānthaiḥ śuṣka-vivāda-baddha-kalahaiḥ puṇyāgnir āsevyate ।।
pāka-praślatha-patra-koṣa-dalanavyaktāṅkura-granthayo niṣṭhīvanty api hasta-yantra-kalitāḥ puṇḍrekṣa-yaṣṭyo rasam ।। abhinava-vadhū-roṣa-svāduḥ karīṣa-tanūnapād asarala-janāśelṣa-krūras tuṣāra-samīraṇaḥ ।। uddhūmair bīja-koṣoccaṭana-paṭu-ravaiḥ sarṣapa-kṣoda-kūṭaiḥ koṇe koṇe khalānāṃ parisara-sa-kaṭuḥ kīryate ko api gandhaḥ ।। utpākatvād vighaṭita-śamī-koṣa-saṃdarśitāni vyākurvanti sphuṭa-sahacarī-vīrudhaḥ kṛṣṇalānām ।।
manojñā mañjaryo harita-kapiśaiḥ pāṃsu-mukulaiḥ sphuṭanti pratyaṅgaṃ paṭu-parimalāhūta-madhupāḥ ।। puṣpāḍhyāḥ śata-puṣpikāḥ phala-bhṛtaḥ siddhyanti siddhārthakāḥ snigdhāḥ vāstuka-vāstavaḥ stavakita-stambā ca kustumbinī ।। śanaiḥ śoṣārambhe sthapuṭa-nija-viṣkambha-viṣamaṃ vane vītāmodaṃ badaram arasatvaṃ kalayati ।। ।। iti śiśira-vrajyā ।।
।। anena kila nirjitā vayam iti prayāyāḥ karaṃ kareṇa parilālayañ jayati jāta-hāsaḥ smaraḥ ।। nīlapaṭahasya । te dīrghāpāṅga-puṅkhāḥ smita-viṣa-viṣamāḥ pakṣmalāḥ strī-kaṭākṣāḥ pāyāsur vo ativīryās tribhuvana-jayinaḥ pañcabāṇasya bāṇāḥ ।।
iti vitata-vicitrāścarya-saṃkalpa-śilpo jayati manasijanmā janmibhir mānitājñaḥ ।। manovinodasya । cumbanto jagatāṃ manaḥ sumanaso marm-aspṛśaḥ sāyakāḥ dārāḥ prīti-ratī iti kva mahimā kāmasya nālaukikaḥ ।। api kusuma-pṛṣatkair deva-devasya jetā jayati suratalīlā-nāṭikā-sūtra-dhāraḥ ।।
rājaśekharasya । yenāsāv api bhasma-lāñchita-tanur devaḥ kapālī balāt prema-kruddhanagātmajāṅghri-vinati-krīḍā-vrate dīkṣitaḥ ।। sa jayati saṃkalpa-bhavo rati-mukha-śata-patra-cumbana-bhramaraḥ । yasyānurakta-lalanā-nayanānta-vilokitaṃ vasatiḥ ।।
śarīram akṣataṃ kṛtvā bhinatty antargataṃ manaḥ ।। iyāṃ jetuṃ yasya tribhuvanam adehasya vibhavaḥ sa vaḥ kāmaḥ kāmān diśatu dayitāpāṅga-vasatiḥ ।। kasyacit । tribhuvana-jaya-siddhyai yasya śṛṅgāra-mūrter upakaraṇam apūrvaṃ mālyam indur madhūni ।।
ātmā nivedyam itara-vrata-sāra-jetrīṃ vandāmahe makara-ketana deva dīkṣām ।। ।। iti madana-vrajyā ।। ।। idānīm bālāyāḥ kim amṛta-mayaḥ kim madhu-mayaḥ kim ānandaḥ sākṣāt dhvanati madhuraḥ pañcama-layaḥ ।।
vīryamitrasya । tiryag-locana-ceṣṭitāni vacasi cchekokti-saṃkrāntayaḥ strīṇāṃ glāyati śaiśave pratikalaṃ ko apy eṣa keli-kramaḥ ।। yad ādatte dṛśyād akhilam api bhāva-vyatikaraṃ mano-vṛttiṃ draṣṭuḥ prathayati ca dṛśyaṃ prati janam ।। madhye samucchvasita-vṛtti manāg upānte labdhātma-sīma kuca-kuḍmala-yugmam asyāḥ ।।
yauvana-nagarārambhe rāmā-hṛdaya-sthalīṣu kusumeṣoḥ । makara-patākeveyaṃ rājati romāvalī ramyā ।। ucita-sahaja-lajjā-durbalā bālikānāṃ guru-jana-bhaya-bhājāṃ ke api te bhrū-vilāsāḥ ।। saṃketitāṅga-nava-yauvana-nāṭakasya kaśmīraja-cchurita-nūtana-kāṃsya-tālam ।।
viśantyās tāruṇyaṃ ghusṛṇa-ghana-lāvaṇya-payasi prakāmaṃ pronmajjad vapur api ca tasyā vijayate ।। pratyāsīdati yauvane mṛga-dṛśaḥ kiṃ cānyad āvirbhaval lāvaṇyāmṛta-paṅka-lepa-laḍaha-cchāyaṃ vapur vartate ।। āpyāyamāna-jaghana-sthala-pīḍyamānam ardhorukaṃ truṭati putri tava kṣaṇena ।। ity anyo madhuraḥ sa ko api śiśutā-tāruṇyayor antare vartiṣṇor mṛga-cakṣuṣo vijayate dvaividhya-mugdho rasaḥ ।।
dṛśor līlāmudrā sphurati ca na cāpi sthitimatī tad asyās tāruṇyaṃ prathamam avatīrṇaṃ vijayate ।। prauḍhastrīcaritānuvṛttiṣu raso bālyena lajjā manāk stokārohiṇi yauvane mṛgadṛśaḥ ko apy eṣa kelikramaḥ ।। no dhatte gurutāṃ tad apy upacitābhogā nitamba-sthalī tanvyāḥ svīkṛta-manmathaṃ vijayate netraikapeyaṃ vapuḥ ।। tiryag-locana-ceṣṭitāni vacasāṃ chekokti-saṃkrāntayas tasyāḥ sīdati śaiśave pratikalaṃ ko apy eṣa keli-kramaḥ ।।
cetaḥ kandalita-smara-vyatikaraṃ lāvaṇyam aṅgair vṛtaṃ tanvaṅgyās taruṇimni sarpati śanair anyaiva kācid gatiḥ ।। tasminn adya punaḥ śruti-praṇayini pratyaṅgam utkampitaṃ tāpaś cetasi netrayos taralimā kasmād akasmān mama ।। nitambe saṃkrāntāḥ katipaya-kalā gaurava-juṣo vapur muñcad bālyaṃ kim api kamanīyaṃ mṛga-dṛśaḥ ।। kasyacit ।
mukulita-kucaṃ vakṣaś cakṣur manāg-vṛta-vakrima krama-parigalad-bālyaṃ tanvyā vapus tanute śriyam ।। snihyat-tāram athānya-dṛṣṭi-virahe yaḥ saṃmukhaṃ vīkṣito namraḥ smera-mukhī-bhavann iti vayaḥ-sandhi-śriyāliṅgitaḥ ।। kiṃ cāpi sphuṭa-dṛṣṭi-vibhrama-kalā-nirmāṇa-śikṣā-rasaḥ pratyaṅgaṃ smara-keli-mudritam aho bālā vayo-vibhrame ।। dhatte vakṣaḥ kuca-sacivatām advitīyatvam āsyaṃ tad-gātrāṇāṃ guṇa-vinimayaḥ kalpito yauvanena ।।
rājaśekharasya । tad-artham utthāpita-cāru-caityakalpau stanau pāṇḍutarau taruṇyāḥ ।। stanau saṃbibhrāṇāḥ kṣaṇa-vinaya-vaijātya-masṛṇasmaronmeṣāḥ keṣām upari na rasānāṃ yuvatayaḥ ।। noddiṣṭaṃ guruṇā na bandhu-kathitaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ na śāstre kvacid bālāyāḥ svayam eva manmatha-kalā-pāṇḍityam unmīlati ।।
tatrāyaṃ spṛhaṇīya-śītalatara-cchāyāsu suptotthitaḥ saṃmugdho madhu-bāndhavaḥ sa bhagavān adyāpi nidrālasaḥ ।। vīryamitrasya । idānīm etasyāḥ kuvalaya-dṛśaḥ pratyaham ayaṃ nitambasyābhogo nayati maṇi-kāñcīm adhikatām ।। kiṃ cāmugdha-vilola-nīraja-dṛśas tāruṇya-puṇyātither asyāḥ kuṅkuma-paṅka-lepa-naḍaha-cchāyaṃ vapur vartate ।।
vajramuṣṭeḥ । prayāṇaṃ bālyasya pratipadam abhūd vigraha-bharaḥ parispando vācām api ca kucayoḥ sandhir abhavat ।। etasyā yad uras-taṭī-parisare yad bālya-cāpalyayoḥ sthāne yauvana-śilpi-kalpita-citā-caitya-dvayaṃ dṛśyate ।। nitambe ca svairaṃ vilasati vilāsa-vyasanitā mṛgākṣyāḥ pratyaṅgaṃ kṛta-padam ivānaṅga-laḍitam ।।
unmagnaṃ yat sphurati ca manāk kumbhayor dvandvam etat tan manye asyā smara-gaja-yuvā gāhate hṛt-taḍāgam ।। nava-nidhuvana-krīḍārambha-prakampa-vivartinīṃ anubhava-mṛdū-bhūta-trāsāṃ manaḥ smarati priyām ।। gatīnām ārambhaḥ kisalayita-līlā-parimalaḥ spṛśantyās tāruṇyaṃ kim iva na manojñaṃ mṛgadṛśaḥ ।। asti bhayam asti kautukam asti ca mandākṣam asti cotkaṇṭhā ।
bālānāṃ praṇayi-jane bhāvaḥ ko apy eṣa naika-rasaḥ ।। spṛhām antaḥ kānte vahati na samabhyeti nikaṭaṃ yathaiveyaṃ bālā harati ca tathaiveyam adhikam ।। seyaṃ vibhrama-toraṇa-praṇayinā jṛmbhābharottambhitenoccair bāhu-yugena śaṃsati manojanma-praveśotsavam ।। priyāyāṃ balim uddiśya tanoti stana-maṇḍalam ।।
antar visphurati smaro bahir api vrīḍā samunmīlate svairaṃ locana-vakrimā vilasati śrīḥ kācid ujjṛmbhate ।। rahasi kurute vāsoguptau svamadhyakadarthanāṃ api ca kim api vrīḍāṃ krīḍāsakhīm iva manyate ।। tathā manye dhanyaṃ parama-surata-brahma-nirataṃ kuraṅgākṣī dīkṣā-gurum akṛta kañcit sukṛtinam ।। dṛśor līlārambhāḥ sphuṭam apavadante saralatām aho sāraṅgākṣyās taruṇimani gāḍhaḥ paricayaḥ ।।
rājaśekharasya । viloka-bhrū-vallī-calana-laya-lolaṃ ca nayanaṃ kva jātaṃ bālāyāḥ kva ca viṣayam akṣṇor iyam agāt ।। haratitarāṃ jana-hṛdayaṃ kalikopagatā latā ca dayitā ca । yadi punar atanu-śilīmukha-samākulā kiṃ na paryāptam ।।
atigata-sakhī-hastonmāna-kramaṃ divasa-kramair idam anubhavad-vāñchā-pūrti-kṣamarddhi kuca-dvayam ।। stana-taṭam idam uttuṅgaṃ nimno madhyaḥ samunnataṃ jaghanam । iti viṣame hariṇākṣyā vapuṣi nave ka iha na skhalati ।। asyā yaj jaghanaṃ ghanaṃ ca kalayā pratyaṅgam eṇīdṛśaḥ satyaṅkāra iva smaraika-suhṛdā tad yauvanenārpitam ।।
ayi purāri parunmalayānilā vavur amī jagur eva ca kokilāḥ । kalamalotkalitaṃ tu na me manaḥ sakhi babhūva vṛthaiva yathaiṣamaḥ ।। mada-madana-vivṛddhi-spardhayevābalānāṃ kim api vapuṣi līlā-kuḍmalāni sphuṭanti ।। satyā na prakṛtau guraḥ śiśutayā prasthāna-dattārghayā kāpy anyā hariṇī-dṛśaḥ pariṇatiḥ kandarpa-mudrāṅkitā ।।
।। iti vayaḥ-sandhi-vrajyā ।। ।। atyantābhimate api vastuni vidhir yāsāṃ niṣedhātmakas tās trailokya-vilakṣaṇa-prakṛtayo vāmāḥ prasīdantu vaḥ ।। bibhokasya ।
tanvī naktam iyaṃ cakāsti śucinī cīnāṃśuke bibhratī śītāṃśor adhidevateva galitā vyomāgram ārohitaḥ ।। rājaśekharasya । vāma-bhruvāṃ mṛdu ca mañju ca bhāṣitāni nirmāyam āyudham idaṃ makara-dhvajasya ।। tatrobhau madhupau tathopari tayor ekoṣṭamī-candramās tasyāgre paripuñjitena tamasā naktaṃ divaṃ sthīyate ।।
paścād tulya-samunnati-vyatikaraṃ sauvarṇa-kumbha-dvayākāreṇa sphuṭam eva tat-pariṇataṃ kvedaṃ vadāmodbhutam ।। kva candre saundaryaṃ tad-adhara-ruciḥ sātiśayinī kva bālāyās te kva caṭula-kaṭākṣā naya-muṣaḥ ।। tatrāpi kāpi nanu citra-parampareyam ujjṛmbhitaṃ kuvalaya-dvitayaṃ yad atra ।। nija-nayana-pratibimbair ambuni bahuśaḥ pratāritā kāpi ।
nīlotpale api vimṛśati karam arpayituṃ kusumalāvī ।। dharaṇīdharasya । yauvana-śilpi-sukalpita-nūtana-tanu-veśma viśati rati-nāthe । lāvaṇya-pallavāṅgau maṅgala-kalaśau stanāv asyāḥ ।।
asyās trivali-bandhena saiva madhyasya namratā ।। trailokya-labdha-vijayasya manobhavasya saurvarṇa-paṭṭa-likhiteva jaya-praśastiḥ ।। kasyacit । virūpākṣasya jayinīs tāḥ stuve vāma-locanāḥ ।।
rājaśekharasya । yasya pārvaṇa-candreṇa tulyataiva hi lāñchanam ।। dhātā jināsanāmbhojavinimīlana-duḥsthitaḥ ।। lolālakaṃ tarala-vīkṣitam āyatākṣyāḥ sākṣān mukhaṃ yadi bhavān anukartu-kāmaḥ ।।
ānandottaralasya puṣpa-dhanuṣas tat-kāla-nṛtyotsavaprāpti-prodyata-kāṃsya-tāla-yugala-prāyaṃ samālokyate ।। hatau rambhā-stambhau hatam ahaha bandhūka-kusumaṃ hatau hemnaḥ kumbhāv ahaha vihataḥ pārvaṇa-śaśī ।। sura-sumanasaḥ śvāsāmode śaśī ca kapolayor amṛtam adhare tiryag-bhūte viṣaṃ ca vilocane ।। lakṣmīdharasya ।
bhavatu mahimā lāvaṇyānām ayaṃ katham anyathā vigalita-tanur lekhāśeṣaḥ kathaṃ ca niśākaraḥ ।। etat-sādhana utsaheta sa jagaj jetuṃ kathaṃ manmathas tasyāmogham amūr bhavanti nahi ced astraṃ kuraṅgī-dṛśaḥ ।। amara-siṃhasya । gurutāṃ jaghana-stanayoḥ sraṣṭur muṣṭyonnamayya tulitavataḥ ।
magnāṅguli-sandhi-traya-nirgata-lāvaṇya-paṅktilā trivalī ।। adarpaṃ kandarpaṃ jana-nayana-nirmāṇam aphalaṃ jagaj jīrṇāraṇyaṃ katham asi vidhātuṃ vyavasitaḥ ।। ity akṣuṇṇa-manojña-cāṭu-janita-vrīḍaḥ purandhrī-janā dhanyānāṃ bhavaneṣu pañjara-śukair āhāram abhyarthyate ।। kasyacit ।
pratyagrāṇi priya-kara-ruha-krīḍitāny eva mugdhe śobhā-bhāñji stana-kalaśayos tanvi hāro api bhāraḥ ।। tatas tāṃ śreyobhiḥ pariṇatim asau vindati yayā ruciṃ tanvan pīna-stani hṛdi tavāyaṃ vilasati ।। mamāpy eṣā bhrāntiḥ prathamam abhavad bhṛṅga kim u te kṛtaṃ yatnair ebhyo virama viramety añjalir ayam ।। rājaśekharasya ।
iti janita-virodhād bhūta-kopād ivāyaṃ harati tuhina-raśmiḥ paṅkajānāṃ vikāśam ।। tat-kānti-saṃpadam avāpsyata cec cakorāḥ pānotsavaṃ kim akariṣyata candrikāsu ।। sūcyagra-mātra-parikhaṇḍita-vigraheṇa prāptaṃ yataḥ stana-taṭaṃ tava kañcukena ।। unmajjatā yauvana-vāraṇena vāpīva tanvaṅgi taraṅgitāsi ।।
āmodam ulbaṇam akṛtrimam udvahanti śvāsāḥ svabhāva-subhagaṃ katham anyathaite ।। stana-yuga-bhara-bhaṅgāśaṅkiteneva dhātrā trivali-valaya-baddhaṃ madhyam ālokayāmaḥ ।। tad evaṃ tanvaṅgyāḥ katham api nitamba-sthalam idaṃ mayā labdhaṃ puṇyair iti raṇati kāñcī-parikaraḥ ।। guṇa-vṛddhir varṇa-lopa-dvandva-nipātopasarga-saṃkīrṇā ।
durghaṭa-paṭavākyārthā vyākaraṇa-prakriyevāsau ।। nayana-cchalena sutanor vadana-jite śaśini kula-vibhau krodhāt । nāsānāla-nibaddhaṃ sphuṭitam ivendīvaraṃ dvedhā ।। rekhā kāpi rada-cchade ca sutanor gātre ca tat kāminīṃ enāṃ varṇayitā smaro yadi sa ced vaidarbhyam abhyasyati ।।
niḥśaṅkam aṅkurita-puṣpita-kānti-kāśe tatrādhunā tuhina-dhāmni mṛgāś caranti ।। kṣobhaṃ yad eti na manāg api tena manye suvyatam eva jala-rāśir ayaṃ payodhiḥ ।। bhujāśliṣṭo harṣād anubhavasi hastāhṛti-kalām aye vīṇā-daṇḍa prakaṭaya phalaṃ kasya tapasaḥ ।। vācaspateḥ ।
imāṃ manye mudrām atanutara-sindūra-subhagāṃ idaṃ muktā-ratnaṃ madana-nṛpater mudritam iva ।। kim aṅge tanvaṅgyāḥ kalayati jagat kāntam adhikaṃ yad etasyāṃ śaśvat paravaśam ivonmattam iva ca ।। bhruvor līlāṃ bālaḥ śiryam alika-paṭṭasya taruṇo mukhendoḥ sarvasvaṃ harati hariṇākṣyāḥ pariṇataḥ ।। vāmadevasya ।
unmajjati dvirada-kumbha-taṭī ca yatra yatrāpare kadala-kāṇḍa-mṛṇāla-daṇḍāḥ ।। ayaṃ kaṇṭhe bāhuḥ śiśira-masṛṇo mauktika-rasaḥ kim asyā na preyo yadi param asahyas tu virahaḥ ।। bhavabhūteḥ । tavākṣṇo apabhraṣṭaṃ smara-jara-śarendīvara-dalaṃ mukhaṃ tad yasyenduḥ prathama-likhana-proñchana-padam ।।
mithaḥ sīmā-mātre yad idam anayor maṇḍalavator rapi spardhā yuddhaṃ tad iha hi namasyaḥ kaṭinimā ।। bhāvaka-devyāḥ । līlā-nirjhariṇī manoja-nṛpater lāvaṇya-sindhor iyaṃ velā kasya mṛgekṣaṇā sukṛtinaḥ saundarya-sīmā-sthalī ।। iti nava-hariṇākṣyāḥ kāntim ālokayanto jagad akhilam asāraṃ bhāram ālocayāmaḥ ।।
aho mohaḥ ko ayaṃ śatamakha-mukhānāṃ sumanasāṃ yad asyārthe atyarthaṃ jaladhi-mathanāyāsam aviśan ।। tasyāḥ satyam anaṅga-vibhrama-bhuvaḥ pratyaṅgam āsaṅginī bhrāntir viśva-sṛjo api yatra kiyatī tatrāsmad-āder matiḥ ।। uttuṅga-saṃgata-payodhara-padma-yugmaṃ nābher adhaḥ kathayatīva mahā-nidhānam ।। antaḥ kiṃ ca sudhā-sapatnam aniśaṃ jāgarti yad-rāgiṇāṃ visrambhāspadam adbhutaṃ kim api tat-kānteti tattvāntaram ।।
kasyacit । hārāya guṇine sthānaṃ na dattam iti lajjayā ।। prāpra-śravaṇayor akṣṇor na muktaṃ jana-māraṇam ।। tayor antara-saṃlagnāṃ dṛṣṭim utpāṭayann iva ।।
taruṇi yena tavādhara-pāṭalaṃ daśati bimba-phalaṃ śuka-śāvakaḥ ।। dharma-kīrteḥ । nāpy āmīlita-locanasya racanād rūpaṃ bhaved īdṛśaṃ tasmāt sarvam akartṛkaṃ jagad idaṃ śreyo mataṃ saugatam ।। roṣād vaśīkaraṇam astram upādade yat sā subhruvāṃ vijayate jagati pratiṣṭhā ।।
manovinodasya । ātma-drohiṇi rohiṇī-parivṛḍhe paryaṅka-paṅkeruhaḥ saṃkocād atiduḥsthitasya na vidhes tac chilpam unmīlitam ।। ūnasya nūnaṃ paripūraṇāya tārāḥ sphuranti pratimāna-khaṇḍāḥ ।। ekāgrāṃ yad dadhati bhagavaty uṣṇa-bhānau ca bhaktiṃ tat prāpus te sutanu vadanaupamyam ambhoruhāṇi ।।
ity ākṛṣṭa-śilīmukhena racanāṃ kṛtvā tad atyadbhutaṃ yat-padmena jigīṣuṇāpi na jitaṃ mugdhe tvadīyaṃ mukham ।। kasyacit । tasyāḥ sakhe niyatam indu-sudhāmṛṇālajyotsnādi kāraṇam abhūn madanaś ca vedhāḥ ।। sudhā-baddha-grāsair upavana-cakorair anusṛtāṃ kiran jyotsnām acchāṃ nava-lavala-pāka-praṇayinīm ।।
yenākriyanta sutanoḥ sa kathaṃ vidhātā kiṃ candrikāṃ kvacid aśīta-ruciḥ prasūte ।। ayaṃ jṛmbhārambha-sphaṭika-śuci-dantāṃśu-nicayo mukhendur gaurāṅgyā galita-mṛga-lakṣmā vijayate ।। kiṃ cāntar nihitānurāga-madhurām avyakta-varṇa-kramāṃ mugdhe vācam udīrayāstu jagato vīṇāsu bherī-bhramaḥ ।। bherī-bhramarasya ।
līyante kabarīṣu bāndhava-jana-vyāmoha-jāta-spṛhā durvārā madhupāḥ kiyanti taruṇi sthānāni rakṣiṣyasi ।। pāṇineḥ । yat tu projjhita-lāñchane hima-rucāv unnidram indīvaraṃ saṃsaktaṃ ca mitho rathāṅga-mithunaṃ tat kutra dṛṣṭaṃ punaḥ ।। tvad-vācāṃ svara-mātrikāṃ mada-kalaḥ puṃskokilo ghoṣayaty abhyāsasya kim asty agocaram iti pratyāśayā mohitaḥ ।।
eṣāpi sva-guṇānurūpa-ramaṇābhāvād varākī hatā ko arthaś cetasi vedhasā vinihitas tanvyās tanuṃ tanvatā ।। kāmasya ghora-hara-hūṅkṛti-dagdha-mūrteḥ saṃjīvanauṣadhir iyaṃ vihitā vidhātrā ।। vedābhyāsa-jaḍaḥ kathaṃ nu viṣaya-vyāvṛtta-kautūhalo nirmātuṃ prabhaven manoharam idaṃ rūpaṃ purāṇo muniḥ ।। dhik kandarpa-dhanur-bhruvau ca yadi te kiṃ vā bahu brūmahe yat satyaṃ punarukta-vastu-vimukhaḥ sarga-kramo vedhasaḥ ।।
rājaśekharasya । itīva śīta-dyutir ātma-bimbaṃ nirmāya nirmāya punar bhinatti ।। avanamra-mukhi vyaktam etenaivāsya lāghavam ।। kṛśaḥ śambhu-jaṭājūṭataṭinī-taṭam āśritaḥ ।।
kasyacit । anyonya-maṇḍalākrāntau naṣṭa-sandhī nṛpāv iva ।। yasyām agre karaṃ dattvā yojyate nakha-lāṅgalam ।। yeṣām upetya sotkampā rājāno api kara-pradāḥ ।।
śaṅke paṅkaja-saṃbhavas tu bhagavān adyāpi bālyāvadhiḥ sarvāṅga-praṇayāṃ priyāṃ kalayituṃ dīrghaṃ tapas tapyate ।। ।। iti yuvati-varṇana-vrajyā ।। ।। antar-visphurad-indranīla-maṇiman-muktāvalīm-āṃsalāḥ sa-prema prahitāḥ smara-jvara-muco dvitrāḥ kaṭākṣa-cchaṭāḥ ।।
mugdhe kevalam etad āhita-nakhotkhātāṅkam utpāṃśulaṃ bāhvor mūlam alīka-mukta-kabarī-bandha-cchalād darśitam ।। tataḥ kiṃcit phullaṃ tad anu ghana-bāṣpāmbu-laharīparikṣāmaṃ cakṣuḥ patatu mayi tasyā mṛga-dṛśaḥ ।। vīryamitrasya । nīlābja-vyatimiśra-ketaka-dala-drāghīyasīnāṃ srajāṃ sodaryāḥ suhṛdaḥ smarasya sudhayā digdhāḥ kaṭākṣa-cchaṭāḥ ।।
niryāntīṣu sakhīṣu vāsa-bhavanān nirgantum evehate jātā vāmatayaiva me adya sutarāṃ prītyai navoḍhā priyā ।। śrī-harṣa-devasya । hāsya-śrī-lava-lāñchitā ca yad asāv asyāḥ kapola-sthalī lolal-locana-gocaraṃ vrajati sa svargād apūrvo vidhiḥ ।। pradyumnasya ।
virata-carita-tāra-sphāra-netraṃ yad asyāś cakitam iha na dṛṣṭaṃ mūḍha tad vañcito asi ।। viśālaḥ śyāmāyāḥ skhalita-ghana-nīlāṃśuka-vṛtiḥ stanābhogaḥ snihyan-masṛṇa-ghusṛṇālepa-subhagaḥ ।। manovinodasya । lāvaṇyārdre katham itarathā tatra tasyāṅgulīnāṃ āmagnānāṃ trivali-valaya-cchadmanā bhānti mudrāḥ ।।
tan mitraṃ kusumāyudhasya dadhatī bālāndhakārāñcitā tāraikāvali-maṇḍaneyam anaghā śyāmā vadhūr dṛśyatām ।। tat-prema-paṅka-patito na samujjihīte mac-citta-kuñjara-patiḥ parigāhamānaḥ ।। mad-dṛṣṭis tṛṣiteva saṃprati śanair āruhya tuṅgau stanau sākāṅkṣaṃ muhur īkṣate jala-lava-prasyandinī locane ।। iti yadi śatakṛtvas tattvam ālokayāmas tad api na hariṇākṣīṃ vismaraty antarātmā ।।
ramate tac ca tatraiva hatāḥ pāṇininā vayam ।। muktānām apy avastheyaṃ ke vayaṃ smara-kiṅkarāḥ ।। kāntām ayaṃ virahiṇīm anurantu-kāmaḥ kāmāturo japati mantram ivāntarātmā ।। sākrāntā jaghana-sthalena guruṇā gantuṃ na śaktā vayaṃ doṣair anya-janāśritair apaṭavo jātāḥ sma ity adbhutam ।।
hṛdayam aśaraṇaṃ me pakṣma-lākṣyāḥ kaṭākṣair apahṛtam apaviddhaṃ pītam unmūlitaṃ ca ।। digdho amṛtena ca viṣeṇa ca pakṣmalākṣyā gāḍhaṃ nikhāta iva me hṛdaye kaṭākṣaḥ ।। na saṃtāpa-cchedo hima-sarasi vā candramasi vā mano niṣṭhā-śūnyaṃ bhramati ca kim apy ālikhati ca ।। viveka-pradhvaṃsād upacita-mahāmoha-gahano vikāraḥ ko apy antar jaḍayati ca tāpaṃ ca kurute ।।
kvāpi sveda-samuccayaḥ snapayati kvāpi prakamodgamaḥ kvāpy aṅgeṣu tuṣānala-pratisamaḥ kandarpa-darpa-kramaḥ ।। amṛta-siktam ivāṅgam idaṃ yadi bhavati tanvi tavādbhuta-vīkṣitaiḥ । adharam indukarād api śubhrayanty aruṇayanty aruṇād api kiṃ dṛśam ।। etāvad bahu yad babhūva katham apy ekatra manvantare nirmāṇaṃ vapuṣo mamoru-tapasas tasyāś ca vāma-bhruvaḥ ।।
yatas tan-netra-sañcārasūciteṣu pravartate ।। ākṛṣṭaṃ sahajābhijātya-kalanāt premṇā puraḥ preritaṃ cakṣur bhūri kathaṃ kathaṃcid agamat preyāṃsam eṇīdṛśaḥ ।। gacchati puraḥ śarīraṃ dhāvati paścād asaṃsthitaṃ cetaḥ । cīnāṃśukam iva ketoḥ prativātaṃ nīyamānasya ।।
karoti kasya no mugdhe pipāsā-taralaṃ manaḥ ।। kasyacit । aṅge ca pratibhāti mārdavam idaṃ snigdha-svabhāvaś ciraṃ premṇā man-mukha-candram īkṣita eva smereva vaktīti ca ।। anyān mantrayate punar mayi gate maunaṃ samālambate nīto dūram ahaṃ tayā dayitayā sāmānya-lokād api ।।
bahalatara-nakhāgra-kṣoda-vinyasta-mārge śirasi ṭasiti likṣāṃ hanti hūṅkāra-garbham ।। alasayati gātram adhikaṃ bhramayati cetas tanoti saṃtāpam । mohaṃ ca muhuḥ kurute viṣama-viṣaṃ vīkṣitaṃ tasyāḥ ।। vakṣo nidhāya bhuja-pañjara-madhya-vartī dhanyaḥ kṣapāḥ kṣapayati kṣaṇa-labdha-nidraḥ ।।
bhrū-bhaṅga-vibhrama-vilāsa-nirīkṣitāni kopa-prasāda-hasitāni kutaḥ śaśāṅke ।। yāvan na vakra-gatir añjana-nīla-rocir eṇīdṛśāṃ daśati locana-danta-śūkaḥ ।। hṛtaṃ hṛdayam ekeṣām anyeṣāṃ cakṣuṣaḥ phalam ।। kasyacit ।
māyeyaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇikāsv api payaḥ pātuṃ samīhā tava tyaktavye pathi mā kṛthāḥ punar api prema-pramādāspadam ।। avayavāvaraṇaṃ ca yad añcalavyatikareṇa tad-aṅga-samarpaṇam ।। kālidāsasya । hṛdaya-nihitaṃ bhāvākūtaṃ vamadbhir ivekṣaṇaiḥ kathaya sukṛtī ko ayaṃ mugdhe tvayādya vilokyate ।।
racayatobhaya-dharmi tavānanaṃ prakaṭitaṃ vidhinā bahu naipuṇam ।। vinaya-vārita-vṛttir atas tayā na vivṛto madano na ca saṃvṛtaḥ ।। nīlābja-karburita-madhya-vinidra-kundadāmābhirāma-rucibhis taralaiḥ kaṭākṣaiḥ ।। śanaiścarābhyāṃ pādābhyāṃ reje graha-mayīva sā ।।
hṛdaya-nihitaṃ bhāvākūtaṃ vamadbhir ivekṣaṇaiḥ kathaya sukṛtī ko asau mugdhe tvayādya vilokyate ।। vivṛta-vilasad-vāmāpāṅga-stanārdha-kapolayā kuvalaya-dala-srak-saṃdigdha-śriyaḥ prahitā dṛśaḥ ।। parameśvarasya । vaidarbhākṣara-garbhiṇīṃ giram udīryānyāpadeśād śiśuṃ prītyā karṣati cumbati tvarayati śliṣyaty asūyaty api ।।
dattvāṅgaṃ svapiti priyasya rataye vyājena nidrāṃ gatā tanvy-aṅgyā viphalaṃ viceṣṭitam aho bhāvānabhijñe jane ।। kasyacit । dattvā pīlu-śamīkarīra-kavalān svenāñcalenādarādāmṛṣṭaṃ karabhasya kesara-saṭābhārāvalagnaṃ rajaḥ ।। keśaṭasya ।
āsīd vivṛtta-vadanā ca vimocayantī śākhāsu valkalam asaktam api drumāṇām ।। romāñco api nirantaraṃ prakaṭitaḥ prītyā na śaityād apāṃ akṣuṇṇo vidhir adhvagena ghaṭito vīkṣya prapā-pālikām ।। karaṃ vyādhunvatyāḥ pibasi rati-sarvasvam adharaṃ vayaṃ tattvānveṣān madhukara hatās tvaṃ khalu kṛtī ।। mā gā ity uparuddhayā yad api tat sāsūyam uktā sakhī sarvaṃ tat kila mat-parāyaṇam aho kāmaḥ svatāṃ paśyati ।।
bhṛṅgāgra-graha-kṛṣṭa-ketaka-dala-spardhāvatīnāṃ dṛśāṃ dīrghāpāṅga-taraṅgaṇaika-suhṛdām eṣo asmi pātrīkṛtaḥ ।। manāg vapur apāvṛṇu spṛśatu kāñcanaṃ kālikāṃ udañcaya nijānanaṃ bhavatu ca dvi-candraṃ nabhaḥ ।। kiṃ citraṃ yadi tanvaṅgyāḥ stanābhyāṃ nirjitaṃ jagat ।। dadhānāḥ sarvasvaṃ kusuma-dhanuṣo asmān prati sakhe navaṃ netrādvaitaṃ kuvalaya-dṛśaḥ saṃnidadhati ।।
rājaśekharasya । viyati ca racayantaś candrikāṃ dugdha-mugdhāṃ pratinayana-nipātāḥ subhruvo vibhramanti ।। rājaśekharasya । bhāṣante ca yad uktibhiḥ stavakitaṃ vaidagdhya-mudrātmabhisḥ tad devasya rasāyanaṃ rasanidher manye manojanmanaḥ ।।
sthita-mati-ciram uccair agrapādāṅgulībhiḥ kara-kalita-sakhīkaṃ māṃ didṛkṣoḥ smarāmi ।। rājaśekharasya । vahati hṛdaya-coraṃ kuṅkuma-nyāsa-gauraṃ valayitam iva nālaṃ locanendīvarasya ।। kasyacit ।।
svecchāhita-bhramaraka-bhrami-maṇḍalībhir anyaṃ rasaṃ racayatīva ciraṃ nata-bhrūḥ ।। rājaśekharasya । idaṃ tarala-kaṅkaṇāvali-viśeṣa-vācālitaṃ mano harati subhruvaḥ kim api kanduka-krīḍitam ।। tasyaiva ।
kambor viḍambana-karaś ca sa eva kaṇṭhaḥ saiveyam indu-vadanā madanāyudhāya ।। kva vā pārīmeyo bata bakula-dāmnāṃ parimalaḥ kathaṃ svapnaḥ sākṣāt kuvalaya-dṛśaṃ kalpayatu tām ।। [note kva peyaṃ jyotsnāmbho vadata visavallī-saraṇibhir] rājaśekharasya । sakṛd api punar madhyasthaḥ san rasāntara-vijjano vadatu yad ihānyat svādu syāt priyāradana-cchadāt ।।
kasyacit । viṣam upahitaṃ cintāvyājān manasy api kāmināṃ alasa-madhurair līlā-tantrais tayārdha-vilokitaiḥ ।। śvāsa-truṭyad-vacāṃsi drutam itara-karotkṣipta-lolālakāni srasta-srañji pramodaṃ dadhati mṛgadṛśāṃ kanduka-krīḍitāni ।। iti dina-śata-prāpyaṃ deśaṃ priyasya yiyāsato harati gamanaṃ bālālāpaiḥ sabāṣpa-galaj-jalaiḥ ।।
ity udbāṣpa-vadhū-giraḥ pratipadaṃ saṃpūrayanty āntike kāntaḥ prasthiti-kalpitopakaraṇaḥ sakhyā bhṛśaṃ vāritaḥ ।। strī kācid ity abhihite hi mano madīyaṃ tām eva vāma-nayanāṃ viṣayī-karoti ।। ।। ity anurāga-vrajyā ।। ।।
niḥśvāsaiḥ kuca-kumbha-pīṭha-luṭhana-pratyudgamān māṃsalaiḥ śyāmībhūta-kapolam indur adhunā yat tan mukhaṃ spardhate ।। śṛṅgārasya । itthaṃ duḥsaha-dāha-dāyini dhṛta-dveṣāpi puṣpāyudhe mugdhā sā subhage tvayi pratimuhuḥ premādhikaṃ puṣyati ।। tasyaiva ।
dṛśor bāṣpaḥ pāṇau vadanam asavaḥ kaṇṭha-kuhare hṛdi tvaṃ hrīḥ pṛṣṭhe vacasi ca guṇā eva bhavataḥ ।। acala-siṃhasya । prādurbabhūva subhaga tvayi dūrasaṃsthe caṇḍāla-candra-dhavalāsu niśāsu tasyāḥ ।। caṇḍāla-candrasya ।
tasyās tvad-virahe vipakva-lavalī-lāvaṇya-saṃvādinī chāyā kāpi kapolayor anudinaṃ tasyāḥ paraṃ śuṣyati ।। dharmakīrteḥ । kiṃ cānyat kathayāmi rātrim akhilāṃ tvad-vartma-vātāyane hasta-cchatra-niruddha-candra-mahasas tasyāḥ sthitir vartate ।। rājaśekharasya ।
kāmaḥ puṣpa-śaraḥ kileti sumano-vargaṃ lunīte ca yat tat kāṃ sā subhaga tvayā varat-tanur bātūlatāṃ lambhitā ।। tasyaiva । balākarṣa-tryuṭyad-valayaja-kaḍatkāra-ninadair vinidrāyāḥ paścād anavarata-bāṣpāmbu-nivahāḥ ।। yad liptaṃ kuca-candanena sutanor adyāpi candra-cchalāc chvāsoḍḍīna-viśuṣka-pāṇḍu-bisinī-patraṃ divi bhrāmyati ।।
prakaṭayati kṣaṇa-bhaṅgaṃ paśyati sarvaṃ jagad gataṃ śūnyam । ācarati smṛti-bāhyaṃ jātā sā bauddha-buddhir iva ।। mṛṇāla-cīraṃ dadhatī stanābhyāṃ smaropadiṣṭaṃ carati vrataṃ sā ।। kasyacit ।
bhīṣmoṣmabhiḥ smaraṇa-mātra-viṣais taveyam avyāla mārayati kāpi bhujaṅga-bhaṅgiḥ ।। sā bālā balavan-mṛgāṅka-kiraṇair utpāditāntar-jvarā tvat-saṃkalpa-jaḍe tva-aṅka-śayane nidrā-sukhaṃ vāñchati ।। antaḥprajvalitasya kāma-śikhino dāhārjitair bhasmabhiḥ śvāsā-vega-vinirgatair iva tanoḥ pāṇḍutvam unmīlati ।। bāṣpa-vyākulam īkṣitaḥ sapulakaṃ cūtāṅkurair arcito mūrdhnā ca praṇataḥ sakhīṣu madana-vyājena cāpahnutaḥ ।।
vākkūṭasya । janmāntare viraha-duḥkha-vināśa-kāmā puṃskokilābhihiti-mantra-padair juhoti ।। tad alam adhunā nirbandhena prasīda parasparaṃ praṇaya-madhuraḥ sad-bhāvo vāṃ cirāya vivardhatām ।। tad-gātrāṇāṃ kim iva hi bahu brūmahe durbalatvaṃ yeṣām agre pratipad uditā candralekhāpy atanvī ।।
rājaśekharasya । ādau śuṣyati saṃkucaty anu tataś cūrṇatvam āpadyate paścān murmuratāṃ dadhad dahati ca śvāsāvadhūtaḥ śikhī ।। kasyacit । aye kiṃcid vakre tvayi subhaga sarve katham amī samaṃ jātās tasyām ahaha viparīta-prakṛtayaḥ ।।
acala-siṃhasya । kiṃ cānyad-viraha-vyathā-praṇayiṇīṃ saṃprāpya mūrcchāṃ cirāt pratyujjīvati karṇa-mūla-paṭhitais tvan-nāma-mantrākṣaraiḥ ।। kasyacit । gāḍhāv adhaḥ-kṛta-bali-tritayau susaṅga tuṅgau stanāv iti tayos talam ārtam āgāt ।
tasyāḥ sphuṭaṃ hṛdayam ity api na smareṣūnta rakṣataḥ praviśato vimukho atha vā kva ।। iti tu niyataṃ nārī-rūpaḥ sa loka-dṛśāṃ priyas tava śaṭhatayā śilpotkarṣo vidher vighaṭiṣyate ।। vācaspateḥ । punaruktāvadhi-vāsaram etasyāḥ kitava paśya gaṇayantyāḥ ।
iyam iva karajaḥ kṣīṇas tvam iva kaṭhorāṇi parvāṇi ।। ।। iti dūtīvacana-vrajyā ।। ।। kāntenāśu mudhā vilokitam atho tanvyā mudhā lajjitaṃ bhūyo anena mudhāvakṛṣṭam atha tat tanvyā mudhā saṃvṛtam ।।
pratyakṣaraṃ madana-mantharam arthayantyāḥ kiṃ kiṃ na hanta hṛdayaṅgamam aṅganāyāḥ ।। kṣaṇaṃ śroṇau pāṇī kṣaṇam api kucāgre priya-dṛśoḥ kṣaṇaṃ vinyasyantyār jagad api na mūlyaṃ mṛgadṛśaḥ ।। aṅke nilīya kamituḥ śithilāṅga-mudrā nidrāti nālpa-tapasaḥ phala-saṃpad eṣā ।। yad vardhiṣṇu manobhava-pranayitā yan manda-manyu-grahasḥ tenaiveha mano haraty adharita-prauḍhā navoḍhā na kim ।।
yad bālā balavan manobhava-bhaya-bhraśyat-trapaṃ satrapā tat-kālocita-narma-karma dayitādamyāsyam abhyasyati ।। kasyāpi । tapobhir bhūyobhiḥ kim u na kamanīyaṃ sukṛtinām idaṃ ramyaṃ vāmyaṃ madana-vivaśāyā mṛgadṛśaḥ ।। kasyacit ।
yad ayam udaya-līlā-lālasānāṃ vadhūnāṃ rati-vinimaya-bhājāṃ kelibhir yāti kālaḥ ।। yasmin vismayanīya-tapta-tapase svairaṃ samucchṛṅkhalā viśrāmyanti tava smara-jvara-harāḥ kandarpa-keli-śriyaḥ ।। śroṇīṃ tasya kare adhirohati punar vrīḍāmbudhau mām atho majjantīm udatārayan manasijo devaḥ sa mūrcchā-guruḥ ।। matis tv eṣāsmākaṃ kuca-yuga-taṭī-cumbaka-śilāniveśād ākṛṣṭaḥ smara-śara-śalākotkara iva ।।
nābhī-mūla-nibaddha-cakṣuṣi tayā brīḍānatāṅgyā priye dīpaḥ phūtkṛti-vāta-vepita-śikhaḥ karṇotphalenāhataḥ ।। karṇotpalasya । tad-aṃśukā-kṣepam adhīra-pāṇe vimuñca kāñcī-maṇayo raṇanti ।। etāvat sakhi vedmi kevalam ahaṃ tasyāṅga-saṅge punaḥ ko asau kāsmi rataṃ tu kiṃ katham iti svalpāpi me na smṛtiḥ ।।
vikaṭa-nitambāyāḥ । sakhi svairaṃ svairaṃ suratam akarod vrīḍita-vapuḥ yataḥ paryaṅgo ayaṃ ripur iva kaḍat-kāra-mukharaḥ ।। nīvīṃ prati praṇihite tu kare priyeṇa sakhyaḥ śapāmi yadi kiṃcid api smarāmi ।। vidyāyāḥ ।
ślatha-tanu-bhuja-bandha-prāpra-dīrgha-prasāro mukha-parimala-mugdhaḥ kāntayoḥ śvāsavātaḥ ।। sahūṅkārojjṛmbhā smara-paravaśā kānta-vimukhaṃ mukhaṃ mugdhāpāṅgaṃ kṣipati virasaṃ prauḍha-yuvatī ।। api taruṇayoḥ kiṃ syāt tasyāṃ divi spṛhayālutāḥ mukulita-dṛśor udbhidyante na ced viraha-tviṣaḥ ।। bhāvānām api tādṛśāṃ mṛgadṛśo hāvānugānām aho nādhanyaḥ kurute prarūḍha-pulakair ātithyam aṅgair janaḥ ।।
tayā dṛṣṭiṃ dattvā mahati maṇi-dīpe nipuṇayā niruddhaṃ hastābhyāṃ jhagiti nija-netrotpala-yugam ।। kasyacit । tad evaṃ ko apy ūṣmā ramaṇa-parirambhotsava-milatpurandhrī-nīrandhra-stana-kalaśa-janmā vijayate ।। saṃrambha-ślatha-keśa-bandha-vigalan-muktā-kalāpa-drutachvāsa-ccheda-taraṅgita-stana-yugaṃ prīṇāti śṛṅgāriṇī ।।
sonnokasya । eṇī-dṛśāṃ makara-ketu-niketanāni vandāmahe surata-vibhrama-ceṣṭitāni ।। kasyacit । śramāmbhobhis tamyat-tilaka-malikā-ghūrṇa-dalakaṃ mukhaṃ līlāvatyā harati viparīta-vyatikare ।।
svedaḥ kiṃ na sarinnātho romāñcaḥ kiṃ na parvataḥ ।। anirvyūḍhe tasmin prakṛti-sukumārāṅga-latayā punar lajjālolaṃ mayi vinihitaṃ locana-yugam ।। koṅkasya । sapadi maraṇam eva sā tu yāyād yadi na pibed adharāmṛtaṃ priyasya ।।
svasmāt karān mama kare valayaṃ kṣipantyā vācaṃ vinābhyupagamaḥ kathito mṛgākṣyā ।। patatu tavorasi satataṃ dayitā-dhammilla-mallikā-prakaraḥ । rati-rasa-rabhasa-kaca-graha-lulitālaka-vallarī-galitaḥ ।। ardhocchvāsa-sphuṭa-nakha-padālaṃkṛtābhyāṃ stanābhyāṃ dṛṣṭā dhārṣṭya-smṛti-nata-mukhī mohanānte mayā sā ।।
rājaśekharasya । hariṇa-śiśu-dṛśo asyā mugdha-mugdhaṃ hasantyāḥ pariṇata-śara-kāṇḍa-snigdha-pāṇḍuḥ kapolaḥ ।। sthagayati karaiḥ patyur netre vihasya samākulā surata-viratau ramyaṃ tanvī punaḥ punar īkṣitum ।। kasyāpi ।
prāyaḥ kānte rati-śrānte kāminī puruṣāyate ।। jalpantyaiva muhur naneti nibhṛtaṃ pradhvasta-cāritrayā niḥśeṣeṇa samāpito rati-vidhir vācā tu nāṅgīkṛtaḥ ।। kasyacit । tac chlāghyaṃ surataṃ ca tat tad amṛtaṃ tad vastu tad brahma tac ceto-hāri tad eva tat kim api tat tattvāntaraṃ sarvathā ।।
kuca-kalaśayor ūḍhaḥ kampas tayā mama saṃnidhau manasija-rujo bhāvair uktā vacobhir apahnutāḥ ।। romāñca-kañcuka-tiraskṛta-dehayā vā jñātāni tāni parirambha-sukhāni kiṃ vā ।। acalasya । vilokyāśleṣād apy avahita ivāmīlya nayane vyudañcad-romāñca-sthagita-vapur āliṅgati samām ।।
aśithila-parirambha-vyāpṛtaikaika-doṣṇor avidita-gata-yāmā rātrir eva vyaraṃsīt ।। nirvyūḍhaṃ na yadā tayā tad akhilaṃ khinnais tatas tārakaiḥ sa-vrīḍaiś ca vilokitair mayi punar nyastaḥ samasto vyayaḥ ।। kasyacit । iha hi niviḍa-vrīḍānaṅga-jvarātura-cetasor nava-taruṇayoḥ ko jānīte kim adya phaliṣyati ।।
lajjā-mugdha-vilocana-smita-sudhā-nirdhauta-bimbādharaṃ kampa-praślatha-bāhu-bandhanam asāv āliṅgito bālayā ।। kasyacit । ujjṛmbhaḥ kila vallabho api virate vastuny api prastute ghūrṇantī kila sāpi hūṅkṛtavatī śūnyaṃ sakhī dakṣiṇā ।। īṣad-vakrima-kandharaḥ sa-pulakaḥ premollasan-mānasām antar-hāsa-lasat-kapola-phalakāṃ dhūrto aparāṃ cumbati ।।
bahir vyājāmarṣa-prasara-paruṣāntar-gata-rasā nirīkṣyā re māyī kim idam iti pūrvā vijayate ।। antar-gūḍha-vigāḍha-saṃbhrama-rasa-sphārī-bhavad-gaṇḍayā tūṣṇīṃ śāri-visāraṇāya nihitaḥ khedāmbu-garbhaḥ karaḥ ।। rājaśekharasya । bhogaḥ sa yadyapi jaye ca parājaye ca yūnor manas tad api vāñchati jetum eva ।।
murāreḥ । dayitam abhitas tām utkaṇṭhāṃ vivavrur anantaraṃ jhaṭiti jhaṭiti truṭyanto antaḥ stanāṃśuka-sandhayaḥ ।। nidhuvana-yudhas tūryātodyaṃ jahāra nata-bhruvāṃ jaghana-sarasī-haṃsa-svānaḥ śrutiṃ rasanā-ravaḥ ।। śruti-kuvalayaṃ dīpocchittyai nirāsa yad aṅganā jvalati rasanā-rocir dīpe tad āpa nirarthatām ।।
na bhuja-latikā-gāḍhāśleṣaiḥ śramaṃ lalitā yayur yuvatiṣu kim apy avyākhyeyaṃ smarasya vijṛmbhitam ।। vilayanam atha prāptā rāgānaloṣmabhir ity aho na pati-bhujayor niṣyandāntaḥ priyā niravīyata ।। ।। iti saṃbhoga-vrajyā ।। ।।
antaḥ-pravṛddha-makara-dhvaja-pāvakasya śaṅke vibhidya hṛdayaṃ niraguḥ sphuliṅgāḥ ।। rājaśekharasya । lāvaṇya-saṃbhāra-nidhāna-kumbhe mudrākṣarāṇīva manobhavasya ।। kasyacit ।
valī-bhaṅgābhogeṣv alaka-patitākīrṇa-kusumaḥ striyāḥ sarvāvasthaṃ kathayati rataṃ pracchada-paṭaḥ ।। āvṛṇoti vivṛṇoti cekṣate labdha-ratnam iva duḥkhito janaḥ ।। kasyacit । tirayati śiśu-līlānartana-cchadma-tālapracala-valaya-mālāsphāla-kolāhalena ।।
ratautsukyāt tāmyat-tarala-manasoḥ paryavasite kṛtārthatve anyonyaṃ tad anu viditau kiṃ na kurutām ।। paśyasi nakha-saṃbhūtāṃ rekhāṃ varatanu payodharopānte । kiṃ vāsasā stanāntaṃ ruṇatsi hima-ruci-kṛte vacmi ।। tat sānanda-milad-dṛśoḥ katham api smṛtvā gurūṇāṃ puroaḥ hāsodbheda-nirodha-manthara-milat-tāraṃ kathaṃcit sthitam ।।
ārdrāṇi kuṅkuma-rucīni vilāsinīnām aṅgeṣu kiṃ nakha-padāni na maṇḍalāni ।। karṇālaṃkṛti-padma-rāga-śakalaṃ vinyasya cañcū-puṭe vrīḍārtā prakaroti dāḍima-phala-vyājena vāg-bandhanam ।। vadhū-vaktraṃ vrīḍābhara-namitam antar vihasitaṃ haraty ardhonmīlan-nalina-malināvarjitam iva ।। idaṃ tarītuṃ trivalī-taraṅgiṇīṃ virājate pañca-śarasya naur iva ।।
kasyacit । kāminyā smara-vedanākula-dṛśā yaḥ keli-kāle kṛtaḥ so atyarthaṃ katham anyathā dahati mām eṣa tvad-oṣṭha-vraṇaḥ ।। kasyacit । abhimukha-patayālubhir lalāṭa-śrama-salilair avidhauta-patra-lekhaḥ ।
kathayati puruṣāyitaṃ vadhūnāṃ mṛdita-hima-dyuti-durmanāḥ ।। murāreḥ । api rahasi kṛtānāṃ vāg-vihīno api jātaḥ surata-vilasitānāṃ varṇako varṇako asau ।। pratidiśam apara-strī-saṃga-śaṃsī visarpan nava-parimala-gandhaḥ kena śakyo varītum ।।
eṇīdṛśaḥ kusuma-cāpa-narendra-dattā jaitra-praśastir iva citra-lipir vibhāti ।। dakṣasya । mugdhe hastaḥ kim-artho ayam apārtha iha dīyate ।। lasat-kāñcī-granthi-sphurad-aruṇa-ratnāṃśu jaghanaṃ priyāṅgonmṛṣṭāṅgyā viṣam idam iyad bhāvaka-nṛṇām ।।
krīḍā-śārikayā nilīya nibhṛtaṃ trotuṃ trapārtāṃ vadhūṃ prārabdhaḥ sahasaiva saṃbhrama-karo mārjāra-garjā-ravaḥ ।। āḥ kiṃ chadma-vidagdha-mānini mayi brūṣe puro-bhāgini krūrair ullikhitāsmi tatra kusumāny uccinvatī kaṇṭakaiḥ ।। ito niṣkrāmantī nava-rati-guroḥ proñchati vadhūḥ sva-kastūrī-patrāṅkura-makarikā-mudritam uraḥ ।। likhantīnāṃ patrāṅkuram aniśam asyās tu kucayoś camatkāro gūḍhaṃ karaja-padam āsāṃ kathayati ।।
murārer etau murāreḥ ।etau ।। iti samāpta-nidhuvana-cihna-vrajyā ।। ।। ākāra-mātra-masṛṇena viceṣṭitena dhūrtasya tasya hi guṇān upavarṇayanti ।।
tad api na mayā saṃbhāṣyo asau punar dayitaḥ śaṭhaḥ sphuṭati hṛdayaṃ maunenāntar na me yadi tat-kṣaṇāt ।। amaroḥ । yad uktaṃ pratyuktaṃ tad apaṭu śiraḥ kampana-paraṃ priyā mānenāho punar api kṛtā me nava-vadhūḥ ।। yadi niyamitaṃ dhyāne cakṣuḥ kathaṃ pulakodgamaḥ kṛtam abhinayair dṛṣṭo mānaḥ prasīda kim ucyatām ।।
amaroḥ । ālāpo api na miśritaḥ parijanaṃ vyāpārayanty āntike kāntaṃ pratyupacārataś caturayā kopaḥ kṛtārthīkṛtaḥ ।। hastābhyām api vāritaḥ sapulakaḥ svedodgamo gaṇḍayoḥ sakhyaḥ kiṃ karavāṇi yānti sahasā yat kañcuke sandhayaḥ ।। māninyāś caraṇānati-vyatikare bāṣpāmbu-pūrṇekṣaṇaṃ cakṣur jātam aho prapañca-caturaṃ jātāgasi preyasi ।।
tasyaiva । samāśvāsas tena praṇata-śirasaḥ patyur abhavat priyā prauḍha-krodhāpy apahṛtavatī yan na caraṇau ।। āgaskāriṇy aham iha yayā jīvitaṃ tad-viyoge bhartṛ-prāṇāḥ striya iti nanu tvaṃ mamaivānuneyaḥ ।। yal lajjā niruṇaddhi yatra śapathair utpādyate pratyayaḥ tat kiṃ prema sa ucyate paricayas tatrāpi kopena kim ।।
dhairyaṃ kartum api sthirīkṛtam idaṃ cetaḥ kathaṃcin mayā baddho māna-parigrahe parikaraḥ siddhis tu daiva-sthitā ।। idānīṃ nāthas tvaṃ vayam api kalatraṃ kim aparaṃ mayāptaṃ prāṇānāṃ kuliśa-kaṭhinānāṃ phalam idam ।। amaroḥ । idānīm arkas tvaṃ khara-ruci samutsārita-rasaḥ kirantī kopāgnīn aham api ravi-grāva-ghaṭitā ।।
acala-siṃhasya । tasya premṇas tad idam adhunā vaiṣamaṃ paśya jātaṃ tvaṃ pādānte luṭhasi nahi me manyu-mokṣaḥ khalāyāḥ ।। tad etat kvācakṣe ghṛta-madhu-maya tvan-mṛdu-vacoviṣeṇāghūrṇantī kim api na sakhīyaṃ gaṇayati ।। hiṅgokasya ।।
keli-skhalad-vasanam utpulakāṅga-bhaṅgam uttuṅga-pīna-kucam ālikhitā tvam eva ।। vīrya-mitrasya ।। mugdhe cumbatu nāma cañcalatayā bhṛṅgaḥ kvacit kandalīm unmīlan-nava-mālatī-parimalaḥ kiṃ tena vismaryate ।। kasyacit ।
prāṇeśvaraś caraṇayoḥ patitas tavāyaṃ saṃbhāṣyatāṃ vikasatā nayanotpalena ।। tat kiṃ rodiṣi gadgadena vacasā kasyāgrato rudyate nanv etan mama kā tavāsmi dayitā nāsmīty ato rudyate ।। praṇāmānto mānas tyajasi na tathāpi krudham aho kuca-pratyāsattyā hṛdayam api te caṇḍi kaṭhinam ।। idaṃ nidrā-cchede rasati sarasaṃ sāra-sakulaṃ cakorākṣi kṣipraṃ jahihi jahihi prema-laḍitam ।।
ayaṃ tvākūtajñaḥ pariṇati-parāmarśa-kuśalaḥ sakhī līko apy āsīl likhita iva citreṇa kim idam ।। bimbokasya । tava yathā tathābhūtaṃ prema prapannam imāṃ daśāṃ prakṛti-capale kā naḥ pīḍā gate hata-jīvite ।। gṛhāṇainaṃ mugdhe vrajatu tava kaṇṭha-praṇayitām upāyo nāsty anyo hṛdaya-paritāpopaśamane ।।
bhaṭṭahareḥ । samākṛṣṭā hy ete viraha-dahanodbhāsura-śikhāḥ sva-hastenāñgārās tad alam adhunāraṇya-ruditaiḥ ।। kaḥ kopāvasaraḥ prasīda rahasi svedāmbhasaṃ bindavo lumpantu stana-patra-bhaggam akarīḥ saudhā-guru-śyāmalāḥ ।। mugdhe dagdha-giraḥ skhalanti śataśaḥ kim kupyasi preyasi prāṇās tanvi mamāsi nocitam idaṃ tad vyartham uttāmyasi ।।
tataḥ śroṇī-bimbaṃ vyavasita-vilāsaṃ tad ucitaṃ svabhāva-svacchānāṃ vipad api sukhaṃ nāntarayati ।। kasyacit । kasmād brūhi tavādya kaṇṭha-vigalan-muktāvalī-vibhramaṃ bibhrāṇā nipatanti bāṣpa-payasāṃ prasyandino bindavaḥ ।। rājaśekharasya ।
muhuḥ kaṇṭhe lagnas taralayati bāṣpaḥ stana-taṭaṃ priyo manyur jātas tava niranurodhe na tu vayam ।। smaḥ kecin na vayaṃ yad ekam aparasyāpy uktam ākarṇyatāṃ atyunmāthini candane api niyataṃ nāmāgnir uttiṣṭhati ।। iti sarabhasaṃ mānāṭopād udīrya vacas tayā ramaṇa-padavī sāraṅgākṣyā sa-śaṅkitam īkṣitā ।। dampatyoḥ śanakair apāṅga-valanān miśrī-bhavac-cakṣuṣor bhagno mānakaliḥ sahāsa-rabhasaṃ vyāsakta-kaṇṭha-graham ।।
paśya prasīda caramācala-cūla-cumbi bimbaṃ vidhor lavala-pāṇḍu-rasas tam eti ।। samānābhijñānaṃ katham itarathā paśyati puro bhavān ekas tasyāḥ pratikṛti-mayīr eva ramaṇīḥ ।। prasīda premāpi praśamayatu niḥśeṣam adhṛtīr abhūmiḥ kopānāṃ nanu niraparādhaḥ parijanaḥ ।। ḍimbokasya ।
āśleṣam arpaya mad-arpita-pūrvam uccair uccaiḥ samarpaya mad-arpita-cumbanaṃ ca ।। sakhi kalitaḥ skhalito ayaṃ heyo naiva praṇāma-mātreṇa । ciram anubhavatu bhavatyā bāhu-latā-bandhanaṃ dhūrtaḥ ।। māyā-svāpam upetya tan-nipuṇayā nidrāndhyam āceṣṭitaṃ māna-mlānir abhūn na yena ca na cāpy āsīd rahaḥk-haṇḍanam ।।
smita-jyotsnārambha-kṣapita-viraha-dhvānta-nivahoaḥ mukhendur māninyāḥ sphurati kṛta-puṇyasya surate ।। mānī so api jano na lāghava-bhayād abhyeti mātaḥ svayaṃ kālo yāti calaṃ ca jīvitam iti kṣuṇṇaṃ manaś cintayā ।। dṛṣṭe dhūrta-viceṣṭite tu dayite tasmin avaśyaṃ mama svedāmbhaḥ-pratirodhi-nirbharatara-smeraṃ mukhaṃ jāyate ।। tvat-kṛtyaṃ tvad-agocare api hi kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ mayaivādhunā mām ājñāpaya kiṃ karomi sarale bhūyaḥ sapatnyās tava ।।
kasyacit । iti nigadati nāthe tiryag-āmīlitākṣyā nayana-jalam analpaṃ muktam uktaṃ na kiṃcit ।। tat-tat-kopa-viceṣṭite kusumitaṃ pādānate tu priye māninyāṃ phalitaṃ tu māna-taruṇā paryanta-bandhyāyitam ।। ruṣaṃ muñcāmuñca priyam anugṛhānāyatihitaṃ śṛṇu tvaṃ yad brūmaḥ priya-sakhi na māne kuru matim ।।
kasyacit । eṣā kapola-phalake agaru-patra-vallī kiṃ pīḍyate sutanu bāṣpa-jala-praṇālaiḥ ।। ity uktvāśru-galan-mukhī viṭa-sakhī dhvastā viśantī gṛhaṃ dhanyenādhim upāśruṇor asi kṛtātyantaṃ priyā roditā ।। na jānīmaḥ kiṃ nu kva nu kiyad anena vyavasitaṃ yad asyāḥ pratyaṅgaṃ nayana-jala-bindur viharati ।।
kasyacit । vada suvadane lajjā-mūkā bhavantu śikhaṇḍinaḥ paraparibhavo māna-sthānair na mānini sahyate ।। kapole yal-lākṣā-bahala-rasa-rāga-praṇayinīm imāṃ dhatte mudrām anaticira-vṛttānta-piśunām ।। yūnor mitho abhilaṣatoḥ prathamānunītiṃ bhāvāḥ prasāda-piśunāḥ kṣapayanti nidrām ।।
kaṭhina-hṛdaye mithyā-mauna-vrata-vyasanād ayaṃ parijana-parityāgopāyo na māna-parigrahaḥ ।। kasyacit । idaṃ tu preyasyāḥ prathayati ruṣo antarvikasitāḥ śate api praśnānāṃ yad abhidura-mudrodhara-puṭaḥ ।। vaidyadhanyasya ।
kiṃ tu prasādana-bhayād atinihnutena kopena ko api nihito adya rasāvatāraḥ ।। ūrvor gāḍha-nipīḍanena jaghane pāṇiṃ ca ruddhvānayā patyuḥ prema na khaṇḍitaṃ nipuṇayā māno api naivojjhitaḥ ।। visrambhaika-rasa-prasāda-madhurā yatra pravṛttāḥ kathās tāny anyāni dināni muñca caraṇau saivāham anyo bhavān ।। manasvinyāḥ svairaṃ prasarati niśā-sīma-samaye manaḥ pratyāvṛttaṃ kamitari kathaṃcin na tu vapuḥ ।।
tāvat kiṃ kathayāmi keli-paṭunā nirgatya kuñjodarād ajñātopanatena tena sahasā mūrdhnaiva saṃbhāvitaḥ ।। mama tu manasaḥ saṃtāpo ayaṃ priye vimukho api yat katham api hata-vrīḍaṃ ceto na yāti virāgitām ।। kasyacit । ruddhāyām api vāci sasmitam idaṃ dagdhānanaṃ jāyate dṛṣṭe nirvahaṇaṃ bhaviṣyati kathaṃ mānasya tasmin jane ।।
tāvat pratyuta pāṇi-saṃpuṭa-lasan-nīvī-nibandhaṃ dhṛto dhāvitv eva kṛta-praṇāmakam aho premṇo vicitrā gatiḥ ।। tad utprekṣyotprekṣya priyasakhi gatāṃs tāṃś ca divasān na jāne ko hetur dalati śatadhā yan na hṛdayam ।। sutanu nitambas tava pṛthur akṣṇor api niyatam arjuno mahimā । madhyaḥ savalir idāniṃ māndhātā kuca-taṭaḥ kriyatām ।।
nīvī-bandhavadāgataṃ śithilatāṃ saṃbhāṣamāṇe tato mānenāpasṛtaṃ hriyeva sudṛśaḥ pāda-spṛśi preyasi ।। kasyacit । ।। iti māninī-vrajyā ।। ।।
kiṃ cāsyā malaya-druma-drava-bharair limpāmi yāvat karaṃ tāvac chvāsa-samīraṇa-vyatikarair uddhūlitr āsīt karaḥ ।। tvyaktvā tān bata haṃsi mām api kṛśāṃ bālām anāthāṃ striyaṃ dhik tvā dhik tava pauruṣaṃ dhig udayaṃ dhik kārmukaṃ dhik śarān ।। śrī-rājyapālasya । tenendur dahanāyate malayajālepaḥ sphuliṅgāyate rātriḥ kalpa-śatāyate visalatāhāro api bhārāyate ।।
kasyacit । maunaṃ cedam idaṃ ca śūnyam akhilaṃ yad viśvam ābhāti te tad brūyāḥ sakhi yoginī kim asi bhoḥ kiṃ vā viyoginy api ।। naitat toyaṃ nabhastaḥ patati mada-jalaṃ śvāsa-vātāvadhūtaṃ tat kiṃ mugdhe vṛthā tvaṃ malinayasi mukhaṃ prāvṛḍ ity aśru-pātaiḥ ।। no cet sneha-rasāvaseka-vikasaj-jvālāvalī-dāruṇo dārūṇīva na me viraṃsyati dahann aṅgāny anaṅgānalaḥ ।।
sakhi priyas te kṣaṇikaḥ kim anyan nirātmakaḥ śūnyatamaḥ sa vandyaḥ ।। ardhāvadagdha-galad-aṅga-rasāvasiktam ardrendhanaṃ tad iva bhasma-kaṇānuyātam ।। itīva pratyaṅga-prathita-madanāgniṃ kṛśa-tanur ghana-śvāsotkṣepair jvalayati muhur mṛtyu-vaśinī ।। idaṃ vyasta-nyāsaṃ ślatha-bhuja-latākṣepa-valanaiḥ kṛśāṅgyāḥ saṃtāpaṃ vadati visinī-patra-śayanam ।।
kasyacit । hinasti pratyaṅgaṃ jvara iva garīyān ita ito na māṃ trātuṃ tātaḥ prabhavati na cāmbā na bhavatī ।। niḥśaktīkṛta-candanauṣadhi-vidhāv tasmiṃś camat-kāriṇo lāja-sphoṭam amī sphuṭanti maṇayo viśve api hāra-srajām ।। rājaśekharasya ।
gaurī krudhyatu vartate yadi na te tat ko api citte yuvā dhig dhik tvāṃ saha-pāṃśu-khelana-sakhī-loke api yan nihnavaḥ ।। rājaśekharasya । yāvat kiṃcid udantam ātmakam itus tāvat sa evety atha vrīḍā-vakrita-kaṇṭha-nālam abalā kaiḥ kair na bhinnā rasaiḥ ।। kasyacit ।
iha hi tava luṭhantaḥ ploṣa-pīḍāṃ bhajante dara-jaṭhara-mṛṇālī-kāṇḍa-mugdhā mayūkhāḥ ।। kasyacit । ekādhīnaṃ kathayati manas tāvad eṣā daśā te kosāv ekaḥ kathaya sumukhi brahma vā vallabho vā ।। lakṣmīdharasya ।
avasthām āpannā madana-dahanoddāha-vidhurām iyaṃ naḥ kalyāṇī ramayati matiṃ kalpayati ca ।। bhavabhūteḥ । kiṃ cānyat priya-saṃgame adya calito gacchan vipad-vatsalo mūrcchā-vismṛti-vedanā-parijano dṛṣṭo asmadīyo na vā ।। aravindasya ।
haṃho vāyasa rājahaṃsa śuka he he sārike kathyatāṃ kā vārteti mṛgīdṛśo vijayate bāṣpāntarāyaṃ vacaḥ ।। citrāṅgasya । balavati sati yasmin sārdham āvartya hemnā rajatam iva mṛgākṣyāḥ kalpitāny aṅgakāni ।। rājaśekharasya ।
nirlajjā he jīvita na śrutaṃ kiṃ mahājano yena gataḥ sa panthāḥ ।। itthaṃ yasya viyoga-yoga-vidhuraṃ mugdhe tavedaṃ vapur no jāne katamaḥ sa puṣpa-dhanuṣā nītaḥ prasāda-śriyam ।। śṛṅgāra-vāri-ruha-kānana-rāja-haṃsi kasmāt kṛśāsi virasāsi malīmasāsi ।। viramati rajanī na saṅgam āśā vrajati tanus tanutāṃ na cānurāgaḥ ।।
pravarasenasya । ākarṣaka-drāvaka-cumbakeṣu naiko apy asau bhrāmaka ity avaihi ।। praṣṭavyaḥ śivamāli kevalam asau kaccid bhavad-gocare nāyātaṃ malayānilair mukulitaṃ kaccin na cūtair iti ।। vākkūṭasya ।
mugdheyaṃ kurute atha tad-guṇa-kathāṃ manyur girām argalaḥ prāyaḥ puṇya-dinānubhāva-valanād āśaṃsitaṃ sidhyati ।। etāṃ mlānim upāgatāṃ srajam iva tyaktvā tanuṃ durvahām eṣāhaṃ sukhinī bhavāmi na sahe tīvrāṃ viyoga-vyathām ।। kasyacit । yāntyaiva sva-niveśanaṃ pratipathaṃ pāntha-striyāsmin kṣaṇe mā bhūd āgata ity amanda-valitodgrīvaṃ muhur vīkṣitam ।।
siddhokasya । aṅgeṣu prathama-prabuddha-phalinī lāvaṇya-saṃpādinī pāṇḍimnā virahocitena gamitā kāntiḥ kathā-gocaram ।। śadhokasya । api stokonnidrair nayana-kumudair modaya diśoaḥ viśeṣās te mugdhe dadhatu kṛtināṃ cetasi padam ।।
ayam asamayaṃ kiṃ ca klāmyaty asaṃsmaraṇena te śaśimukhi sakhī-hasta-nyasto vilāsa-paricchadaḥ ।। abhinandasya । saṃkrāntair valayair alaṃkṛta-galo yuṣmad-viyogocitāṃ tanvaṅgyāḥ prakaṭīkarīti tanutām aṅge bhraman vāyasaḥ ।। kasyacit ।
bāle bāla-mṛṇāla-nāla-valayālaṃkāra-kānte kare vinyasyānanam āyatākṣi sukṛtī ko ayaṃ tvayā smaryate ।। kṣaṇam api sukhaṃ yasmin prāpte gate ca na labhyate kim aparam ataś citraṃ yan me tathāpi sa vallabhaḥ ।। kasyacit । yaṃ dhyāyantyāḥ sumukhi likhitaṃ kajjala-kleda-bhāñji vyālumpanti stana-kalasayoḥ patram aśrūṇy ajasram ।।
koka-bhrānti-kṣaṇa-virahiṇīyan mayākāri haṃsī tasyaitan me phalam upanataṃ nātha yat te viyogaḥ ।। kiṃ cākuñcita-kaṇṭha-rodha-kuṭilāḥ śrotrāmṛta-syandinoaḥ hūṅkārāḥ kala-pañcama-praṇayinas truṭyanti niryānti ca ।। ayaṃ mugdhe candraḥ kim iti mayi tāpaṃ prakaṭayaty anāthānāṃ bāle kim iha viparītaṃ na bhavati ।। svapnāsādita-saṃgame priyatame sānandam āliṅgite svacchando bhavatāṃ bhaviṣyati punaḥ kaṣṭo viceṣṭā-rasaḥ ।।
taralita-kara-śākhā-mañjarīkaḥ śarīre dhanuṣi ca makare ca svastha-rekhā-niveśaḥ ।। akṣṇor bāṣpa-cayaṃ nigṛhya katham apy ālokitaḥ kevalaṃ kiṃcit-kuḍmala-koṭi-bhinna-śikharaś cūta-drumaḥ prāṅgaṇe ।। vākkūṭasya । āpāṇḍuḥ kara-pallave ca nibhṛtaṃ śete kapola-sthalī mugdhe kasya tapaḥ-phalaṃ pariṇataṃ yasmai taveyaṃ daśā ।।
yaṃ dhyāyantī sutanu bahula-jvāla-kandarpa-vahniprodyad-bhasma-pracaya-racitāpāṇḍimānaṃ dadhāsi ।। tatraivāstāṃ dahati nayane candravac candanāmbhaḥ sakhyas toyendhana iva śikhī vipratīpo ayam ādhiḥ ।। āste kevalam abjinī-kisalaya-prastāri-śayyā-tale saṃkalpopanata-tvad-ākṛtir asāyat tena cittena sā ।। rājaśekharasya ।
cittātaṅkaṃ nija-garimataḥ samyag āsūtrayanto niryānty asyāḥ kuvalaya-dṛśo bāṣpa-vārāṃ pravāhāḥ ।। vārāṃ pūraḥ katham aparathā sphāra-netra-praṇālīvaktrodvāntas trivali-vipine sāraṇī-sāmyam eti ।। talpādṛśya-karaṅka-pañjaram idaṃ jīvena liptaṃ manāṅ muñcantī kim u kartum icchasi kuru premānya-deśa-gate ।। tat kiṃ roditi muhyati śvasiti kiṃ smeraṃ ca dhatte mukhaṃ dṛṣṭaḥ kiṃ katham apy akāraṇa-ripuḥ śrī-bhojya-devo anayā ।।
chittapasya । dṛśaḥ sāmarthyāni sthagayati muhur bāṣpa-salilaṃ prapañco ayaṃ kiṃcit tava sakhi hṛdi-sthaṃ kathayati ।। narasiṃhasya । kim api sakhi kuru tvaṃ deha-yātrānurūpaṃ śatam iha virahiṇyo nedṛśaṃ kvāpi dṛṣṭam ।।
।। iti virahiṇī-vrajyā ।। ।। bhramati bhuvane kandarpājñā vikāri ca yauvanaṃ lalita-madhurās te te bhāvāḥ kṣipanti ca dhīratām ।। sadyaḥ svidyann ayam aviratotkampa-lolāṅgulīkaḥ pāṇir lekhā-vidhiṣu nitarāṃ vartate kiṃ karomi ।।
tām īṣat-pracala-vilocanāṃ natāṅgīm āliṅgan pavana mama spṛśāṅgam aṅgam ।। jvalati ca tanūm antar-dāhaḥ karoti na bhasmasāt praharati vidhir marma-cchedī na kṛntati jīvitam ।। daivenāntarita-priyo asi hariṇa tvaṃ cāpi kiṃ yac ciraṃ pradadri pratikandaraṃ pratinadi prayūṣaraṃ bhrāmyasi ।। muñjasya ।
