kārāgāre kṣipata tarasā pañcamaṃ rāgarājaṃ candraṃ cūrṇī-kuruta ca śilā-paṭṭake piṣṭa-peṣam ।। ghanoru-prāg-bhāraṃ nidhi-mukham ivāmudritam aho kadā nu drakṣyāmo vigalita-dukūlaṃ mṛga-dṛśaḥ ।। ete kiṃśuka-śākhino api malinair aṅgāritāḥ kuḍmalaiḥ kaṣṭaṃ viśramayāmi kutra nayane sarvatra vāmo vidhiḥ ।। vākkūṭasya ।
ā jñātaṃ madhulampaṭair madhukarair ābaddha-kolāhale nūnaṃ sāhasikena cūta-mukule dṛṣṭiḥ samāropitā ।। rājaśekharasya । api nanu śaśalakṣman mā mucas tvaṃ ca tasyāṃ akaruṇa-kiraṇolkāḥ kandalī-komalāyām ।। nidre kiṃ viratāsi tāvad aghṛṇe yāvan na tasyāś cirāt krīḍanti kramaśaḥ kṛśīkṛta-ruṣaḥ pratyaṅgam aṅgāni me ।।
svapnena dviṣatendra-jālam iva me saṃdarśitā kevalaṃ cetas tat-parirambhaṇāya tad api sphīta-spṛhaṃ tāmyati ।। kasyacit ।। śayyā-niśītha-kalaheṣu mṛgekṣaṇāyāḥ prāptaṃ mayā vidhi-vaśād idam uttarīyam ।। udgrīvaś caraṇārdha-ruddha-vasudhaḥ kṛtvāśru-pūrṇāṃ dṛśaṃ tām āśāṃ pathikas tathāpi kim api dhyāyaṃś ciraṃ vīkṣate ।।
tenāsmākam iyaṃ gatir matir iyaṃ saṃvṛttir evaṃvidhā tāpo ayaṃ tanur īdṛśī sthitir iyaṃ tasyā apīti śrutiḥ ।। viyoge tanvaṅgyāḥ kalayati sa evāyam adhunā himartur naidāghīm ahaha viṣamāṃ tāpana-rujam ।। so apy astu nāma jagataḥ pratipakṣa-bhūtaś cūta-drumaḥ kim iti nirmita eṣa dhātrā ।। kiṃ brūmo vayam apy anena hatakenāpuṅkha-magnaiḥ śarair viddhā eva na cedṛśaḥ parikarasyaivaṃ-vidhā vedanā ।।
kāntāpāda-talāhatis tava mude tadvan mamāpy āvayoḥ sarvaṃ tulyam aśoka kevalam ahaṃ dhātrā sa-śokaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। kaṣṭaṃ kāma nirāyudho asi bhavatā jetuṃ na śakyo jano duḥkhī syām aham eka eva sakalo lokaḥ sukhaṃ jīvatu ।। rājaśekharasya । tataḥ snāna-krīḍā-janita-jaḍa-bhāvair avayavaiḥ kadācin muñceyaṃ madana-śikhi-pīḍā-paribhavam ।।
idaṃ cāsmat-karṇe yadi bhavati kenāpi kathitaṃ tad icchāmaḥ saṅgād viraha-bharam ekatra vasatau ।। visṛjati hima-garbhair agnim indur mayūkhais tvam api kusuma-bāṇān vajra-sārī-karoṣi ।। yad bālendu-kalodayād avacitaiḥ sārair ivotpāditaṃ tat paśyeyam anaṅga-maṅgala-gṛhaṃ bhūyo api tasyā mukham ।। bhavabhūteḥ ।
jitās tu bhrū-bhaṅgārcana-vadana-lāvaṇya-rucibhiḥ saroṣā no jāne mṛgadṛśi vidhāsyanti kim amī ।। tad anu ca mṛdu-snigdhālāpa-kramāhita-narmaṇaḥ surata-sacivair aṅgaiḥ saṅgo mamāpi bhaviṣyati ।। bhrū-bhaṅgaṃ kurute na sā dhṛta-dhanur mathnāti māṃ manmathaḥ ko vā tām abalāṃ vilokya sahasā nātropakṛcchro bhavet ।। tat-kāruṇya-parigrahāt kuru dayām asmin vidheye jane svāmin manmatha tādṛśaṃ punar api svapnādbhutaṃ darśaya ।।
priyāyā bālatvād abhinava-viyogāt tava tanor na jānīmas tasyā bata katham amī yānti divasāḥ ।। kasyacit । kacākarṣa-krīḍā-sarala-surala-śreṇī-subhagaṃ kadā tad draṣṭavyaṃ vadanam avadātaṃ mṛgadṛśaḥ ।। kasyacit ।
aham iva śūnyam araṇyaṃ vayam iva tanutāṃ gatāni toyāni । asmākam ivocchvāsā divasā dīrghāś ca taptāś ca ।। sā naś cetasi kīliteva viśikhaiś ceto-bhuvaḥ pañcabhiś cintā-saṃtati-tantu-jāla-niviḍasyūteva lagnā priyā ।। tal-lāvaṇya-jalāvagāhana-jaḍair aṅgair anaṅgānalajvālā-jāla-mucas tyajeyam asamāḥ prāṇa-cchido vedanāḥ ।।
itīmām udbhūtāṃ sphuṭam anupapattiṃ manasi me rudām āvirbhāvād anubhava-virodhaḥ śamayati ।। mṛgarājasya । avyakta-hūṅkṛti-calat-kuca-maṇḍalāyās tasyāḥ smarāmi muhur ardha-vilokitāni ।। adya smarāmi parimṛjya paṭāñcalena netre tayā kim api yat punaruktam uktam ।।
sonnokasya । śītāṃśu-bimba-galitāmṛta-nirmiteti bālām abāla-hariṇāṅka-mukhīṃ smarāmi ।। nilīyānyonyasmin upari sahakārāṅkura-mayī samīkṣante pakṣmāntara-tarala-tārā virahiṇaḥ ।। kalā na yadi śītāṃśor ambare kati tārakāḥ ।।
upari ghanaṃ ghana-paṭalaṃ dūre kāntā tad etad āpatitam । himavati divyauṣadhayaḥ krodhāviṣṭaḥ phaṇī śirasi ।। sthagitaṃ navāmbuvāhair uttānāsyo vilokayan vyoma । saṃkramayatīva pathikas taj-jala-nivahaṃ sva-locanayoḥ ।।
lāvaṇyāmṛta-bindu-varṣi vadanaṃ tac caivam eṇīdṛśas tasyās tad vayam ekam evam asakṛd dhyāyanta evāsmahe ।। yad amṛta-rasāsārasrudbhir dhinoty akhilaṃ jagaj jvalayati tu mām ebhir vahni-cchaṭā-kaṭubhiḥ karaiḥ ।। prāptās tasya viyoginaḥ smṛti-pathaṃ khedaṃ samātanvate premārdrāḥ sudṛśo vikuñcana-tati-preṅkhat-kaṭākṣā dṛśaḥ ।। muktās tanvyā masṛṇa-paruṣās te kaṭākṣa-kṣuraprāś chinnaṃ chinnaṃ hṛdayam adayaiś chidyate adyāpi yair me ।।
candraṃ cūrṇayata kṣaṇāc ca kaṇaśaḥ kṛtvā śilā-paṭṭake yena draṣṭum ahaṃ kṣame daśa diśas tad vaktra-mudrāṅkitāḥ ।। yasyāmībhir itas tataś ca viśikhair āpuṅkha-magnātmabhir jātaṃ me vidalat-kadamba-mukula-spaṣṭopamānaṃ manaḥ ।। spardhā te vadanāmbujair mṛga-dṛśāṃ tat-sthāṇu-cūḍāmaṇe haṃho candra kathaṃ nu muñcasi mayi jvālā-muco vedanāḥ ।। rājaśekharasya ।
ayi pibata cakorāḥ kṛtsnam unnāmi-kaṇṭha-krama-saralita-cañcac-cañcavaś candrikāmbhaḥ । viraha-vidhuritānāṃ jīvita-trāṇa-hetor bhavati hariṇa-lakṣmā yena tejo-daridraḥ ।। ity eṣāṃ kim ivāstu hanta madana-jyotir-vighātāya yad bāhyākāra-paribhrameṇa tu vayaṃ tattva-tyajo vañcitāḥ ।। kusuma-śayanaṃ kāmāstrāṇāṃ karoti sahāyatāṃ dvi-guṇa-harimā māronmāthaḥ kathaṃ nu viraṃsyati ।।
yasyendhanāni sarasāny api candanāni nirvāṇam eṣyati kathaṃ sa manobhavāgniḥ ।। kasyacit । [amaru; sbhsuā bāṇa-kaveḥ; auc bhaṭṭa-bāṇasya] hāra-prakāṇḍa-saralāḥ katham anyathāmī śvāsāḥ parvartita-dukūla-daśāḥ saranti ।। kasyacit । [vid ]
akṛta-premaiva varaṃ na punaḥ saṃjāta-vighaṭita-premā । uddhṛta-nayanas tāmyati yathā hi na tatheha jātāndhaḥ ।। kasyacit । [sbhsuā raviguptasya] dṛṣṭvā satī niviḍa-bāhu-nabandha-lagnaṃ tatraiva māṃ nayati sā yadi vā na yāti ।।
kālidāsasya । ।। iti virahi-vrajyā ।। ।। ekākiny api yāmi tad varam itaḥ srotas tamālākulaṃ nīrandhrās tanum ālikhantu jaṭhara-cchedānala-granthayaḥ ।।
vidyāyāḥ । vicchinne smara-talpa-kalpana-vidhi-cchedopayoge adhunā te jāne jaraṭhī-bhavanti vigalan nīla-tviṣaḥ pallavāḥ ।। avinayavatī-nirviccheda-smara-vyaya-dāyinaḥ kathaya murale kenāmī te kṛtā nicula-drumāḥ ।। vidyāyāḥ ।
caṇḍāṃśor api raśmayaḥ pratidiśaṃ mlānās tvam eko yuvā sthānaṃ nāsti gṛhe mamāpi bhavato bālāham ekākinī ।। viṭapini śiśira-cchāye kṣaṇam iha viśramya gamyatāṃ pathikāḥ । ataru-ravārir ataḥ param asama-śilā-durgamo mārgaḥ ।। asmin pāpāham ekā katipaya-divasa-proṣita-prāṇa-nāthā pānthāyetthaṃ yuvatyā kathitam abhimataṃ vyāhṛti-vyāja-pūrvam ।।
kuvalaya-dṛśā śūnye daivād atarkita-labdhayā nibhṛta-nibhṛtaṃ ye cumbyante ta eva viduḥ sukham ।। muhur baddhotkampaṃ diśi diśi muhuḥ-preṣita-dṛśor ahalyā-sutrāmṇoḥ kṣaṇikam iva tat-saṃgatam abhūt ।। yogeśvarasya । sā caivāsmi tathāpi tatra surata-vyāpāra-līlā-vidhau revā-rodhasi vetasī-taru-tale cetaḥ samutkaṇṭhate ।।
ekākinī vada kathaṃ na bibheṣi bāle nanv asti puṅkhita-śaro madanaḥ sahāyaḥ ।। itīva duṣṭyā paridevite muhuḥ kuhū kuhūr ity alam āha kokilaḥ ।। adyainaṃ vadarī-nikuñja-kuhare līnam pracaṇḍorage karṣantyā mama tāvad aṅga-likhanair evāpad eṣā gatā ।। tenāśeṣa-janaugha-kalmaṣam uṣā nīlābja-bhāsā sakhi kiṃ kṛṣṇena na yāmunena payasā kṛṣṇānurāgas tava ।।
baddhāsaktir nitambe patati caraṇayor yaḥ sa tādṛk priyo me bāle lajjā praṇaṣṭā na hi na hi kuṭile colakaḥ kiṃ trapā-kṛt ।। āyāsitāsmi sakhi tena divāvasāne mattena kiṃ praṇayinā na hi kesareṇa ।। uttāna-dviguṇāsamañjasa-milaj-jānūdarāstāṃśukastokonmīlad-asañjitoru vayam apy ekākinaḥ kiṃ tv idam ।। svādhīnāmanukūlinīṃ sva-gṛhiṇīm āliṅgya yat supyate tat kiṃ prema gṛhāśrama-vratam idaṃ kaṣṭaṃ samācaryate ।।
lakṣmīdharasya । vadati bahuśo gacchāmīti prayatna-dhṛtāpy aho ramayatitarāṃ saṃketasthā tathāpi hi kāminī ।। durdina-niśītha-pavane niḥsaṃcārāsu nagara-vīthīṣu । patyau videśayāte paraṃ sukhaṃ jaghana-capalāyāḥ ।।
ājānuūddhṛta-nūpurā karatalenācchādya netre bhṛśaṃ kṛcchrāl labdha-paristhitiḥ sva-bhavane panthānam abhyasyati ।। svaṃ saṃketam adūram eva kamitur bhrū-saṃjñayā śaṃsatī siddhiṃ yāti viṭaika-kalpa-latikā raṇḍā na puṇyair vinā ।। paṅgutvena śarīra-jarjaratayā prāyaḥ sa lakṣyākṛtir dṛṣṭo asau bhavatā na kiṃ pathika he sthitvā kṣaṇaṃ kathyatām ।। etāḥ kuntala-mallikā-parimala-vyālola-bhṛṅgāvalījhaṅkārair vikalīkṛtāḥ pathi bata vyaktaṃ kuraṅgī-dṛśaḥ ।।
ataḥ kācit tanvī rati-vidita-saṃketa-gataye gṛhād vāraṃ vāraṃ nirasarad atha prāviśad atha ।। cakorair uḍḍīnair jhaṭiti kṛta-śaṅkāḥ pratipadaṃ parāñcaḥ saṃcārāna-vinayavatīnāṃ vivṛṇute ।। śaśabhṛti vitata-dhāmni dhavalayati dharām avibhāvyatāṃ gatāḥ priya-vasatiṃ vrajanti sukham eva mitho nirasta-bhiyo abhisārikāḥ ।। bāṇasya ।
niśāndhakāre vihitābhisārāḥ sakhīḥ śapantīha nitānta-mugdhā । pathi skhalantī bata vāridhārām āliṅgituṃ vāñchanti vāri-dānām ।। kasmai kupyasi yāvad asmi calitā tāvad vidhi-preritaḥ kāśmīrī-kuca-kumbha-saṃbhrama-haraḥ śītāṃśur abhyudyataḥ ।। kasyacit ।
priyamabhisarasyevaṃ mugdhe samāhataḍiṇḍimā yadi kimadhikatrāsotkampaṃ diśaḥ samudīkṣase ।। madana-huta-bhug-dhūma-cchāyaiḥ paṭair asitair vṛtāḥ prayayur arasad-bhūṣair aṅgaiḥ priyānabhisārikāḥ ।। bhaṭṭa-śiva-svāminaḥ ।। ।।
āśā-cchedini dūti bāndhava-janasyājñāta-pīḍāgame vāpīṃ snātum ito gatāsi na punas tasyādhamasyāntikam ।। kasyacit । savraṇā eva śobhante śūrādhara-payodharāḥ ।। yan mad-arthe virugṇāsi dantair api nakhair api ।।
adharo vīta-rāgas te kaṣāye tava locane ।। pañca pañcanakhā bhakṣyāḥ ṣaṣṭhī tvaṃ yena khāditā ।। sādhu yad durvinītasya tvayā daṇḍo nipātitaḥ ।। dūti virvyājam ākhyātā sarva-vastuṣu śūnyatā ।।
dūti saṃgrāma-yogyāsi na yogyā dūta-karmaṇi ।। śaraṇāgata-vidhvaṃsī chidrānveṣī nipātitaḥ ।। vāg aspṛṣṭā ślathaṃ vāso dūti tvaṃ jvaritāsi kim ।। tvayā prītyānītaṃ sva-nivasana-dānāt punar idaṃ kutas tvādṛg dūti skhalita-śamanopāya-nipuṇā ।।
svedāmbhaḥ-kaṇa-dāyi vepanam idaṃ tyaktvā bhaja svasthatāṃ ko lokasya sakhi svabhāva-kuṭilasyāntargataṃ jñāsyati ।। taṃ labdhvā khalu bandhakīva surata-vyāpāra-dakṣaṃ janaṃ kiṃ dūti jvaritāsi pāpam athavā spṛṣṭvā bhavanty āpadaḥ ।। svedārdraṃ mukham ātapena galitā nīvī gamād āgamād dūti mlāna-saroruha-dyuti-muṣaḥ svauṣṭhasya kiṃ vakṣyasi ।। adhareṇonnati-bhājā bhujaṅga-paripīḍitena te dūti ।
saṃkṣobhitaṃ mano me jalanidhir iva manda-rāgeṇa ।। yenāmbhoruha-saṃnibhasya vadanasyāpāṇḍutā te kṛtā dūti bhraṣṭa-guṇasya tasya nilayaṃ svapne api mā gāḥ punaḥ ।। tvayā phalenaiva vibhāvito ayaṃ mayā sahābhinna-śarīra-vādaḥ ।। vittokasya ।
।। iti dūtikopālambha-vrajyā ।। ।। nidrāṇa-strī-nitambāmbara-haraṇa-raṇan-mekhalārāva-dhāvatkandarpānaddha-bāṇa-vyatikara-taralaṃ kāminaṃ yāminīṣu ।। vamatīva śanair eṣa pradīpaḥ kajjala-cchalāt ।।
kasyacit । ity evam ākalayituṃ sakalaṅka-lajjadudgrīvikām iva dadāti rati-pradīpaḥ ।। kasyacit । vilokya jāmātaram eṣa dīpo vātāyate kampam upaiti bhītaḥ ।।
kasyacit । ।। iti pradīpa-vrajyā ।। ।। cakrāṅkāṇām avirala-jalair ārdra-viśleṣa-bhājāṃ vakṣaḥ-sparśair iva śiśiratāṃ yānti nirvāpyamāṇāḥ ।।
kiṃ brūmahe abhyudayate ca jagat-pidhānaṃ dhvāntaṃ bhavanti ca viśuddha-dṛśo divāndhāḥ ।। paryanteṣu jvalati jaladhau ratnasānau ca madhye citrāṅgīyaṃ ramayati tamaḥ-stoma-līlā dharitrī ।। kiṃ cāmī śalyayantas timiram ubhayato nirbharāhas tamisrāsaṃghaṭṭotpiṣṭa-saṃdhyā-kaṇa-nikara-parispardhino bhānti dīpāḥ ।। upari-bharād ivotsalitayā chaṭayā gaganaṃ prati-nava-saṃdhyayā sapadi saṃvalitaṃ śuśubhe ।।
apy etās tu cikīrṣayeva tapasāṃ tārākṣa-mālā diśo manye khañjana-kaṇṭha-komala-tamaḥ-kṛṣṇājinaṃ bibhrati ।। tāvat saṃtama-sāccha-bhalla-pariṣat-saṃdhyāstram āpīyate kumbha-bhraṃśa-vikīrṇa-mauktika-ruco rājanty amūs tārakāḥ ।। dhvānta-mlānāṃśuka-paricaya-cchanna-lāvaṇya-śocyā dyauḥ pratyagra-dyumaṇi-virahād vāntam akṣṇor na yāti ।। ayaṃ nandī saṃdhyā-samaya-kṛta-kṛtya-vyavasitis tri-netrābhiprāya-pratisadṛśam unmārṣṭi murajān ।।
khedenevānatāsu skhalad-ali-rasanāsv abjinī-preyasīṣu prāyaḥ saṃdhyātapāgniṃ viśati dinapatau dahyate vāsara-śrīḥ ।। vellad-bāhu-latā-viloka-valaya-svānair itaḥ sūcitavyāpārāś ca niyojayanti vividhān varāṅganā varṇakān ।। kakubhi kakubhi prāptāhārāḥ kulāyamahī-ruhāṃ śirasi śirasi svairaṃ svairaṃ patanti patattriṇaḥ ।। kasyacit ।
oṣadhīśaṃ samādāya dhāvatīva pitṛ-prasūḥ ।। tatholūkaḥ stoka-vyapagata-bhayaḥ koṭara-mukhād vapur magna-grīvo ḍamaritaśirāḥ paśyati diśaḥ ।। jihveva sārdra-rudhirāruṇa-sūrya-māṃsagrāsārthinī nabhasi visphurati sma saṃdhyā ।। etaj jagan-nayana-hāri ghanaṃ tamo asya pṛṣṭhe śriyaṃ vitata-kuntalavat tanoti ।।
lalala-bharitam antaḥ kiṃ nu tārkṣyāṇḍa-khaṇḍaṃ janayati hi vitarkān sāndhyam arkasya bimbam ।। māhendrī dig api prasanna-nalinā candrodayākāṅkṣiṇī bhāty eṣā cira-viprayukta-śavarī-gaṇḍāvapāṇḍu-cchaviḥ ।। acalasiṃhasya acala-siṃhasya । atiharita-patra-parikara-saṃpanna-spandanaika-viṭapasya ।
ghana-vāsanair mayūkhaiḥ kusumbha-kusumāyate taraṇiḥ ।। dinamaṇir anargha-mūlyo dina-vaṇijārgha-prasārito jagati । anurūpārgham alabdhvā punar iva ratnākare nihitaḥ ।। kiṃ ca stoka-tamaḥ-kalāpa-kalanā-śyāmāyamānaṃ manāg dhūma-dhyāma-purāṇa-citra-racanā-rūpaṃ jagaj jāyate ।।
valgat-turaṅga-khura-cūrṇita-padma-rāgadhūlīva vāta-valitollasati sma saṃdhyā ।। astādri-śiro-vinihita-ravi-maṇḍala-sarasa-yāva-ghaṭṭāṅkam । nayatīva kāla-kaulaḥ kvāpi nabhaḥ-sairibhaṃ siddhyai ।। tad-anu valanā-mātraṃ kiṃcid vyadhāyi bahir dalair mukulana-vidhau vṛddhābjānāṃ babhūva kadarthanā ।।
nirvāṇāj jala-viprakīrṇa-nivaha-śyāmatvam ātanvate prāg-vipluṣṭa-tamo-guror abhinavās tasyās tamisra-tviṣaḥ ।। astopadhāna-vinihita-ravi-bimba-śiro-nikuñcita-dig-aṅgaḥ । vaste andhakāra-kambalam amara-śayane dinādhvanyaḥ ।। saṃtyajya tārakitam etad iti pravādaṃ vyomāṅgaṇaṃ gaṇaya citritam īśvareṇa ।।
।। ity aparāhṇa-vrajyā ।। ।। kiṃ sāmbhodhikulābalāṃ vasumatīṃ svasmin vidhatte hariḥ saṃkalpān iti māṃsalaṃ vitanute kādambanīlaṃ tamaḥ ।। dhvānte limpati mattakokilavadhūkaṇṭhābhinīle jagad lakṣyante bhavanāni jālavivaroddhāntaiḥ pradīpāṃśubhiḥ ।।
śocyante vayasāṃ gaṇair ita itaḥ paryantacaityadrumāḥ kiṃ cābhyarṇaparākrameṇa tamasā prorṇūyate rodasī ।। vinyastātmapadapramāṇakam idaṃ bhūmītalaṃ jñāyate kiṃ cānyat karasaṃgamaikagamakaḥ svāṅge api saṃpratyayaḥ ।। ghanatamatimiraghuṇotkarajagdhānām iva patanti kāṣṭhānām । chidrair amībhir uḍubhiḥ kiraṇavyājena cūrṇāni ।।
sa-ḍatkārād alpād api nibhṛta-saṃprāpta-ramaṇībhrama-bhrāmyad-bāhur dama-damikayottāmyati yuvā ।। noḥ ।। kālaḥ so api kim asti yatra bhagavān udgamya śīta-dyutir dhvāntaughād bhuvam uddhariṣyati hariḥ pātāla-garbhād iva ।। aṅgeṣv alabdha-paribhoga-sukho andhakāro gṛhṇāti keśa-racanāsu ruṣeva nārīḥ ।।
kasyacit । vātyāsaṃvega-viṣvag-vitata-valayita-sphīta-dhūmyāprakāśaṃ prārambhe api triyāmā taruṇayati nijaṃ nīlimānaṃ vaneṣu ।। ārūḍhasya bhareṇa yauvanam iva dhvāntasya naktaṃ mukhe niryātāḥ kapilāḥ karāla-virala-śmaśrū-prarohā iva ।। tanu-lagnā iva kakubhaḥ kṣmā-valayaṃ caraṇa-cāra-mātram iva ।
viyad iva cālika-daghnaṃ muṣṭi-grāhyaṃ tamaḥ kurute ।। nīlābjaiḥ śekhara-śrī-rasita-vasanatā cety abhīkābhisāre saṃpraty eṇekṣaṇānāṃ timira-bhara-sakhī vartate veśa-līlā ।। ।। ity andhakāra-vrajyā ।। ।।
jyotsnāsatraṃ dadhānaḥ pura-mathana-jaṭājūṭa-koṭīśayālur devaḥ kṣīroda-janmā jayati kumudinī-kāmukaḥ śveta-bhānuḥ ।। ayam udeti kareṇa dig-aṅganāḥ parimṛṣann iva kuṅkuma-kāntinā ।। svaccha-jyotsnāmṛta-rasa-nadī-srotasām eka-śailaḥ so ayaṃ śrīmān udayati śaśī viśva-sāmānya-dīpaḥ ।। etat tarkaya kairava-klama-hare śṛṅgāra-dīkṣā-gurau dikkāntāmukure cakora-suhṛdi prauḍhe tuṣāra-tviṣi ।।
ghana-śroṇī-bimbe nayana-mukule cādhara-dale kapole grīvāyāṃ kuca-kalaśayoś cumbati śaśī ।। śrīkaṇṭhasya । candraḥ sundari dṛśyatām ayam itaś caṇḍīśa-cūḍāmaṇiḥ sadyo-mārjita-dākṣiṇātya-yuvatī-dantāvadāta-dyutiḥ ।। deśāntara-praṇayinor api yatra yūnor nūnaṃ mithaḥ sakhi milanti vilokitāni ।।
rājaśekharasya । nāyaṃ śaśi niviḍa-piṇḍita-bhoga eṣa śeṣo na lāñchanam idaṃ harir eṣa suptaḥ ।। ratānte talpa-sthān harati vanitāpy aṃśukam iva prabhā-mattaś candro jagad idam aho viklavayati ।। bhavati bhaviṣyati kim idaṃ nipatiṣyati bimbam ambarād śaśinaḥ ।
aham api candana-paṅkair aṅkam anaṅkaṃ kariṣyāmi ।। idaṃ tv asya jyotir dara-dalita-karpūra-dhavalaṃ marudbhir bhasmeva prasarati vikīrṇaṃ diśi diśi ।। udgacchaty ayam accha-mauktika-maṇi-prālamba-lambaiḥ karair mugdhānāṃ smara-lekha-vācana-kalā-keli-pradīpaḥ śaśī ।। rājaśekharasya ।
purandhrīṇāṃ preyo-viraha-dahanoddīpita-dṛśāṃ kaṭākṣebhyo bibhyan nibhṛtam iva candro abhyudayate ।। kasyacit । apy usrair dhavalī-bhavatsu giriṣu kṣubdho ayam unmajjatā viśveneva tamo-mayo nidhir apām ahnāya phenāyate ।। pratyudyat-puruhūta-pattana-vadhū-dattārgha-dūrvāṅkurakṣīvotsaṅga-kuraṅgam aindavam idaṃ tad bimbam ujjṛmbhate ।।
mathnanti sthala-sīmni śaila-gahanotsaṅgeṣu saṃrundhate jīva-grāham iva kvacit kvacid api cchāyāsu gṛhṇanti ca ।। kiṃ vā tat-kara-kartarībhir abhito nistakṣaṇād ujjvalaṃ vyomaivedam itas tataś ca patitāś chāyā-chalena tvacaḥ ।। mada-capala-cakora-cañcu-koṭīkavalana-tuccham ivāntarāntar ābhūt ।। samantād unmīlad-bahu-jala-bindustabakino yathā puñjāyante prati-guṇa-kameṇāṅka-maṇayaḥ ।।
murāreḥ । saṃdhyānalena bhṛśam ambara-mūṣikāyām āvartitair uḍubhir eva bhṛto ayam induḥ ।। prācīnād acalād itas tri-jagatām āloka-bījād bahir niryāntaṃ hariṇāṅkam aṅkuram iva draṣṭuṃ jano jīvati ।। antaḥ-prauḍha-kalaṅka-tuccham abhitaḥ sāndraṃ paristīryate bimbād aṅkura-bhagna-naiśika-tamaḥ-saṃdoham indor mahaḥ ।।
śaśinam asūta prācī nṛtyati madano hasanti kakubho api । kumuda-rajaḥ-paṭa-vāsaṃ vikirati gaganāṅgane pavanaḥ ।। dharma-kīrteḥ । anyonyālokanībhiḥ paricaya-janita-prema-nisyandinībhir dūrārūḍhe pramode hasitam iva parispaṣṭam āśā-vadhūbhiḥ ।।
pāṇineḥ ।। udyad-dūratara-prasārita-karaḥ karṣaty asau tat-kṣaṇāt phullat-kairava-kośa-niḥsara-dali-śreṇī-kṛpāṇaṃ śaśī ।। vasukalpasya । śīta-sparśam avāpya saṃprati tathā gupte mukhāmbhoruhe hāseneva kumudvatī-vanitayā vailakṣya-pāṇḍū-kṛtaḥ ।।
vasukalpasya । dinaṃ-manyā rātriś cakita-cakitaṃ kauśika-kulaṃ praphullaṃ nidrāṇaiḥ katham api yathāmbhoruha-vanaiḥ ।। bimbaṃ kaṭhora-visakāṇḍa-kaḍāra-gaurair viṣṇoḥ padaṃ prathamam agrakarair vyanakti ।। aparājita-rakṣitasya ।
kva dhairyaṃ tac cābdher viditam udayādreḥ pratisarasthalī-madhyāsīne śaśini jagad apy ākulam idam ।। aparājitsya । prasarati punar dhvānta-dhvaṃsa-kṣamaḥ kṣaṇadāmukhe sarasa-bisinī-kanda-ccheda-cchavir mṛga-lāñchanaḥ ।। kasyacit ।
kṣīrodāmbhasi majjatīva divasa-vyāpāra-khinnaṃ jagat tat kṣobhāj jala-budbudā iva tarantyālohitās tārakāḥ ।। caturṇām । sphaṭikāla-vāla-lakṣmīṃ pravahati śaśi-bimbam ambarodyāne । kiraṇa-jala-sikta-lāñchana-bāla-tamālaika-viṭapasya ।।
kasyacit । rati-bhara-parikheda-srastarārthaṃ vadhūnāṃ kara-kisalaya-līlā-bhañjana-vyañjikābhiḥ ।। ayam udayācalaika-cūḍāmaṇir abhinava-darpaṇo diśāṃ udayati gagana-sarasi haṃsasya hasann iva vibhramaṃ śaśī ।। bhāti pakṣa-puṭa-gopita-cañcū rāja-haṃsa iva śīta-mayūkhaḥ ।।
parikalita-kalaṅkaḥ stoka-paṅkānulepo nija-kiraṇa-mṛṇālī-mūla-kando ayam induḥ ।। jana-hṛdaya-vibheda-kuṇṭhiteṣor viśikha-niśāta-śileva manmathasya ।। ratnāni lipsur iva dig-bhuvanāntarāle jyotsnā-chalena dhavalo jaladhir jagāha ।। tad ādāya karair indur limpatīva dig-aṅganām ।।
kṣīrāmbhodhi-rasāyanaṃ kamalinī-nidrauṣadhī-pallavo devaḥ kānti-mahā-dhano vijayate dākṣāyaṇī-vallabhaḥ ।। svacchaika-sphaṭikāśma-veśma-jaṭhara-kṣiptām iva kṣmām imāṃ kurvan pārvaṇa-śarvarī-patir asāv uddāmam uddyotate ।। tadānīm etat tu pratinava-tamāla-dyuti-haraṃ tamo api vyālolaṃ vigalati tadīyaṃ nivasanam ।। tathāyaṃ kastūrī-mada-likhita-patrāvali-tulāṃ navāmbhoda-ccheda-cchavir api samārohati mṛgaḥ ।।
śarvasya । tathāyaṃ lāvaṇya-prasara-makaranda-drava-tṛṣāpatad-bhṛṅga-śreṇi-śriyam api kalaṅkaḥ kalayati ।। krama-laṅghita-mugdha-bhāvam indoḥ sphaṭika-ccheda-nibhaṃ vibhāti bimbam ।। bhagīrathasya ।
ambhasi vikasatīva hasatīva sudhādhavaleṣu dhāmasu dhvajapaṭapallaveṣu lalatīva samīracaleṣu candrikā ।। tad anu ca nava-svarṇāmbhoja-prabhaṃ śaśinas tatas taruṇi tagarākāraṃ bimbaṃ vibhāti nabhas-tale ।। kasyacit । dig-yoṣitas tad avalokya kutūhalinyo hrīṇāś ca sa-smitam ivāpasaranti dūram ।।
gobhir navīna-bisa-tantu-vitāna-gaurair āḍhyambhaviṣṇur ayam ambaram āvṛṇoti ।। kasyacit । vinirgataḥ siṃha ivodayācalād gṛhīta-niṣpanda-mṛgo niśākaraḥ ।। ujjaharṣa jhaṣa-ketur avāpuḥ ṣaṭpadāḥ kumuda-bandhana-mokṣam ।।
pāṭita-dhvānta-mātaṅgamuktābhā bhānti tārakāḥ ।। tanvanti vellana-vilāsam ivāmalāsu muktāvalīṣu viśadāḥ śaśino mayūkhāḥ ।। kara-mūla-baddha-pannaga-viṣāgni-dhūma-hata-madhyam । aiśānam iva kapālaṃ sphuṭa-lakṣma sphurati śaśibimbam ।।
himāṃśu-maṇḍale lakṣma nīla-pārāvatāyate ।। unmeyākulaśībhir añjali-puṭair grāhyā mṛṇālāṅkuraiḥ pātavyā ca śaśiny-amugdha-vibhave sā vartate candrikā ।। rājaśekharasya । ye dhārāmbu-viḍambinaḥ kṣaṇam atho ye tāra-hāra-śriyas te amī sphāṭika-daṇḍa-ḍambara-jito jātāḥ sudhāṃśoḥ karāḥ ।।
rājaśekharasya । tad akṣaṇaḥ sīmneyaṃ yad-urasi manāg añjana-mayī mṛga-cchāyā daivād aghaṭi na kalaṅkaḥ punar ayam ।। yāminyās tilakaḥ kalā mṛga-dṛśāṃ prema-vrataikāśramaḥ krāmaty eṣa cakorayācaka-mahaḥ-karpūra-varṣaḥ śaśī ।। etasminn udayāsta-bhūdhara-taru-dvandvāntarāle tatair ebhir bhāti gabhasti-tantu-paṭalaiḥ śvetorṇa-nābhaḥ śaśī ।।
।। iti candra-vrajyā ।। ।। kiṃ cāyaṃ rajanī-patiḥ pravigalal-lāvaṇya-lakṣmīr itaḥ paryanta-sthita-cāru-vṛtta-kaṭhinī-khaṇḍa-cchaviṃ vāñchati ।। sarojānāṃ karṣann ali-mayam ayaskānta-maṇivatd kṣaṇād antaḥ-śalyaṃ tapati patir adyāpi na rucām ।।
lūtātantu-vitāna-vartulam ito bimbaṃ dadhac cumbati prātaḥ proṣita-rocir ambara-talād astācalaṃ candramāḥ ।। sūkṣmocchvāsam apīdam utsukatayā saṃbhūya koṣād bahir niṣkrāmad-bhramaraugha-saṃbhrama-bharād ambhojam ujjṛmbhate ।। bhūyo api kramaśaḥ prasārayati tāḥ saṃpraty amūn udyataḥ saṃkhyātuṃ sakutūhaleva nalinī bhānoḥ sahasraṃ karān ।। niryan-madhuvrata-kadamba-miṣād vamanti bibhranti kāraṇa-guṇān iva mauktikāni ।।
। tatra stambhita-pārada-drava-jaḍo jātaḥ prage candramāḥ paurastyaṃ ca purāṇa-sīdhu-madhura-cchāyaṃ nabho vartate ।। yāto astācala-cūlam udvasa-madhu-cchatra-cchaviś candramāḥ prācī bāla-biḍālalocanarucāṃ yātā ca pātraṃ kakup ।। pārāvāra-gataiś ca koka-mithunair ānandato gadgadaṃ sākūtaṃ rutam eva kintu bahalaṃ sātkṛtya noḍḍīyate ।।
kasyacit । na yāvad udayācaloddhata-rajāḥ samākrāmati prabhā-paṭala-pāṭalī-kṛta-nabho antarālo raviḥ ।। hā kaṣṭaṃ timira-tviṣo vayam api vyaktaṃ hatā ity amī kākāḥ saṃprati ghoṣayanti sabhayāḥ kāketi nāmnātmanaḥ ।। dhvāntaṃ harann amara-nāyaka-pālitāyāṃ devo abhyudeti diśi vāsara-bīja-koṣaḥ ।।
viṣṇu-hareḥ । kuntala ivāvaśiṣṭaḥ smarasya candana-saro-nimagnasya । pratibhāti yatra hariṇaḥ sa hariṇa-lakṣmā gato asta-mayam ।। prabhraṃśi-sthūla-muktāphala-nikara-parispardhitārāśru-binduḥ pronmīlat-pūrva-saṃdhyāhuta-bhuji rajanī paśya dehaṃ juhoti ।।
kasyacit । ity ākalayya niyataṃ śaśabhṛt samastam astād dadau jhagiti jhampa-mayaṃ payodhau ।। pratyāsannatarodaya-stha-taraṇer bimbāruṇimnā tato mañjiṣṭhā-rasa-lohinī dig api ca prācī samunmīlati ।। śrayati śithila-cchāyābhogas taṭīm aparāmbudher jaraṭha-lavalī-lāvaṇyāccha-cchavir mṛga-lāñchanaḥ ।।
śarvasya । kuruṇṭaka-vipāṇḍuraṃ dadhati dhāma dīpāṅkurāśḥ cakora-nayanāruṇā bhavati dic ca sautrāmaṇī ।। sajjad-dānodaka-tanu-malo jarjarābhīṣu-rajjur bhraśyaty eṣa praśithila iva śrotra-śaṅkhaḥ śaśāṅkaḥ ।। sadyo mādyan-makara-kamaṭha-sthūla-matsyā ivaite yānty antasthāḥ kulaśikhariṇo vyakti-vartma krameṇa ।।
kasyacit । bhrāntyādaṣṭa-sphuṭa-bisalatā-cuñcubhiś cañcu-cakraiś cakrā bandīkṛta-viraha-kṛc-candralekhā ivaite ।। gaganodadhi-paścimānta-lagno vidhur uttāna ivāsti kūrma-rājaḥ ।। śatānandasya ।
viraha-vidhura-koka-dvandva-bandhur vibhindan kupitakapi-kapola-kroḍa-tāmras-tamāṃsi ।। yogeśvarasya । gīyante nagareṣu nāgara-jana-pratyūṣa-nidrānudo rādhā-mādhavayoḥ paraspara-rahaḥ-prastāvanā-gītayaḥ ।। ।। iti pratyūṣa-vrajyā ।।
।। utsaṅga-ślatha-mukta-hasta-yugala-nyastānanaḥ kānane jhillī-toya-kaṇābhiṣeka-sukhito nidrāyate vānaraḥ ।। kiṃ cānyat-paritapta-dhūli-luṭhana-ploṣāsahatvād iva cchāyā dūra-gatāpi bhūruha-tale vyāvartya saṃlīyate ।। malaya-rājasya ।
utsaṅgāntara-vartinām anugamāt saṃpīḍitā gām imāṃ sarvāṅga-praṇaya-priyām iva taru-cchāyā samālambate ।। gajapati-mukhodgīrṇair āpyair api trasareṇubhiḥ śiśira-madhurām eṇāḥ kaccha-sthalīm adhiśerate ।। bhaumoṣma-plavamāna-sūra-kiraṇa-krūra-prakāśā dṛśor āyuḥ karma samāpayanti dhig amūr madhye ahni śūnyā diśaḥ ।। murārer etau murāreḥ ।etau
adhyetṝṇāṃ dadhānaṃ bhṛśam ala-sadṛśāṃ kiṃcid aṅgāvasādaṃ devasyaitat samantād bhavatu samucita-śreyase madhyam ahnaḥ ।। dātyūhais tiniśasya koṭaravati skandhe nilīya sthitaṃ vīrun-nīḍa-kapota-kūjitam anukrandanty adhaḥ kukkubhāḥ ।। kiṃ caitad-danujādhirāja-yuvatī-vargāvagāhotsaratkṣobhoḍḍīna-vihaṅga-maṇḍala-kṛtālīkātapatraṃ saraḥ ।। mithyā leḍhi mṛṇāla-koṭi-rabhasād daṃṣṭrāṅkuraṃ śūkaro madhyāhne mahiṣaś ca vāñchati nija-cchāyā-mahā-kardamam ।।
kasyacit । gabhīre tan nābhī-kuhara-pariṇāhe adhvani sakṛt kuhuṅkāra-sphāraṃ racayati ca nādaṃ namati ca ।। megha-cchāya-dhiyābhidhāvati puro nirdagdha-dūrvāvanaṃ pānthaḥ kiṃ ca marīci-vīciṣu payaḥ-pūra-bhramaḥ klāmati ।। tallāmbho vana-tāmasolla-nivahasyāśakta-sūrya-srutivrāta-sphīta-varāhasairi-bhasa-bhāsva-sthaiṇa-yūthāc cyutam ।।
utsarpad-dava-dhūma-vibhrama-bharaḥ kiṃ ca pratīcīr apaḥ kurvanty accha-marīci-vīci-nicaya-bhrāntyā hradānte mṛgāḥ ।। līlā-tāṇḍava-ḍambarair avakiran pānīya-pūrṇodarasḥ tuṇḍāgrāt kṣaṇa-pīta-vāri-guḍikām udgīrya saṃlīyate ।। ।। tad yācemahi sapta-piṣṭapa-śucībhāvaikatāna-vrataṃ saṃyaccha svayaśaḥ sitāsita-payo-bhedād viveko astu naḥ ।।
kasyacit । deśe deśe vipaṇiṣu tathā catvare pāna-goṣṭhyām unmatteva bhramati bhavato vallabhā hanta kīrtiḥ ।। tutātitasya । karṇātī-sita-danta-patra-mahaso apy atyantam uddyotinī kīrtis te bhuja-vīrya-nirjita-ripor loka-trayaṃ bhrāmyati ।।
vārtika-kārasya । amī pānaka-raṅkābhāḥ saptāpi jala-rāśayaḥ ।। yenānarghatayā ca sundaratayā cedaṃ yaśobhis tava spardhām etya virājate nanu pariṇāmo adbhuto bhautikaḥ ।। utkīrṇaṃ kuśalaiḥ praśastiṣu sadā gītaṃ ca nākeṣadāṃ dārer ujjayinī-bhujaṅga bhavataś candrāvadātaṃ yaśaḥ ।।
kasyacit । nītāḥ karkatvam arka-pravahaṇa-harayo hāritotsaṅga-lakṣmā rājann uddāma-gaurair ajani ca rajanī-vallabhas tvad-yaśo bhoḥ ।। rājann idaṃ bahula-pakṣa-dalan-mṛgāṅkacchedojjvalais tava yaśobhir aśobhi viśvam ।। kṣemaṃ me anyad yugāntāvadhi tapatu bhavān yad-yaśo-ghoṣaṇābhiḥ devo nidrā-daridraḥ saphalayati harir yauvana-rddhiṃ mameti ।।
pratāpāya jagannātha yātā mārtaṇḍa-maṇḍalam ।। vāg yātā caturānanasya vadanaṃ lakṣmīr murārer uraḥ kāntir maṇḍalam aindavaṃ mama punar nādyāpi viśrāma-bhūḥ ।। kasyacit । śeṣo mūlaṃ prakāṇḍaṃ hima-girir udadhir dugdha-pūrālavālaṃ jyotsnā śākhā-pratānaḥ kusumam uḍu-cayo yasya candraḥ phalaṃ ca ।।
kasyacit । gītā-karṇana-moda-mukta-yavasa-grāsābhilāṣo vada svāminn aṅka-mṛgaḥ kiyanti hi dināny etasya vartiṣyate ।। । samayasulabhāṃ kīrtiṃ bhavyām asūta sutām asāv api ramayituṃ rāgāndheva bhramaty akhilaṃ jagat ।।
hārāvalī-hariṇa-lakṣma-harāṭṭa-hāsaheramba-danta-hari-śaṅkha-nibhaṃ yaśas te ।। kiṃ tv ekaḥ param asti dūṣaṇa-kaṇo yan nopayāti bhramāt kṛṣṇaṃ śrīḥ śiti-kaṇṭham adri-tanayā nīlāmbaraṃ revatī ।। nīlotpalāni kumudanti ca sarva-śailāḥ kailāsituṃ vyavasitā bhavato yaśobhiḥ ।। ekākiny api setu-bandha-rahitān saptāpi vārāṃ nidhīn helābhis tava deva kīrti-vanitā yasmāt samullaṅghati ।।
tasyaiva । yad udbhūtenedaṃ nava-visalatā-tantu-śucinā yaśo-nrimokeṇa sthagitam avanī-maṇḍalam abhūt ।। saṅgha-śriyaḥ । tvat-kīrtayo gagana-dig-valayaṃ tad-antaḥpiṇḍībhavan-niviḍa-mūrti-paramparābhiḥ ।।
yad ari-rudhiraṃ pāyaṃ pāyaṃ kusumbha-rasāruṇaṃ jhagiti vamati kṣīrāmbhodhi-pravāhasitaṃ yaśaḥ ।। dakṣasya । yuṣmābhis tribhir ebhir arpita-tanus tvat-kīrtir ujjṛmbhiṇī māṇikya-stavaka-traya-praṇayinīṃ hārasya dhatte śriyam ।। dig-vadhūnāṃ mukhe jātam akasmād ardha-kuṅkumam ।।
adyāpy urvī-valaya-tilaka śyāmalimnāvaliptāny ābhāsante vada dhavalitaṃ kiṃ yaśobhis tvadīyaiḥ ।। ।। ।। tato anyāpadeśa-vrajyā ।। kim atraivātmānaṃ jarayasi mudhā śukti-kuhare mahā-gambhīro ayaṃ jaladhir iha kas tvāṃ gaṇayati ।।
murāreḥ । śambūko api yad atra durlabhatarair ratnair anarghaiḥ saha spardhām eka-nivāsa-kāraṇa-vaśād ekāntato vāñchati ।। kiṃ tena nīra-nidhinā mahatā taṭe api yasyormayaḥ prakupitā galahastayanti ।। martye asya grahaṇaṃ kva darśana-sudhāpy unmukta-netra-śriyāṃ svar-loke api lavaḥ śaveśvara-jaṭā-jūṭaika-cūḍāmaṇiḥ ।।
yasmin vitta-vyaya-bhara-saho grāhakas tāvad āstāṃ nāsti bhrātar marakata-maṇe tvat-parīkṣākṣamo api ।। kasyacit । hā kaṣṭaṃ phala-lolupair apasṛtaṃ śākhāmṛgaiś cañcalair ekenaiva davānala-vyatikaraḥ soḍhaḥ paraṃ śākhinā ।। kasyacit ।
ka evaṃ jānīte nija-kara-puṭī-koṭara-gataṃ kṣaṇādenaṃ tāmyat-timi-makaram āpāsyati muniḥ ।। kavinandasya । apy asmād avatāra eva bhavato nonmāda-bherī-ravaḥ samyaṅ mūrchiti-kelayaḥ punar ime bhṛṅga dvir abhyāhatiḥ ।। jetavyo asti hareḥ sa lāñchanam ato vandāmahe tām abhūd yad-garbhe śarabhaḥ svayaṃjaya iti śrutvāpi yo nāṅkitaḥ ।।
antaḥ prastara-saṃgraho bahir api bhraśyanti gandha-drumā bhrātaḥ śoṇa na so asti yo na hasati tvat-saṃpadāṃ viplave ।। kasyacit । aye paśyāvasthām akaruṇa-samīra-vyatikarasphurad-dāva-jvālāvali-jaṭila-mūrter viṭapinaḥ ।। kasyacit ।
etat tv adṛṣṭa-caram aśruta-vārtam etāḥ śākhā-tvaco api tanu-kāṇḍa-samās tyajanti ।। kathāpi śrotavyā bhavati hata-ketor na ca punar janānāṃ dhvaṃsāya prabhavati hi yasyodgatir api ।। apaśyat kāsāra-śriyam amṛta-varti-praṇayinīṃ sukhaṃ jīvaty andhūdaravivaravarti plava-kulam ।। kuto api nāśrāvi yad atra pallyāṃ pallīpatir yāvad aviddha-karṇaḥ ।।
daivāt kaṣṭa-daśā-vaśaṃ gatavataḥ siṃhasya tasyādhunā karṣaty eṣa kareṇa keśara-saṭābhāraṃ jarat-kuñjaraḥ ।। ālasyād avimuñcatā giri-guhāṃ siṃhena nidrālunā sarvaṃ viśva-jayaika-sādhanam idaṃ labdhaṃ na kiṃcit kṛtam ।। kasyacit । anyaiva sā sthitir aho malaya-drumasya yad gandha-mātram api tāpam apākaroti ।।
tatrātīndriya-modi-māṃsala-rasodgāras tavaiṣa dhvanir doṣo abhūt kalakaṇṭha-nāyaka nijas teṣāṃ svabhāvo hi saḥ ।। yat tvan-mūla-niṣaṇṇa-svinna-pathika-stomaḥ stuvann anv aho na svādūni mṛdūni khādati phalāny ākaṇṭham utkaṇṭhitaḥ ।। kasyacit । kiṃ tv etasminn aśani-piśunair ātapair ākulānām adhvanyānām aśaraṇa-maru-prāntare ko abhyupāyaḥ ।।
gadādharasya । vyādhāḥ padāny anusaranti gṛhīta-cāpāḥ kaṃ deśam āśrayatu yūthapatir mṛgāṇām ।। kṣārīkṛtaṃ ca vaḍavā-dahane hutaṃ ca pātāla-kukṣi-kuhare viniveśitaṃ ca ।। nāmany anta tadātanīm api nija-cchāyākṣitiṃ taiḥ punas teṣām eva tale kṛtajña-caritaiḥ śuṣyadbhir apy āsyate ।।
kasyacit । gate daivād śoṣaṃ vara-sarasi tatraiva taralā baka-grāsa-trāsād viśati śapharī paṅkam adhunā ।। kasyacit । dhik tat sarvaṃ tava jalanidhe yad vimucyāśru-dhārās tīre nīra-grahaṇa-vimukhair adhvagair ujjhito asi ।।
kasyacit । ity antaḥ-sva-kuṭumba-durnaya-parāmarśāgninā dahyate bāḍhaṃ vāḍava-nāmadheya-dahana-vyājena vārāṃ nidhiḥ ।। kasyacit । dṛpyad-durdama-gandha-sindhura-jayotkhāto api kāmaṃ stutiḥ smero ayaṃ śarabhaḥ parāṃ hṛdi ghṛṇām āyāti jāti-smaraḥ ।।
kasyacit । āho śuṣyati daiva-dṛṣṭi-valanād ambhobhir ambho-mucaḥ saṃbhūyāpi vidhātum asya rajasi staimityam apy akṣamāḥ ।। kasyacit । āho kṣobhaṃ vrajeyuḥ kvacid api samaye daiva-yogāt tadānīṃ na kṣoṇī nādri-vargā na ca ravi-śaśinau sarvam ekārṇavaṃ syāt ।।
kasyacit । puro naḥ saṃprāptās taṭa-bhuvi salipsaṃ tu vasatām udagrāḥ kallolāḥ sphuṭa-vikaṭa-daṃṣṭrāś ca makarāḥ ।। antas te yadi koṭarodara-calad-vyālāvalī-visphuradvaktodvānta-viṣānalātibhayadaṃ vandyas tadānīṃ bhavān ।। kasyacit ।
dhruvam itarathā draṣṭavyo asi svajāti-vilakṣaṇadhvanita-kupita-dhvāṅkṣa-troṭī-puṭāhati-jarjaraḥ ।। kasyacit । siṃho apy alaṅghya-mahimā harinām adheyaṃ dhatte jarat-kapir apīti kim atra vācyam ।। kva ca khara-śilā-paṭṭe ghṛṣṭiḥ kva paṅka-sarūpatā malayaja sakhe mā gāḥ khedaṃ guṇās tava dūṣaṇam ।।
kasyacit । sariti sarasi sindhau cātakenārpito asāv api vahala-pipāsā-pāṃśulaḥ kaṇṭha-nālaḥ ।। lakṣmīdharasya । gāmbhīryaṃ kim ayaṃ jahāti kim ayaṃ puṣṇāti nāmbhodharān maryādāṃ kim ayaṃ bhinatti kim ayaṃ na trāyate vāḍavam ।।
kasyacit । tasmād durgam aśṛṅgala ghana-kalā-durlālitātman vraja tvad-vāsāya sa eva kīrṇa-kanaka-jyotsno girīṇāṃ patiḥ ।। athāśāḥ pūrayann eva kiṃ meghair vyavadhīyate ।। saṃśliṣṭāṅguli-randhra-līna-makara-grāhāvalir nīravo yair nāyaṃ kara-śuktikodara-laghur dṛṣṭo muner añjalau ।।
abhinandasya । tasminn eva sarasy akāla-jaladenāgatya tac ceṣṭitaṃ yenākumbha-nimagna-vanya-kariṇāṃ yūthaiḥ payaḥ pīyate ।। dvandūkasya । evaṃ kartum ahaṃ samartha iti ced dhiṅ mūrkha kiṃ sarvato nālaṃ plāvayituṃ jagaj-jala-nidhir dhairyam yad ālambate ।।
kasyacit । kiṃ cānyat-phala-bhoga-kṛṣṭa-mukharās tvām āśritāḥ patriṇo yat-puṃskokila-kūjitaṃ vidadhate tan nānurūpaṃ param ।। kasyacit । ekas tatra sa kaścid aṅkura-varo badhnāti tām unnatiṃ yām adhyan yajanaḥ svamātaram iva klānti-cchide dhāvati ।।
śālikanāthasya । śālmalyāḥ paripāka-kāla-kalanā-rodhena kīraḥ sthito yāvat tat-puṭa-sandhi-nirgata-patat-tūlaṃ phalāt paśyati ।। śālika-nāthasya । tatrāpy arṇasi varṇanā sphurati me yat-saṃgatau vardhate dugdhaṃ yena puraiva cāsya suhṛdaḥ kvāthe svayaṃ kṣīyate ।।
naivāyaṃ sa imaṃ nṛjaḥ sa iva vā naivaiṣa doṣākaraḥ ko ayaṃ bhoḥ śaśinīva locanavatām arke kalaṅkaḥ samaḥ ।। āyānti yānti satataṃ nīraṃ śiśiraṃ kharaṃ na gaṇayanti । vidmo na hanta divasāḥ kasya kim ete kariṣyanti ।। yad atraiva brahmā pibati nijam āyur madhu punar vilumpanti svedādhikam amṛta-hṛdyaṃ madhulihaḥ ।।
idānīm astādriṃ śrayati galitāloka-vibhavaḥ piśācā valgantu sthagayatu tamisraṃ ca kakubhaḥ ।। itas tu kṣārābdher jaraṭha-makara-kṣuṇṇa-payaso nivṛttiḥ kalyāṇī na punar avatāraḥ katham api ।। svabhāvād garvād vā na pibati payas tasya śakunaiḥ kim etenoccais tvaṃ bhavati laghimā vāpi sarasaḥ ।। kasyacit ।
asaṃjñāḥ khalv ete jala-śikhi-maruddhūsa-nicayāḥ prakṛtyā garjanti tvayi tu bhuvanaṃ nirmadam idam ।। amara-siṃhasya । tadā jānīmas te karivara balodgāram asamaṃ saṭāṃ suptasyāpi spṛśasi yadi pañcānana-śiśoḥ ।। nārāyaṇasya ।
avaśyaṃ ko api tvad-guṇa-paricayākṛṣṭa-hṛdayo narendras tvāṃ kuryān mukuṭa-makarī-cumbita-rucim ।। kasyacit । kusumbhe viśrambhaṃ yad iha bhajase kaṇṭaka-śatair asaṃdigdhaṃ dagdha-bhramara bhavitāsi kṣata-vapuḥ ।। etāvat tu vyathayati yadāloka-bāhyais tamobhis tasmin eva prakṛti-mahati vyomni labdho avakāśaḥ ।।
sūte vātaṃ javanam aparas tena jānīhi tāvat kiṃ vyādatse vihaga vadanaṃ tatra tatrāmbuvāhe ।। nūnaṃ prāvṛt-samaya-kaluṣair ūrmibhis tāla-tuṅgair adya śvo vā sarid akaruṇā tvāṃ śriyā pātayitrī ।। paśyāmaḥ kiṃ subhaga bhavataḥ krīḍati kroḍa eva vyāḍas tubhyaṃ bhavatu kuśalaṃ muñca naḥ sādhayāmaḥ ।। iha sarasi manojñe saṃtataṃ pātum ambhaḥ śrama-paribhava-magnāḥ ke na magnāḥ karīndrāḥ ।।
jaladhara-jala-dhārā dūratas tāvad āstāṃ dhvanir api madhuras te na śrutaś cātakena ।। acala-siṃhasya । kim asi nitarām uktṣubhormiḥ prasīda namo astu te pathi pathi śivāḥ santy asmākaṃ śataṃ kamalākarāḥ ।। acalasya ।
upacitaraso dāhe cchede śilātalagharṣaṇe apy adhikam adhikaṃ yat saurabhyaṃ tanoti manoharam ।। visahati garutaṃ rutaṃ vidhatte jala-pṛṣate kiyate api cātako ayam ।। baddho asi viddhi tāvan madhu-rasana vyasanam īdṛg etad iti । anavahita-kamala-mīlana madhukara kiṃ viphalam utphalasi ।।
hṛtvāpi vasu-sarvasvam amī te jaladāḥ sakhi । mitrāpy apakurvanti vipriyāṇāṃ tu kā kathā ।। hasaty ullasati preṅkhaty adhastād īkṣate janam ।। śākhoṭakasya punar asya mahāśayo ayam ambhoda eva śaraṇaṃ yadi nirguṇasya ।।
prācīna-karma-paratantra-nija-pravṛtter etasya paśya vihagasya gatis tvam eva ।। kasyacit । saṃpraty upoḍha-mada-manthara-bāhu-daṇḍakaṇḍūyanāvasara eva surāsurāṇām ।। unmūlito api marutā bata vāri-durgamārge yad atra jana-saṃkramatām upetaḥ ।।
kasyacit । itthaṃ na kiṃcid api cāru mṛgādhipasya tejas tu tat kim api yena jagad-varākam ।। kasyacit । kasya tṛṣaṃ na kṣapayasi na payasi tava kathaya ke nimajjanti ।
yadi san-mārga-jalāśaya nakro na kroḍam adhivasati ।। na sphūrjati na ca garjati na ca karakāḥ kirati sṛjati na ca taḍitaḥ । na ca vinimuñcati vātyāṃ varṣati nibhṛtaṃ mahā-meghaḥ ।। na bhavatu kathaṃ kadambaḥ pratipratīka-prarūḍha-ghana-pulakaḥ ।
viśvaṃ dhinoti jaladaḥ pratyupakāra-spṛhā-rahitaḥ ।। na kevalam anenātmā divaso api laghūkṛtaḥ ।। dahyamānāny api snehavyaktiṃ kṛtvā sphuṭanti yat ।। pūrvārjitāśubha-vaśīkṛta-pauruṣasya kalpa-drumo api na samīhitam ātanoti ।।
nānā-nadīnada-śatāni ca pūrayitvā rikto asi yaj jalada saiva tavonnatā śrīḥ ।। kasyacit । etāḥ saṃnidhi-mātra-kalpita-puraskārās tu dhanyās tvaco yāsāṃ chedanam antareṇa patito nāyaṃ kuṭhāras tvayi ।। vittokasya ।
saudāminībhir asakṛd yadi haṃsi cakṣur nānyā gatis tad api vārida cātakasya ।। hā kaṣṭa miṣṭa-phaladāna-vidhāna-hetor ambhodharāt patati saṃprati vajrapātaḥ ।। laḍaha-candrasya । tasyaivāstam upeyuṣaḥ kara-śatāny ādāya vidhvaṃsayann eṣa tvāṃ kalitaḥ kalābhir udayaty agre śaśī pārvaṇaḥ ।।
ākrīḍan nimiṣaṃ sa naiti phalitaṃ yat tvāṃ vikaśaika-mut tad-dharmo asya phalāśayā paricayaḥ kalpa-drume apy asti kim ।। vallabhasya । snigdhaṃ pallavito ghanaṃ mukulitaḥ sphāra-cchaṭaṃ puṣpitaḥ sotkarṣaṃ phalito bhṛśaṃ ca vinataḥ ko apy eṣa cūta-drumaḥ ।। kasyacit ।
ākalpaṃ dharaṇī-dharodvahanataḥ saṃkoca-khinnātmano yaḥ kūrmasya dināni nāma katicid viśrāma-dāna-kṣamaḥ ।। hanūmataḥ । parakīyair aparathā katham ākṛṣyase guṇaiḥ ।। bhagavati yāmini vande tvayi bhuvi dṛṣṭaḥ pativratā-dharmaḥ ।
gatavati rajanī-nāthe kajjala-malinaṃ vapur vahasi ।। yad etasyaivāgre kavalita-tanur dāva-dahanair na tīrāraṇyānī salila-culukenāpy upakṛtā ।। kaṇikākārasya । āśvāsanaṃ yad avakṛṣṭam abhūn maharṣe toyaṃ tvayā tad api niṣkaruṇena pītam ।।
katipaya-divasa-sthāyini mada-kāriṇi yauvane durātmānaḥ । vidadhati tathāparādhaṃ janmaiva yathā vṛthā bhavati ।। kasyacit । tathāpy āsāṃ tais tais tarubhir abhitas tīra-patitaiḥ sa evāgre buddhau pariṇamati ruddho apy avinayaḥ ।।
śabdārṇavasya । satataṃ yā madhyasthā prathayati yaṣṭiḥ pratiṣṭhitāsīti । puṣkariṇi kim idam ucitaṃ tāṃ cedānīm adho nayasi ।। kṛtam idam asādhu hariṇaiḥ śirasi tarūṇāṃ davānale jvalati ।
ājanma keli-bhavanaṃ yad bhītair ujjhitaṃ vipinam ।। bhasmīkṛtya sa-puṣpa-pallava-phalāṃs tāṃs tān mahā-pādapān nirvṛttena davānalena vihitaṃ valmīka-śeṣaṃ vanam ।। smartavyatām upagateṣu saroruheṣu dhik jīvita-vyasanam asya malīmasasya ।। saṃbhāvyate api kim idaṃ nu yathendukāntās te pāvanaṃ ca śiśiraṃ ca rasaṃ sṛjanti ।।
dāha-ccheda-nikāṣair ati pariśuddhasya te vṛthā garimā । yad asi tulām adhirūḍhaṃ kāṃcana guñjāphalaiḥ sārdham ।। surabheḥ । dagdhaḥ kiṃ vā na bhavati masī ceti saṃdehinībhiḥ śāmbūkābhiḥ saha paricito nīyate pāmarībhiḥ ।।
sucaritasya । chidraṃ maṇer guṇārthaṃ nāyaka-pada-hetur asya tāralyam । katham anyatheśvarāṇāṃ viluṭhati hṛdaye ca maulau ca ।। anavadhi-kaṭhinatvaṃ nārikerasya yasmin vaśika-hṛdaya-vṛtter lupta-sāra-śriyaś ca ।।
kiṃpāka pāke bahir eva rakta tiktāsitāntar dṛśi kāntim eṣi । etāvatā kākam apāsya kasya hṛt-prīti-bhittis tvam idaṃ na jāne ।। dṛśaṃ merau dadyāḥ sa hi maṇimaya-prastha-mahito mahā-maunaḥ sthairyād atha bhuvanam eva sthirayati ।। kasyacit ।
mainākādi-mahīdhra-labdha-vasatiṃ yaḥ pītavān ambudhiṃ tasya tvāṃ gilataḥ kapola-milana-kleśo api kiṃ jāyate ।। kasyacit । danta-stambha-niṣaṇṇa-niḥsaha-karaḥ śvāsair atiprāṃśubhir yenāyaṃ virahī tu vāraṇa-patiḥ svāmin sa vindhyo bhavān ।। ।। ity anyāpadeśa-vrajyā ।।
।। dūrottāna-taraṅga-laṅghana-jalā-jaṅghāla-garva-spṛśaḥ karpūra-drava-śīkarair iva diśo limpanti pampānilāḥ ।। jighrantaḥ siṃhalīnāṃ mukha-kamala-malaṃ keralīnāṃ kapolaṃ cumbanto vānti mandaṃ malaya-parimalā vāyavo dākṣiṇātyāḥ ।। punas tat-saṅga-śaṅkīva vāti vātaḥ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।।
revā-śīkara-dhāriṇo andhra-murala-strī-māna-mudrābhidoaḥ vātā vānti navīna-kokila-vadhū-hūṅkāra-vācālitāḥ ।। priya-premākarṣa-cyuta-racanam āmūla-saralaṃ lalāṭe lāṭīnāṃ luṭhitam alakaṃ tāṇḍavayati ।। vitarati ghana-sārāmodam antar-dhunāno jaladhi-jala-taraṅgān khelayan gandha-vāhaḥ ।। sa-gandha-sārādi-kṛtāṅga-bhūṣaṇaḥ prayāty udīcīṃ dayitām ivānilaḥ ।।
svairaṃ dakṣiṇa-sindhu-kūla-kadalī-kacchopakaṇṭhodbhavaḥ kāverī-taṭa-tāḍi-tāḍana-taṭatkārottaro mārutaḥ ।। aṅgaṃ vihvalayan mano vikalayan mānaṃ samunmūlayan nārīṇāṃ malayānilaḥ priya iva pratyaṅgam āliṅgati ।। vanānām ābhoge kusumavati puṣpoccaya-paro marun mandaṃ mandaṃ vicarati parivrājaka iva ।। suptaṃ saṃprati bodhayanti śanakaiś ceto-bhuvaṃ kāmināṃ pratyagra-sphuṭa-mallikā-surabhayaḥ sāyanṃtanā vāyavaḥ ।।
prāyaḥ praślathayanti puṣpa-dhanuṣaḥ puṣpākare niṣṭhite nirvedaṃ nava-mallikā-surabhayaḥ sāyaṃ nayā vāyavaḥ ।। manasijaḥ praviveśa viyoginīhṛdayam āhita-śoka-hutāśanaḥ ।। mandaṃ mandaṃ nipatati cirād āgato mādhavīṣu vyākurvāṇo bhayam iva paraṃ dākṣiṇo gandhavāhaḥ ।। amī mandaṃ mandaṃ surata-samara-śrānta-taruṇīlalāṭa-svedāmbhaḥ-kaṇa-parimuṣo vānti marutaḥ ।।
surata-bhara-khinna-pannaga-vilāsinī-pāna-keli-jarjaritaḥ । punar iha virahi-śvāsair malaya-marun māṃsalī-bhavati ।। vānti svairaṃ sarasi sarasi kroḍa-daṃṣṭrā-vimardatruṭyad-gundrā-parimala-guṇa-grāhiṇo gandhavāhāḥ ।। sevyante nitya-mādyat-kari-kāṭhina-karā-sphāla-kāla-prabuddhakrudhyat-pañcānanāgra-dhvani-bhara-vigalad-guggulūdgāra-garbhāḥ ।।
amī svairaṃ svairaṃ malaya-maruto vānti dinajaṃ dināpāye cakṣuḥ-klamam apaharanto mṛgadṛśām ।। sruta-malayaja-vṛkṣa-kṣīra-saurabhya-sabhyo vahati sakhi bhujaṅgī-bhukta-śesaḥ samīraḥ ।। kasyacit । te kaṇṭhe loṭhayantaḥ para-bhṛta-vayasāṃ pañcamaṃ rāga-rājaṃ vānti svairaṃ samīrāḥ smara-vijaya-mahā-sākṣiṇo dākṣiṇātyāḥ ।।
rājaśekharasya । vibhindann udyānāny atanu-makaranda-drava-hara śrama-svairo vāyur manasija-śarair jarjarayati ।। ete saṃvasathopakaṇṭha-vilasad-vṛṣṭy-ambu-vīcī-cayonmīlad-bāla-tuṣāra-śīkara-kirau krīḍanti jhañjhānilāḥ ।। ।।
।। anirvāṇotthena prabalatara-tailākta-tanavo mayā sadyo bhṛṣṭāḥ katipaya-kavayyaḥ kavalitāḥ ।। śaṣpair ardhāvalīḍhaiḥ śrama-vivṛta-mukha-bhraṃśibhiḥ kīrṇa-vartmā paśyodagra-plutatvād viyati bahutaraṃ stokam urvyāṃ prayāti ।। kālidāsasya ।
tīvrādhaḥ-pāta-puñjī-kṛta-vitata-calat-pakṣa-pālī-viśālaś cillaś cāṇḍāla-pallī-piṭhara-jaṭharataḥ proddharaty ardha-dagdham ।। anyonyākṣamiṇaḥ śarāri-śiśavaḥ prātar nadī-rodhasi prāleyāmbu pibanti vīraṇa-dala-droṇī praṇālī-srutam ।। kasyacit । tiryag-vistṛta-pīvaroru-yugalā pṛṣṭhān ativyākṛtābhoga-śroṇir udasyati pratimuhuḥ kūpād apaḥ pāmarī ।।
kasyacit । nidrāśeṣa-viśeṣa-rakta-nayano niryāya nīḍodarād āsṛkkānta-vidāritānana-puṭaḥ pārāvato jṛmbhate ।। bhṛṅgārasya । kiṃcit kuñcita-locanāṃ sahacarīṃ saṃcumbya cañcvā ciraṃ manāndolita-kaṇṭha-kuṇṭhita-galaḥ sotkaṇṭham utkūjati ।।
vikramāditya-tapasvinoḥ । madhye-jalaṃ buḍḍati datta-jhampaḥ samatsyam utsarpati matsya-raṅkaḥ ।। vākpati-rājasya । udgrīvam utpuccham udeka-pādam uccūḍam ukūjati tāmra-cūḍaḥ ।।
madhoḥ । nyag-jānu-dvaya-yantra-yantrita-ghaṭī-vaktrāntarāla-skhaladdhārādhvāna-manoharaṃ sakhi payo gāṃ dogdhi dāmodaraḥ ।। upādhyāya-dāmodarasya ।। ārād vīkṣya vipakva-sākrama-kṛta-krodha-sphurat-kandharaṃ śvā mallīkalikā-vikāśi-daśanaū kiṃcit kvaṇan gacchati ।।
taṃ cemaṃ ca karoti mūḍha-jaḍa-dhīḥ kāmāndha-mugdho yatas tundau tundita-vigrahasya surate naiko bhaven nāparaḥ ।। pīnorudvaya-līna-cīna-vasanā stokāvanamrā jalāt tīrodde`ca-nimeṣa-lola-nayanā bāleyam uttiṣṭhati ।। ākarṇayanti kariṇo ardha-nimīlitākṣā dhārā-ravaṃ daśana-koṭi-niṣaṇṇa-hastāḥ ।। hastipakasya ।
calat-pakṣa-dvandva-prabhava-marud-uttambhita-rajaḥkaṇāśleṣa-bhrāmad-ruta-mukulitonmīlita-dṛśaḥ ।। lālā-kīrṇa-vidīrṇa-sṛkka-vikacad-daṃṣṭrākarālānanaḥ śvā niḥśvāsa-nirodha-pīvara-galo mārjāram āskandati ।। viyati vidhṛtaikāṅghris tirag vivartita-kandharo dalam api calat sa-pratyāśaṃ muhur muhur īkṣate ।। kasyacit ।
ātmoddhatair api rajobhir alaṅghanīyā dhāvanty amī mṛga-javākṣamayeva rathyāḥ ।। ghāsa-grāsābhilāṣād anavarata-calat-protha-tuṇḍas turaṅgo mandaṃ śabdāyamāno vilikhati śayanād utthitaḥ kṣmāṃ khureṇa ।। kasyacit ।। pṛṣṭhāntaḥ pārśva-kaṇḍū-vyapa-nayana-rasād dvis-trir-udvartitāṅgaḥ protthāya drāṅ nirīhaḥ kṣaṇam atha vapur āsyānupūrvyāṃ dhunoti ।।
vikramādityasya । mātrā pravartita-mukhaṃ mukha-lihyamānapaścārdha-sustha-manasaḥ stanam utpibanti ।। priyā-prema-prāṇa-pratibhaya-vaśākṛta-vikalo mṛtgaḥ paścād ālokayati ca muhur yāti ca muhuḥ ।। kasyacit ।
dūrādhva-bhrānti-khinnaḥ katham api śanakair aṅghri-pīḍāṃ niyamya svairendha-sphoṭanāya dvija-bhavanam anu snātakaḥ sāyam eti ।। vāraṃ vāram udaṅghri-laṅghana-ghana-preṅkhan-nakha-kṣuṇṇayoḥ kāmaṃ kukkuṭayor dvayaṃ druta-pada-krūra-kramaṃ yudhyati ।। kasyacit । helāndolita-nartitojjhita-hata-vyāghaṭṭitonmūlitaprotkṣipta-bhramitaiḥ prapā-paṭalakaiḥ krīḍanti jhañjhānilāḥ ।।
tāruṇyātiśayāgra-pāmara-vadhū-sollāsa-hasta-grahabhrāmyat-pīvara-yantraka-dhvanir asad-gambhīra-gehodarāḥ ।। dhūmodgāras taruṇa-mahiṣa-skandho anīlo davāgneḥ svairaṃ sarpan sṛjati gagane gatvarān patra-bhaṅgān ।। grāmā nistṛṇa-jīrṇa-kuḍya-bahulāḥ svairaṃ bhramad-babhravaḥ prāyaḥ pāṇḍu-kapota-kaṇṭha-mukharārāme na yānty utkatām ।। pavana-raya-tiraścīs toya-dhārāḥ pratīcchan viśati valita-śṛṅgaḥ pāmarāgāram ukṣā ।।
bhekāḥ pūtini-pātino micimicīty unmīlitārrdhekṣaṇāḥ nakrākāra-vidāritānana-puṭair nirmakṣikaṃ kurvate ।। calanti kala-duṅkṛti-prasabha-kampitoraḥ-sthalatruṭad-gamaka-saṃkulāḥ kalama-kaṇḍanī-gītayaḥ ।। kasyacit । bahir vrajati sātape smarati netra-varteḥ pumān jarā-pramukha-saṃsthitaḥ samavalokayan pustakam ।।
varāhasya । svairaṃ śvāsānila-taralitodbhūta-dhūlī-praveśapluṣṭa-prāṇā vihita-vidhuta-grāsa-vighnaṃ caranti ।। sīmani laghu-paṅkāyām aṅkura-gaurāṇi cañcitoraskāḥ । laghutaram utplavamānāś caranti bījānti kalaviṅkāḥ ।।
karāmbuja-dhṛtollasan-muśalam unnamantī muhuḥ pralambi-maṇi-mālinī kalam akaṇḍanī rājate ।। utkaṇṭhālasa-kūjitaḥ kala-rutāṃ bhūyo riraṃsā-rasanyag-bhūtāṃ caṭakaḥ priyām abhisaraty udvepamānaḥ kṣaṇam ।। sonnokasya । vicchidyamāna-kusumāsu jani-krameṇa pāka-kramaḥ kapiśimānam upādadhāti ।।
dhunānā mūrdhānaṃ gala-bila-galat-sphāra-śapharasphurat-pucchānaccha-vyatikara-sa-bāṣpākula-dṛśaḥ ।। kasyacit । niśvāsair atisaṃtatair buṣa-kaṇā-jālaṃ khale vikṣipann ukṣā goṣṭha-taṭīṣu labdha-vijayo go-vṛndam āskandati ।। agre agre saṃraṭantaḥ pracuratara-masīpāta-durlakṣa-dhūmrāḥ dhūmyāṭāḥ paryaṭanti prativiṭapam amī niṣṭhurāḥ sva-sthalīṣu ।।
gandhena sphuratā manāg anusṛto bhaktasya sarpiṣmataḥ karkandhū-phala-miśra-śāka-pacanāmodaḥ paristīryate ।। mama dadata ivārghaṃ puṣpa-vṛṣṭiṃ kirantaḥ kathaya nati-saparyāṃ śikṣitāḥ śākhino api ।। dvāropānta-paśūkṛtārpya-puruṣa-kṣubdhāsthi-kirmīritāḥkirmīritāś cittotkampam ivānayanti gahanāḥ kāntāra ।। tumbī-vīnā-vinoda-vyavahita-sarakām ahni jīrṇe purāṇīṃ hālāṃ mālūra-koṣair yuvati-sahacarā barbarāḥ śīlayanti ।।
yogeśvarasya । pariṇati-paripāṭi-vyākṛtenāruṇimnā hata-haritim aśeṣaṃ nāga-raṅgaṃ cakāsti ।। ।। ।।
āścaryaṃ gaganasya ko api mahimā sarvair amībhiḥ sthitair dūre pūraṇam asya śūnyam iti yan-nāmāpi nācchāditam ।। keśarasya । kṣīrāmbu-rāśim avalokaya śeṣa-nālam ekaṃ jagat-traya-saraḥ-pṛthu-puṇḍarīkam ।। kumbhodbhavas tu tam apīyata helayaiva satyaṃ na kaścid avadhir mahatāṃ mahimnaḥ ।।
tyāgaḥ ko api sa tasya bibhrati jaganty asyārthino apy ambudāḥ śakteḥ kaiva kathāpi yasya bhavati kṣobheṇa kalpāntaram ।। vācaspateḥ । asmān mandara-kūṭa-koṭi-ghaṭanā-bhīti-bhramat tārakāṃ prāpyaikāṃ jala-mānuṣīṃ tri-bhuvane śrīmān abhūd acyutaḥ ।। muñja-rājasya ।
ekasyāśraya-ghasmarasya pibatas tṛptir na jātā jalair anyasyāpi mahātmano na vapuṣi svalpo api toya-vyayaḥ ।। tathā sarvasvārthe bahu-vimathito yena sa hariḥ svapity aṅke śrīmān ahaha mahimā ko api jaladheḥ ।। vandyaṃ taj-jaṭharaṃ sa mīna-makara-grāhāvalis toyadhiḥ paścād pt pārśvam apūritāntara-viyad yatra svanan bhrāmyati ।। sīmā sarva-mahādbhuteṣu sa tathā vārāṃ patiḥ pīyate pītaḥ so api na pūritaṃ ca jaṭharaṃ tasmai namo agastaye ।।
vācaspateḥ ।। sūryād ṛte na tad udeti na cāstam eti yenoditena dinam astam itena rātriḥ ।। kasyacit । śauryaṃ yac ca na tad-girāṃ pathi nanu vyaktaṃ hi tat karmabhiḥ satyaṃ brahma-tapo-nidher bhagavataḥ kiṃ nāma lokāntaram ।।
itaś ca vaḍavānalaḥ saha samasta-saṃvartakair aho vitatam ūrjitaṃ bharasahaṃ ca sindhor vapuḥ ।। abhyudgate sakala-dhāma-nidhau tu tasminn indoḥ sitābhra-paṭalasya ca ko viśeṣaḥ ।। madhukūṭasya । padaṃ kṛtvā yaḥ svaṃ phaṇi-pati-phaṇā-cakra-valaye nimajjantīm antarjaladhi vasudhām uttulayati ।।
varāhasya । viśvopakāra-jananī-vyavasāya-siddhim ambhomucāṃ jaladhayo yadi pūrayanti ।। maināko api gabhīra-nīra-viluṭhat-pāṭhīna-pṛṣṭhollasacchevālāṅkura-koṭi-koṭara-kuṭī-kuḍyāntare nirvṛtaḥ ।। āścaryaṃ kalasodbhavo sa jaladhir yasyaika-hastodare gaṇḍūṣīyati paṅkajīyati phaṇī bhṛṅgīyati śrīpatiḥ ।।
kasyacit । antaḥ prajvalatā payāṃsi dahatā jvālāvalīr muñcatā ke na syur vaḍavānalena balinā bhasmāvaśeṣīkṛtāḥ ।। keśaṭasya । kiṃ cāsmāj jaṭharānalād iva navas tat-kālavānti-kramād niryātaḥ sa puno yamāya payasām antargato vāḍavaḥ ।।
asty anyo api pralaya-rajanī-saṃnipāte apy anidro yaḥ sāmudrīr aviratam imās tejasi sve juhoti ।। ।। vipady uccaiḥ stheyaṃ padam anuvidheyaṃ ca mahatāṃ satāṃ kenoddiṣṭaṃ viṣamam asi-dhārā-vratam idam ।। puro vā paścād vā tad idam aviparyāsita-rasaṃ rahasyaṃ sādhūnām anupadi viśuddhaṃ vijayate ।।
adyaiva vā maraṇam astu yugāntare vā nyāyyāt pathaḥ pravicalanti padaṃ na dhīrāḥ ।। vidhīyate guṇair eva tac ca muktā-maṇer iva ।। yadā kiṃcit kiṃcid budha-jana-sakāśād adhigataṃ tadā mūrkho asmīti jvara iva mado me vyapagataḥ ।। anuharataḥ khala-sujanāv agrima-pāścātya-bhāgayoḥ sūcyoḥ ।
ekaḥ kurute cchidraṃ guṇavān anyaḥ prapūrayati ।। āndolitās tu namana-spṛhayā pareṇa bhajyanta eva śatadhā na punar namanti ।। satāṃ tu na viśaty eva yadi vā pāradāyate ।। sarva-lokasya vā mūrdhni śīryate vana eva vā ।।
itthaṃ mānada nātidūram ubhayor apy āvayor antaraṃ yady asmāsu parāṅmukho asi vayam apy ekāntato niḥspṛhāḥ ।। iti prāyo bhāvāḥ sphurad-avadhi-mudrā-mukulitāḥ satāṃ prajñonmeṣaḥ punar ayam asīmā vijayate ।। rājaśekharasya । tulyair api guṇaiś citraṃ santaḥ santaḥ śarāḥ śarāḥ ।।
yaśasi cābhiratir vyasanaṃ śrutau prakṛti-siddham idaṃ hi mahātmanām ।। na tu durvihitātītavastu-pālana-paṇḍitaḥ ।। sāphalyam asti sutarām idam eva teṣāṃ yat tāpayanti hṛdayāni punaḥ khalānām ।। ekasya śāmyati snehād vardhate anyasya vāritaḥ ।।
phalanti ca parārthāya pādapā iva sajjanāḥ ।। sadā lokahite saktā ratna-dīpā ivottamāḥ ।। aho kim api citrāṇi caritrāṇi mahātmanām ।। aho sumanasāṃ vṛttir vāma-dakṣiṇayoḥ samā ।।
para-guṇa-tattva-grahaṇaṃ sva-guṇāvaraṇaṃ para-vyasana-maunam । madhuram aśaṭhaṃ ca vākyaṃ kenāpy upadiṣṭam āryāṇām ।। yadā tu cakṣuḥ-patham eti dehināṃ tadāmṛteneva manāṃsi siñcati ।। yat tṛṣṇā-glapito api necchati janaḥ pātuṃ tad eva kṣaṇād ujjhaty ambudharodara-sthitam apāṃ patyuḥ payaḥ kṣāratām ।।
kāraṇe api na kupyanti ye te jagati pañcaṣāḥ ।। sujanāḥ paruṣābhidhāyino yadi kaḥ syād aparo api mañju-vāk । yadi candra-karāḥ sa-vahnayo nanu jāyeta sudhā kṛto anyataḥ ।। maṅgalasya ।।
svasthāḥ saty api yauvanodaya-mahā-vyādhi-prakope api ye te bhū-maṇḍala-maṇḍanaika-tilakāḥ santaḥ kiyanto janāḥ ।। anviṣyanty arthino nārthān nisargo ayaṃ mahātmanām ।। santaḥ kodaṇḍa-dharmāṇo viramanti tathā tathā ।। udāra-caritānāṃ tu vasudhaiva kuṭumbakam ।।
hrīmantaḥ sva-guṇa-praśaṃsana-vidhāv anya-stutau paṇḍitā dhig dhātrā kṛpaṇena yena na kṛtāḥ kalpānta-dīrghāyuṣaḥ ।। hṛdi svacchā vṛttir vijayi-bhujayor vīryam atulaṃ vināpy aiśvaryeṇa sphurati mahatāṃ maṇḍanam idam ।। lokottarāṇāṃ cetāṃsi ko hi vijñātum arhati ।। ā paritoṣād viduṣāṃ na sādhu manye prayoga-vijñānam ।
balavad api śikṣitānām ātmany apratyayaṃ cetaḥ ।। santaḥ parīkṣyānyatarad bhajante mūḍhaḥ para-pratyaya-hārya-buddhiḥ ।। guhya-pidhānaika-paraḥ sujano vastrāyate sadā piśunam । bhavatām ayaṃ viḍambo yad idaṃ chidrair visūtrayatu ।।
aṅgulī-kathanād eva yan na jīvanti māninaḥ ।। saṃbhūyāpi jagat-trayasya nayanair draṣṭuṃ na yat śakyate pratyādiśya dṛśau samāhita-dhiyaḥ paśyanti tat-paṇḍitāḥ ।। kasyacit । yeṣāṃ guṇamayaṃ janma pareṣāṃ guhya-guptaye ।।
ātmanāvaiti te lokaḥ sva-bandhur iti dhāvati ।। satatam asatyād bibhyati mā bhaiṣīr iti vadanti bhīteṣu । atithi-jana-śeṣam aśnati sajjana-jihve kṛtāthāsi ।। yady api daivāt sneho naśyati sādhos tathāpi sattveṣu ।
ghaṇṭā-dhvaner ivāntaś ciram anubadhnāti saṃskāraḥ ।। ।। ।। atimaline kartavye bhavati khalānām atīva nipuṇā dhīḥ ।
timire hi kauśikānāṃ rūpaṃ pratipadyante dṛṣṭiḥ ।। vane puṣpa-kalākīrṇaḥ karabhaḥ kaṇṭakān iva ।। nirmāṇam āśā-nāśāya durjanasya ghanasya ca ।। itthaṃ tad bhuvi nāsti yatra vidhinā nopāya-cintā kṛtā manye durjana-citta-vṛtti-haraṇe dhātāpi bhagnodyamaḥ ।।
viṣaṃ mahāher iva yasya durvacaḥ suduḥsahaṃ saṃnihitaṃ sadā mukhe ।। dhruvaṃ tadaiva lokānāṃ kalyāṇam avagamyate ।। mahā-kāla-phaleneva kaḥ khalena na vañcitaḥ ।। sūtraṃ kiṃcid apūrvam eva jaṭharād utpādya sadyaḥ svayaṃ lūtā-tantu-vitāna-jāla-kuṭilaṃ cakraṃ karoty adbhutam ।।
vāsasāpi na yogo asti niścakrasya pinākinaḥ ।। aho na sadṛśī vṛttis tulākoṭeḥ khalasya ca ।। ākhubhyaḥ kiṃ khalair jñātaṃ khalebhyaḥ kim athākhubhiḥ । anyad pt para-gṛhotkhātāt karma yeṣāṃ na vidyate ।।
durjana-dūṣita-manasāṃ puṃsāṃ svajane api nāsti viśvāsaḥ । bālaḥ pāyasa-dagdho dadhy api phūtkṛtya bhakṣayati ।। na ced evaṃ tādṛk kamala-kalikārdha-pratinidhau muneḥgr gaṇḍūṣe abdhiḥ sthita iti kuto ayaṃ kalakalaḥ ।। mṛdam iva balāt piṇḍīkṛtya pragalbha-kulākavad bhramayati mano no jānīmaḥ kim atra vidhāsyati ।।
ko apy anya eṣa piśuno atra bhujaṅga-dharmā karṇe paraṃ spṛśati hanty aparaṃ sa-mūlam ।। pariśuddhām api vṛttiṃ samāśrito durjanaḥ parān vyathate । pavanāśino api bhujagāḥ paropaghātaṃ na muñcanti ।। jagad bhrāmī-kartuṃ pariṇata-dhiyānena vidhinā sphuṭaṃ sṛṣṭo vyādhiḥ prakṛti-viṣamo durjana-janaḥ ।।
tasyāsya bhogina ivogra-ruṣaḥ khalasya dākṣiṇyam asti katham anya-guṇopamarde ।। svārthārthaṃ mṛdu-bhāṣiṇīṣṭa-vihatav ekāntatas toṣiṇi śreyaḥ kruddha-bhujaṅga-bhoga-viṣame saṃvidyate kiṃ khale ।। tejasviny avaliptatā mukharatā vaktary aśaktiḥ sthire tat ko nāma bhaved guṇaḥ sa guṇināṃ yo durjane nāṅkitaḥ ।। guhyāni prakaṭī-karoti ghaṭayaty anyonya-vairāśrayān brūte śīghram avācyam ujjhita-guṇo gṛhṇāti doṣān khalaḥ ।।
ata eva khalo doṣān sādhubhyaḥ saṃprayacchati ।। karuṇā-dravam eva durjanaḥ sutarāṃ sat-puruṣaṃ prabādhate । mṛdukaṃ hi bhinatti kaṇṭakaḥ kaṭhine kuṇṭhaka iva jāyate ।। dinasya pūrvārdha-parārdha-bhinnā chāyeva maitrī khala-sajjanānām ।।
itīmaṃ vyāmohaṃ parihara vicitrāḥ śṛṇu kathā yathāyaṃ pīyūṣa-dyutir upala-khaṇḍaṃ dravayati ।। upakāriṇi śuddha-matau vārjane yaḥ samācarati pāpam । taṃ janam asatya-saṃdhaṃ bhagavati vasudhe kathaṃ vahasi ।। kṣaṇena viṣatāṃ yānti sūkta-pīyūṣa-bindavaḥ ।।
na kaḥ khalāt tāpita-mitra-maṇḍalād upaiti pāpaṃ tapa-vāsarād iva ।। śaṅkhas tāpa-krakaca-nicayair bhidyate śaṅkha-kāraiḥ ko nāmāntaḥ-prakṛti-kuṭilo durgatiṃ nābhiyāti ।। akalita-nija-para-rūpaḥ svakam api doṣaṃ para-sthitaṃ vetti । nāvāsthitas taṭasthān acalān api vicalitān manute ।।
agnir eva tathāpy asmin syād bhasmani hutaṃ hutam ।। na pravṛddhis tu vistārilāñchana-pratipādinī ।। sarvatra mukhara-capalāḥ prabhavanti na loka-saṃmatā guṇinaḥ । tiṣṭhanti vāri-rāśeḥur upari taraṅgās tale maṇayaḥ ।।
prāyo vairāvasānāni saṃgatāni khalaiḥ saha ।। guṇa-kaṇikān api sujanaḥ śaśilekhām iva śivaḥ śirasi kurute । candra iva padma-lakṣmīṃ na kṣamate para-guṇaṃ piśunaḥ ।। niṣpannam api yaḥ pātraṃ guṇenaiva nikṛntati ।।
para-saṃtāpana-hetur yatrāhani na prayāti niṣpattim । antar-manā asādhur gaṇayati na tad-āyuṣo madhye ।। divasān tān abhinandati bahu-manute teṣu janmano lābham । ye yānti duṣṭa-buddheḥ paropatāpābhiyogena ।।
yatas tu bhaya-śaṅkayā sukṛśayāpi saṃspṛśyate vinīta iva nīcakaiś carati tatra śāntoddhavaḥ ।। tat ketakī-reṇubhir amburāśer bandha-kriyāyām api kaḥ prayāsaḥ ।। yenedānīṃ malina-hṛdayo lakṣyate śīta-raśmir yasmāc cāyaṃ hṛdaya-rahito durvidhaḥ sarvadaiva ।। viśaṅkitānyonya-bhayaṃ sudūrān namaskriyām arhati sauhṛdaṃ tat ।।
ete snigdhatamā iti mā mā kṣudreṣu kuruta viśvāsam । siddhārthānām eṣāṃ sneho apy aśrūṇi pātayati ।। durjanasyāuṣadhaṃ nāsti kiṃcid anyad anuttarāt ।। dvijihve dṛṣṭa-mātre cet kasya na syāc camatkṛtiḥ ।।
krūrasya cāprabhavataḥ para-drohaḥ sarasvatīm ।। tatas tad dārayaty asya vācaḥ krakaca-karkaśāḥ ।। hetor vinopakārī yadi nāma śateṣu kaścid ekaḥ syāt । tatrāpi kliṣṭa-dhiyāṃ doṣaṃ vakṣyaty atikhalatvam ।।
baddhevātanu-rajjubhiḥ para-guṇān vaktuṃ na śaktā satī jihvā loha-śalākayā khala-mukhe viddheva saṃlakṣyate ।। ubhayam idam avaśyaṃ jāyate sarva-vāraṃ paṭur api niyatātmā kīrtim evābhidhatte ।। ।। ।।
muṣṭy-āvaṣṭabhya yaṣṭiṃ kaṭi-puṭa-vicaṭat-karpaṭaḥ pluṣṭa-kanthaḥ kunthann utthāya pānthaḥ pathi paruṣa-marun-mūrcchyamānaḥ prayāti ।। utkampī karpaṭārghe jarati pada-hati-cchidrite cchinna-nidro vāte vāti prakamaṃ hima-kaṇini kaṇan koṇataḥ koṇam eti ।। paścād ambhodhara-jala-parīpātam āsādya tumbī kūṣmāṇḍī ca prabhavati tadā bhūbhujaḥ ke vayaṃ ke ।। gehinyāḥ sphuṭitāṃśukaṃ ghaṭayituṃ kṛtvā sakāku-smitaṃ kupyantī prativeśinī pratidinaṃ sūcīṃ yathā yācitā ।।
kasyacit । kaṭyācchādana-bandhakena katham apy āsāditenāndhasā sindūrāruṇa-maṇḍale savitari prāṇāhutir dīyate ।। sūrya-sphurat-kara-karambita-bhitti-deśa -lābhāya śīta-samaye kalim ācaranti ।। etat soḍhavato api duḥstha-gṛhiṇaḥ kiṃ brūmahe durdaśām adya śvo vijaniṣyamāṇa-gṛhiṇī tatraiva yat kunthati ।।
kasyacit । ity aśru-pāta-malinī-kṛta-gaṇḍa-deśā necched daridra-gṛhiṇī rajanī-virāmam ।। kasyacit । dattvā mūrdhani śīrṇaṃ śūrpa-śakalaṃ jīrṇe gṛhe vyākulā kiṃ tad yan na karoti duḥstha-gṛhiṇī deve bhṛśaṃ varṣati ।।
yogeśvarasya । jarad-ambara-saṃvaraṇa-granthi-vidhau grantha-kāra eko aham । parimita-kadanna-baṇṭana-vidyā-pāraṃ-gatā gṛhiṇī ।। vīrasya ।
śrutvaivaṃ gṛhiṇī-vacāṃsi nikaṭe kuḍyasya niṣkiṃcano niśvasyāśru-jala-phutānata-mukhaḥ pānthaḥ punaḥ proṣitaḥ ।। tat saṃyācya kutaścid īśvara-gṛhād ānīyamānaṃ śanaiḥ adhvany eva hi bindubhir vigalitaṃ śrāṇe śarāvodare ।। ity evaṃ gṛhiṇī-pracaṇḍa-vadanā-vākyena nirbhartsito hasta-nyasta-palāla-muṣṭi-vibhavaḥ pānthaḥ śanair gacchati ।। ekaḥ śīrṇa-jarad-gavo vidhivaśāt sarvasva-bhūto gṛhe sarveṇaiva kuṭumbakena rudatā suptaḥ samutthāpyate ।।
kasyacit । mamāmbara-vihīnasya tvag eva paṭikāyate ।। yadi na syān manorājyarajjubhir dṛḍha-saṃyatam ।। lajjā-nigūḍha-vacaso bata bhoktu-kāmā bhoktāram ardha-nayanena vilokayanti ।।
kasyacit । etāni me vidadhatas tava sarvadaiva dhātas trapā yadi na kiṃ na pariśramo api ।। vardhana-mukhāsikāyām udara-piśācaḥ kim icchakām icchan । paryākulayati gṛhiṇīm akiṃcanaḥ kṛpaṇa-saṃvāsaḥ ।।
ekasya bandhuḥnr nādatte nāmāny asyākhilo janaḥ ।। vibhavas tasya tad-doṣaghoṣaṇā-paṭu-ḍiṇḍimaḥ ।। māṃsaṃ vardhayatānena kākasyopakṛtiḥ kṛtā ।। śrīphalaṃ yan na tad dīrgham iti tāvad vyavasthitam ।
tatraikānta-dhṛtir yasya manyate mugdha eva saḥ ।। dṛḍhatara-nibaddha-muṣṭeḥ koṣa-niṣaṇṇasya sahaja-malinasya । kṛpaṇasya kṛpāṇasya ca kevalam ākārato bhedaḥ ।। idam ahi-bhramitaṃ paca-mandiraṃ balibhujo api na yānti yad-antikam ।।
tena kiṃ na kṛto mṛtyur martyānāṃ vibhava-kṣaye ।। tenaiva niśi śītāṃśur aho daurgatyam etayoḥ ।। ātmanaivātma-kathakā vayaṃ vāyasa-vṛttayaḥ ।। pūrvāparāparāmarśād vimūḍhasyeva me matiḥ ।।
।। ।। tārābhāḥ phaṇa-cakravāla-maṇayo na syur yadi dyotino yair evonnatim āpnuvanti guṇinas tair eva yānty āpadam ।। tṛptas tat-piśitena satvaram asau tenaiva yātaḥ pathā svasthās tiṣṭhata daivam eva jagataḥ śāntau kṣaye cākulam ।।
teṣām asṛk pibati saiva mahī hatānāṃ śrīḥ prāyaśo vikṛtim eti bahūpabhuktā ।। ravir yāty evāntaṃ pratidinam apārasya nabhasaḥ kriyā-siddhiḥ sattve bhavati mahatāṃ nopakaraṇe ।। akṣāṇāṃ ca yudhiṣṭhireṇa mahatā jñāto na doṣaḥ kathaṃ pratyāsanna-vipatti-mūḍha-manasāṃ prāyo matiḥ kṣīyate ।। tulottīrṇasyāpi prakaṭa-nihatāśeṣa-tamasoaḥ raves tādṛk tejo na hi bhavati kanyāṃ gata iti ।।
anena dṛṣṭānta-yugena gamyate sad-artha-saṃkoca-samudyato vidhiḥ ।। tatrānayor vadata kasya guṇātirekaḥ prāyaḥ paricchada-kṛtādara eva lokaḥ ।। śaktā hi kūpam api śoṣayituṃ na kumbhāḥ kumbhodbhavena punar ambudhir eva pītaḥ ।। kaḥ kālakūṭam abhinandati sāgarotthaṃ ko vāravindam abhinindati paṅkajātam ।।
tatrāpy āśu kadācid eva patatā bilvena bhagnaṃ śiraḥ prāyo gacchati yatra bhāgya-rahitas tatrāpadāṃ bhājanam ।। avastheyaṃ sthāṇor api bhavati yatrāmara-guror vidhau vakre mūrdhni sthitavati vayaṃ ke punar amī ।। ka ete saṃbandhān malaya-marutaś cūta-taravo yad etān ālabhya pratiparurudānaṃ janayati ।। vātāpitāpana-muneḥ kalaśāt prasūtir līlāyitaṃ punar amuṣya samudra-pānam ।।
ajānānas tattvaṃ na sa mṛgayate anyāṃ ca sarasīm abhūmau pratyāśā na hi phalati vighnaṃ ca kurute ।। kiṃ tv aṅgīkṛtam utsṛjan kṛpaṇavad ślāghyo jano lajjate nirvyūḍhiḥ pratipanna-vastuṣu satām ekaṃ batāho vratam ।। dugdhābdhi-labdha-janano hara-kandharā-sthaḥ svāṃ kālatāṃ tyajati jātu na kālakūṭaḥ ।। śarvasyety avagamya yāti vimukhī ratnālayaṃ jāhnavī kaṣṭaṃ durgatikasya jīvitam aho dārair api tyajyate ।।
daivāt tato api galito gilito bakena vāme vidhau vada kathaṃ vyasanasya śāntiḥ ।। vahati tu dhuraṃ dhuryo dhairyād anuddhata-kandharo jagati kṛtinaḥ kāryaudāryād pt parān atiśerate ।। adho adho gaṅgāvad vayam upagatā dūram athavā pada-bhraṃśetānāṃ bhavati vinipātaḥ śatamukhaḥ ।। unnataṃ yad avadhīrya bhūdharaṃ nīcam abdhim abhiyāti jāhnavī ।।
na daśati punas tārāśaṅkī divāpi sitotpalaṃ kuhaka-cakito lokaḥ satye apy apāyam avekṣate ।। asthānābhiniveśī prāyo jaḍa eva bhavati no vidvān । bālād anyaḥ ko ambhasi jighṛkṣatīndoḥ sphurad-bimbam ।। nirguṇam apy anuraktaṃ prāyo na samāśritaṃ jahati santaḥ ।
saha-vṛddhi-kṣaya-bhājaṃ vahati śaśāṅkaḥ kalaṅkam api ।। avikāriṇam api sajjanam aniśam anāryaḥ prabādhate atyartham । kamalinyā kim apakṛtaṃ himasya yas tāṃ sadā dahati ।। ekaikaṃ daśakandhara-kṣaya-kṛto rāmasya kiṃ varṇyate daivaṃ varṇaya yena so api sahasā nītaḥ kathā-śeṣatām ।।
tribhuvana-patir lakṣmīṃ tyaktvā hariḥ priya-gopikaḥ paricita-guṇa-dveṣī loko navaṃ navam icchati ।। niyata-viṣayāḥ sarve bhāvā na yānti hi vikriyāṃ janayitum alaṃ śāler bījaṃ na jātu javāṅkuram ।। khagānāṃ ke meghāḥ ka iha vihagā vā jala-mucām ayācyo nārtānām anupakaraṇīyo na mahatām ।। bhartṛhareḥ ।
chalān nīto adhastād balir aṇuka-rūpeṇa tad api svabhāvāc cakrī yaḥ praguṇam api cakreṇa sṛjati ।। rāhos tu cakra-patito astamito ayam induḥ satyaṃ satām ahṛdayeṣu guṇās tṛṇāni ।। tāpāt kaṭhoratara-yantra-nipīḍanāni sneho nimittam iti duḥkha-paraṃmparāyāḥ ।। dugdha mugdham asti yas tvayā dhṛtaḥ sneha eṣa vipad-eka-kāraṇam ।
yat-kṛte tvam apavāsitaṃ punaś chinnam unmathitam agni-sātkṛtam ।। nandī dvāri bahiṣkṛto guṇanidhiḥ kaṣṭaṃ kim atrocyatāṃ pātrāpātra-vicāraṇāsv anipuṇaḥ prāyo bhaved īśvaraḥ ।। pārthasyāpi parābhavaṃ yadi ripuḥnr nādāt kva tādṛk tapo nīyante ripubhiḥ samunnati-padaṃ prāyaḥ paraṃ māninaḥ ।। sthāna-pracyutir alpakasya vipade santas tu deśāntaraṃ yānto yānti sadā samarpita-guṇāḥ ślāghyāḥ parām unnatim ।।
sudhā-sūtiḥ so ayaṃ tripura-hara-cūḍāmaṇiraho prayāty astaṃ hanta prakṛti-viṣamā daiva-gatayaḥ ।। jarāsaṃdhād bhagnaḥ saha halabhṛtā dānava-ripur jaghānainaṃ paścān na kim anila-sūnuḥ priya-sakhaḥ ।। mūrdhnā tathāpi vidhṛtaḥ parameśvareṇa naivāśriteṣu mahatāṃ guṇa-doṣa-cintā ।। nityaṃ yathārtha-ghaṭanāhita-mānasānāṃ svārthodyamo bhavati no mahatāṃ kadācit ।।
anyonya-miśritam api vyatiricya śuddhaṃ dugdhaṃ pibaty udakam ujjhati rājahaṃsaḥ ।। antaḥ-pratapta-maru-saikata-dahyamānamūlasya campaka-taroḥ ka vikāśa-cintā ।। graha-parikavalita-tanur api ravir iha bodhayati padma-ṣaṇḍāni । bhavati vipady api mahatām aṅgīkṛta-vastu-nirvāhaḥ ।।
cātakaḥ svalpam apy ambu gṛhṇāty ananta-kandharaḥ ।। pada-pramāṇam ādhāram ārūḍhaḥ ko na kampate ।। kathaṃcil labdhāni pravitarati toyāni jagate guṇaṃ vā doṣaṃ vā gaṇayati na dāna-vyasanitā ।। vallaṇasya ।
ravir jānāty eva pratidivasam astādri-patanaṃ tathāpi pratyagrābhyudaya-taralaḥ kiṃ na kurute ।। ।। ity arthāntaranyāsa-vrajyā ।। ।। bhānor vājibhir aṅga-karṣaṇa-rasāsvādaḥ samāsādito labdhaḥ kiṃ ca nabhas-talāmara-dhunī-paṅkeruhair anvayaḥ ।।
kasyacit । bibhrāṇāḥ pāri-bhadra-druma-kusuma-ruco raśmayaḥ patyur ahnāṃ madhyāhne apy asta-saṃdhyā-bhrama-cakita-dṛśaś cakrire cakravākān ।। varṣe amuṣmin pratinṛpa-yaśaḥ-pūra-gaure parīkṣākṣīra-nyastaṃ tulayati mahā-nīla-ratnaṃ kṛpāṇaḥ ।। dig-dantinaḥ sva-kara-puṣkara-lekhanībhir gaṇḍa-sthalān madamasiṃ muhur ādadānāḥ ।
śrī-candra-deva tava toya-nidhi-tīra-tāḍī-patrodareṣu vijaya-stutim ālikhanti ।। śubhra-kīrtyāsi tat satyaṃ catur-varṇāśramo bhavān ।। na janayasi kaṃsa-harṣaṃ vahasi śarīraṃ yaśodayā juṣṭam । tyajasi na satyonmukhatām iti satyaṃ vāsudevo asi ।।
guṇo vā vṛddhir vā satatam upakārāya jagatāṃ muner dākṣī-putrād api tava samarthaḥ pada-vidhiḥ ।। pāṇineḥ । vāryante yadi cāpsaraḥ-pariṣadā te cāmarāḍambarair udvellad-bhuja-valli-kaṅkaṇa-jhaṇat-kāras tadā duḥsahaḥ ।। tat-pītaṃ tvad-yaśobhis tribhuvanam abhajaṃs tāni viśrāma-hetos tac cāntaḥ kaiṭabhāreḥ sa ca tava hṛdaye vandanīyas tvam ekaḥ ।।
tathāgata-dāsasya । tat-saudhānāṃ parisara-bhuvi tvat-prasādād idānīṃ krīḍā-yuddha-cchidura-yuvatī-hāra-muktāḥ patanti ।। śubhāṅkasya । yāni praṇāma-militāni nṛṇāṃ lalāṭe lumpanti daiva-likhitāni durakṣarāṇi ।।
abhinandasya । sarvāśā-paripūrako jaladharas tvaṃ ced vayaṃ bhūruhaḥ san-mārga-sthiti-sundaras tvam iti cec chākhī vayaṃ cādhvagāḥ ।। dakṣasya । pada-hīnān bila-vasatīn bhujagān iva jāta-bhoga-saṃkocān ।
vyathayati mantrākṣaram iva nāma tavārīn vanecarair gītam ।। tasyaiva । ṣaḍ-jādi-krama-raṅgad-aṅguli-calat-pāṇi-skhalat-kaṅkaṇaśreṇī-nisvana-māṃsalaḥ kala-girāṃ vīṇā-ravaḥ śrūyate ।। kasyacit ।
nātha tvām anuyāce prasīda vijahīhi saṃgarārambham । unnati-bhājaḥ saṃprati santi vipakṣāḥ paraṃ girayaḥ ।। yām ekaḥ sva-śarīra-śuddhi-rasiko mūrdhnā pratīcchan ripur dvaividhyād anu pañcatāṃ tad anu ca traidaśyam āpa kṣaṇāt ।। rathāṅgasya ।
ity ullāsita-vīci-bāhur udayān mārtaṇḍa-bimba-cchalāt prātas tapta-kuṭhāram eṣa vahate deva tvad-agre ambudhiḥ ।। vasukalpasya । pratyāsanna-vipanna-vāraḍa-vadhū-netra-praṇālī-galadbāṣpāmbhaḥ-plava-paṅka-picchila-talāḥ śrī-muñja modāmahe ।। kasyacit ।
hemante hima-śīta-māruta-bhayād āśliṣya dorbhyāṃ tanuṃ svāṃ mūrtiṃ dayitām ivātirasikāṃ tvad-vidviṣaḥ śerate ।। nirlagnāḥ kvacid ekatām upagatā baddhāḥ kvacin mocitāḥ akṣāṇām iva śārayaḥ pratigṛhaṃ bhrāntās tavāri-striyaḥ ।। mugdhā-vyādha-vadhūs tavāri-nagare śūnye cirāt saṃprati svarṇopaskṛti-muṣṭi-sāyaka-dhiyā sākūtam āditsati ।। kasyacit ।
rājñāṃ tvac-caraṇāravindam atha ca śrīcandra puṣpanty amūś cañcac-cāru-marīci-sañcaya-mucāṃ cūḍāmaṇīnāṃ rucaḥ ।। ākrāntaṃ mahiṣībhir eva śayanaṃ tvad-vidviṣāṃ mandire rājan saiva cirantana-praṇayinī-śūnye api rājya-sthitiḥ ।। vijaya-pālasya । deva tvad-vijaya-pratāpa-dahana-jvālāvalī-śoṣitāḥ sarve vāridhayas tato ripu-vadhū-bāṣpāmbubhiḥ pūritāḥ ।।
vindhya-skandheṣu dhātu-drava-racita-kuca-prānta-patrāṅkurāṇi krīḍanti kroḍa-lagnaiḥ kapi-śiśubhir aviśrāntam antaḥ-purāṇi ।। kiṃ cāsyāṃ jalakeli-lālasa-valan-nāgāṅganānāṃ phaṇaśreṇībhir maṇi-keśarābhir abhavat saṃbhūtir ambhoruhām ।। kodaṇḍena śarāḥ śarai ripuśiras tenāpi bhū-maṇḍalaṃ tena tvaṃ bhavatā ca kīrtir anaghā kīrtyā ca loka-trayam ।। saṃgrāmāṅgaṇasya ।
yam uccair ākarṇya tridaśa-patir apy āhava-bhiyā hriyā pārśvaṃ paśyan nibhṛta-nibhṛtaṃ muñcati dhanuḥ ।। prātar nidrā-vinoda-krama-janita-mukhonmīlitaṃ cakṣur ekaṃ vyādhāḥ pālāla-bhasma-sthita-dahana-kaṇākāram ālokayanti ।। tair etat samalaṃkṛtaṃ nija-kulaṃ kiṃ vā bahu brūmahe ye dṛṣṭāḥ parameśvareṇa bhavatā tuṣṭena ruṣṭena vā ।। jayādityasya ।
antas-toṣa-tuṣāra-saurabha-maya-śvāsānilāpūraṇaprāṇottuṅga-bhujaṅga-talpam adhunā bhadreṇa nidrāyate ।। ity evaṃ ripu-mandireṣu bhavataḥ śṛṇvanti naktaṃcarā golāṅgūla-vimarda-saṃbhrama-vaśād udyāna-devī-giraḥ ।। śubhāṅkasya । adyāyaṃ para-cakra-bhūma-nṛpater voḍhuṃ trilokī-dhuraṃ prauḍhārāti-ghaṭā-vighaṭṭana-paṭur dordaṇḍa evodyataḥ ।।
hastāhallita-hāra-valli-taralā yuddhāṅgaṇālokanakrīḍālola-dig-aṅganā-samudayonmuktāḥ kaṭākṣā iva ।। jihvā-yugmābhipūrṇānanda-viṣama-samudgīrṇa-varṇābhirāmaṃ velā-śailāṅka-bhājo bhujaga-yuvatayas tvad-guṇān udgṛṇanti ।। lakṣmī-sadma-saroja-reṇu-suhṛdaḥ sevāvanamrī-bhavadbhūmīpāla-kirīṭa-ratna-kiraṇa-jyotsnā-nadī-bālikāḥ ।। vallaṇasya ।
iti sucaritair bibhrad rūpaṃ cirantana-bhūbhujāṃ katham asi na māndhātā deva triloka-vidhāyy api ।। kasyacit । yadi tad aguṇaṃ kaṇṭhe mā dhās tathorasi mā kṛthā navam iti kiyat karṇe dhehi kṣaṇaṃ phalatu śramaḥ ।। vīrya-mitrasya ।
dadāti tac ca tenāsti rājan citram idaṃ mahat ।। nārayo lebhire pṛṣṭhaṃ na vakṣaḥ para-yoṣitaḥ ।। mārgaṇaughaḥ samāyāti guṇo yāti dig-antaram ।। hārāvaruddha-kaṇṭhāpi vihārāri-vadhūs tava ।।
pratyakṣe api kaliṅga-maṇḍala-pater antaḥ-purāṇām aho dhik kaṣṭaṃ viṭapair viṭair iva vane kiṃ nāma nāceṣṭitam ।। tvad-vairi-vīra-vanitānayanāmbu-leśaśoṣe kathaṃ pratihatā iti me vitarkaḥ ।। kasyacit । deva kṣmāvalaya-prabho phaṇi-kulaiḥ pravyaktam ekottarasthūla-stambha-sahasra-dhāritam iva kṣmā-cakram ālokyate ।।
kasyacit । nāsīre ca muhur muhuś calacalety ālāpa-kolāhalān kartuṃ nātha varuthinīyam avanīṃ jetuṃ punas tvad-bhujau ।। kasyacit । dṛṣṭaḥ prāroha-śālī vaṭa iva phalito rakta-mūrdhanya-ratnaḥ kūrmeṇoddhṛtya kaṇṭhaṃ nija-vipula-vapuś catvare sarparājaḥ ।।
nimnatvaṃ girayaḥ samaṃ viṣamatāṃ śūnyaṃ jana-sthānakaṃ niryāte tvayi rājya-pāla bhavati tyakta-svabhāvaṃ jagat ।। mahodadheḥ । ataḥ pariharanty ājāvasiṃ dūreṇa te arayaḥ ।। ity ākūta-juṣas tava stava-kṛtā vaitālikenodite lajjante pramadāḥ parasparam abhiprekṣyārayo bibhyati ।।
kasyacit । naivaṃ ced vas tadānīṃ pradhana-dhṛta-dhanur mukta-rāvarṇa-viddhaṃ gṛdhrā mūrdhānam ūrdhvaṃ nabhasi rabhasino lāghavenoddharanti ।। bhavān īhita-kṛn nityaṃ tvaṃ himānī-giri-sthitaḥ । ataḥ śaṅkara evāsi sadā skandaḥ paraṃ na te ।।
itthaṃ khinna ivātyayena yaśasā datto avalambo ambudher yātas tīra-tapo-vanāni bhavato vṛddho guṇānāṃ gaṇaḥ ।। kasyacit । stana-yugam aśru-snātaṃ samīpatara-varti-hṛdaya-śokāgneḥ । carati vimuktāhāraṃ vratam iva bhavato ripu-strīṇām ।।
prātar bhāvini darśane mukulitaṃ dṛṣṭe tu deva tvayi protphullaṃ phalitaṃ ca saṃprati manorājya-drumeṇādya me ।। kasyacit । bhūti-vibhūṣita-dehāḥ kāntā-rāgeṇa labdha-mahimānaḥ । trikaliṅga-nyasta-karā bhavad-arayas tvat-samār jātāḥ ।।
tat paśyāmi ca rohaṇo maṇi-bharair ādhmāya-mānodaraḥ pākotpīḍita-dāḍimī-phala-dṛśāṃ kaiścid dinair yāsyati ।। kasyacit । tāpaṃ ca saṃmada-rasaṃ ca ratiṃ ca tanvan śauryoṣmaṇā ca vinayena ca līlayā ca ।। śrī-hanūmataḥ ।
tad viśrāmaya vīra vīrya-niviḍa-jyā-bandhanāt kārmukaṃ mā bhūd vairi-vadhū-vilocana-jalair mārga-kramo durgamaḥ ।। dārikāri-karīndrāṇāṃ subhaṭānāṃ ca kuṭṭanī ।। suptasyādri-nadi-nikuñja-gahane mattaḥ payodānilaiḥ karṇānte maśakaḥ kim apy ari-vadhū-sārthasya te jalpati ।। lambamāna-nayanāmbu-bindavaḥ kandarāsu gahanāsu bhūbhṛtām ।
ākapola-tala-lola-kuntalāḥ sañcaranti tava vairi-yoṣitaḥ ।। sārdhaṃ bandhubhir aṅgasya yā parasmaipade sici ।। padmāyāḥ śvasitānilāni ca śarat-kālasya tac ca sphuṭaṃ vyomādāya vinirmito asi vidhinā kāmboja tubhyaṃ namaḥ ।। bhavad-bhuja-bala-prauḍhiparityājita-hetayaḥ ।।
no vā dikkariṇaḥ kvaṇan madhulihaḥ paryāya-paryāṇanakrīḍāyāṃ viniyojitā vada kṛtaṃ kiṃ kiṃ tvayā dig-jaye ।। dakṣasya । diṅ-mohākula-sūra-sūta-vipatha-bhrāmyat-turaṅgāvalīdīrghāyuḥ kutavāsaraṃ pratidiśaṃ vyasto ravir tāmyati ।। kasyacit ।
asyodayāt prabhṛti vāñchati dāna-pātraṃ cintāmaṇir yadi dadāti dadātu tāvat ।। kṣīra-kṣmāruhi vāyaso madhura-vāg-vāmā śiveti dhruvaṃ tvāṃ pratyuccalatāṃ narendra-tilaka prādurbhavanty arthinām ।। kasyacit । tatas tato nalina-vanādhivāsinī tad-īpsayā kila kamalānudhāvati ।।
kasyacit । ruditaṃ vanecarair api vindhyādri-nivāsibhis tavāri-śiśau । vana-mānuṣīṣu hastaṃ phala-hastāsu prasārayati ।। ātmaiva saṃgara-mukhe nija-maṇḍalāgracchāyā-chalād abhimukhas tava deva jātaḥ ।।
nija-gṛha-mayūra-nāmabhir āhūtānāgateṣu vana-śikhiṣu । bāla-tanayena rudatā tvad-ari-vadhū roditā dīrgham ।। namrī-bhūtaiḥ phalam abhinavaṃ prāpyate yady avaśyaṃ tat kiṃ kūpāḥ sukṛta-ghaṭitās tvādṛśā vā pumāṃsaḥ ।। na syās tvaṃ yadi deva paṅgula-guṅdaḥ kāle kalāv utkale so ayaṃ paṅgur avasthitaika-caraṇo dharmaḥ kathaṃ bhrāmyati ।।
cittūkasya । tulyas tvayā yadi paraṃ sahadeva eva duḥśāsanas tava punar nanu ko api śatruḥ ।। arciś tigmāṃśu-rocir gagana-malinimā kajjalaṃ dahyamānā śatru-śreṇī pataṅgā jvalati narapate tvat-pratāpa-pradīpaḥ ।। śrī-hanūmataḥ ।
jāne dāna-vilāsa dāna-rabhasaṃ śauryaṃ ca te śuśruvān eko mantha-vighaṭṭanās tad-aparaṣ ṭaṅkā-hatīḥ śaṅkate ।। iti praśna-śraddhākulitam iva karṇāntikam agān mṛgākṣīṇāṃ cakṣuś caṭulatara-tārānta-taralam ।। kvacin na krodhas te svapada-jita-devas tvam udadher abhinno api svāmin na kim asi samudraḥ sva-viṣaye ।। ।।
asmākaṃ tu manorathoparacita-prāsāda-vāpī-taṭakrīḍā-kānana-keli-mandira-sadām āyuḥ paraṃ sīdati ।। kasyacit । paśya bhrātar iyaṃ hi gaurava-jarā-dhikkāra-keli-sthalī māna-mlānimasī guṇa-vyatikara-prāgalbhya-garbha-cyutiḥ ।। duṣer dhātor ivāsmākaṃ doṣa-niṣpattaye guṇaḥ ।।
alīkāhaṅkāra-jvara-kuṭilita-bhrūṇi dhanināṃ mukhāni prekṣyante dhig idam atiduṣpūram udaram ।। śaurye vairiṇi vajram āśu nipatatv artho astu naḥ kevalaṃ yenaikena vinā guṇās tṛṇa-lava-prāyāḥ samastā ime ।। pratyutthānam itas tataḥ pratidinaṃ kurvadbhīr udgītibhir yad dhārārpita-dṛṣṭibhiḥ kṣiti-bhujāṃ vidvadbhir apy āsyate ।। yad īśānām agre draviṇa-kaṇa-mohāndha-manasāṃ kṛtaṃ vīta-vrīḍair nija-guṇa-kathā-pātakam api ।।
ataḥ khedo nāsmin aparam anukampaiva bhavati sva-māṃsa-trastebhyaḥ ka iva hariṇebhyaḥ paribhavaḥ ।। nītaṃ naiva yaśaḥ surendra-bhavanaṃ śastreṇa śāstreṇa vā kālo jīrṇa-maṭheṣu dhṛṣṭa-piśunaiś chātraiḥ saha preritaḥ ।। priyam api vaco mithyā vaktuṃ jaḍair na ca śikṣitaṃ ka iva hi guṇo yo asmān kuryān nareśvara-vallabhān ।। kṛto vitta-stambha-pratihata-dhiyām añjalir api tvam āśe moghāśe kim aparam ato nartayasi mām ।।
kṛtā laṅkā-bhartur vadana-paripāṭīṣu ghaṭanā mayāptaṃ rāmatvaṃ kuśala-vasutā na tv adhigatā ।। abhinandasya । tad anu tat-kṣaṇa-bhaṅgi karoti ced ahaha kaṣṭam apaṇḍitatā vidheḥ ।। sat-puruṣa-pakṣa-pātini bhagavati bhavitavyate namas tubhyam ।
yā tvaṃ svayam akṛtajñaṃ jaḍam akulīnaṃ na saṃspṛśati ।। namo astu tasyai bhavitavyatāyai yasyāḥ phalaṃ bandhanam eva jātam ।। guṇavatyaḥ kulīnebhyo dīyante katham anyathā ।। lajje tiṣṭha parāṅ-mukhī kṣaṇam itas tṛṣṇu puraḥ sthīyatāṃ pāpo yāvad ahaṃ bravīmi dhanine dehīti dīnaṃ vacaḥ ।।
api jñātvā śāstraṃ kaṭakam aṭato jīryati vapus tato re pāṇḍityaṃ yad iha na sukhaṃ no api ca tapaḥ ।। vidyā-late tapasvini vikasita-sita-kusuma-vākya-saṃpanne । virama varaṃ bhramarahite na phalasi bhuktiṃ ca muktiṃ ca ।। aiśvarya-sīdhu-rasa-pāna-vighūrṇamānāḥ ke nāma na pratipadaṃ puruṣāḥ skhalanti ।।
svalpa-draviṇa-kaṇā vayam amī ca guṇino daridrati sahasram । dāna-vyasana-lavo hṛdi dhig dhātaḥ kiṃ viḍambayasi ।। etāvat tu hṛdi vyathāṃ vitanute yat-prāktanaiḥ karmabhir lakṣmīṃ prāpya jaḍo apy asādhur api ca svāṃ yogyatāṃ manyate ।। kasyacit ।
īśvara-gṛham idam atra hi viṣaṃ ca vṛṣabhaś ca bhasma cādriyate । yas tu na viṣaṃ na vṛṣabho na bhasma tasyātra kā gaṇanā ।। kāma-ghnād viṣa-sadṛśo bhūty-avaliptād bhujaṅga-saṅga-ruceḥ । ko bhṛṅgīva na śuṣyati vāñcha na phalam īśvarād aguṇāt ।।
sahante guṇalobhena ta eva maṇayo yadi ।। dṛṣṭaḥ kiṃ kvāpi kenāpi kardamāt kandukodgamaḥ ।। hṛt-paṭṭake yad yad ahaṃ likhāmi tat tad vidhir lumpati sāvadhānaḥ । bhūyo vilopān masṛṇe tv idānīṃ rekhāpi nodeti manorathasya ।।
mām eṣa yācitum upāgata ity asatyasaṃbhāvanā-vikalam asya na cen manaḥ syāt ।। sann apy asad-rūpatayaiva vedyo dāridrya-mudro guṇa-ratna-koṣaḥ ।। svaṃ varṇayasy atha kathaṃ kula-putra mānī hā mugdha dagdha-jaṭhareṇa viḍambito asi ।। sārasavattā vihatā na bakā vilasanti carati no kaṅkaḥ ।
sarasīva kīrti-śeṣaṃ gatavati bhuvi vikramāditye ।। iti nirasta-samasta-sukhānvayaḥ katham ato na viṣīdatu paṇḍitaḥ ।। vyādhānāṃ śara-gocarād atijavenotplutya gacchan mṛgaḥ kūpāntaḥ-patitaḥ karotu viguṇe kiṃ vā vidhau pauruṣam ।। kasyacit ।
kāmaṃ vaneṣu hariṇās tṛṇena jīvanty ayatna-sulabhena । vidadhati dhaniṣu na daintyaṃ te kila paśavo vayaṃ sudhiyaḥ ।। vasumati vasumati bandhau dhana-lava-lobhena ye niṣīdanti । tān ca tṛṇān iva dadhatī kalayasi vada gauravaṃ kasya ।।
yad indoḥ pīyūṣa-drava-maya-mayūkhotkara-kiraḥ kalaṅko ratnaṃ tu pratiphaṇam anarghaṃ viṣa-bhṛtām ।। uttīrṇas tu tato dhanārtham aparāṃ bhūyo viśaty āpadaṃ prāṇānāṃ ca dhanasya cāyam adhiyām anyonya-hetuḥ paṇaḥ ।। no vā vāma-vilocanāmala-mukhāmbhojeṣu bhṛṅgāyitaṃ mātuḥ kevalam eva yauvana-vana-cchede kuṭhārāyitam ।। bhartṛ-hareḥ ।
vidveṣānugamād anarjita-kṛpo rūkṣo jano vartate cakṣuḥ saṃhara bāṣpa-vegam adhunā kasyāgrato rudyate ।। idānīṃ vāk tūṣṇīṃ bhava kim u mudhaiva pralapasi kva pūjā-saṃbhāraḥ kva ca tava guṇollāsa-rabhasaḥ ।। dvi-jihvād anyeṣāṃ kva nanu guṇinām īśvara-juṣāṃ tvayā dṛṣṭo bhogaḥ kim iha viphalaṃ kliśyasi manaḥ ।। pradhvasta-sarva-guṇam arjita-doṣa-sainyaṃ dainyaṃ yad ādiśati tad vayam ācarāmaḥ ।।
asaṃtuṣṭaṃ cetaḥ kuliśa-kaṭhinaṃ jīvitam idaṃ vidhir vāmārambhas tad api ca mano vāñchati sukham ।। anyo mandiram āgataḥ paricayād aprāpta-kāmo gataḥ khinnāḥ smaḥ sva-paropakāra-karaṇa-klībāṃ vahantas tanum ।। kaliḥ kvāyaṃ pāpaḥ kva ca guṇa-nidher janma bhavato vidhiḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ sadṛśa-viniyogeṣv akuśalaḥ ।। ayaṃ mā bhūt kaścit pratanu-mati-kirmīrita-manaḥsamādhānonmīlat-sada-sad-iti-saṃdeha-vidhuraḥ ।।
yasyāgre cira-sañcitāni hṛdaye duḥkhāni saukhyāni vā saṃjalpya kṣaṇam ekam ardham athavā niḥśvasya viśrāmyate ।। ito apy agre tiṣṭhaty ayam ajagaro vistṛta-mukhaḥ kva yāyāt kiṃ kuryān mṛga-śiśur ayaṃ daiva-vaśagaḥ ।। kasyacit । vega-bhraśyat-taṭaruhavano dustarāvarta-vīciḥ kasyedānīṃ kaluṣa-salilaḥ kūlabhedī priyo asi ।।
śatānandasya । āho riktaḥ katham api bhaved eṣa daivāt tadānīṃ ko nāma syād ataṭa-kuharālokanair yasya kalpaḥ ।। meruṃ pradakṣiṇayato api divākarasya te tasya sapta turagā na kadācid aṣṭau ।। na tapaḥ sañcitaṃ kiṃcid gataṃ ca sakalaṃ vayaḥ ।।
prāyeṇa guṇa-pūrṇeṣu rītir lakṣmīvatām iyam ।। rambhe nopari padmayoḥbr bisalate nāgra-sphurat-pallave sauvarṇau na ghaṭau na nūtana-ghanāsannaḥ śaśī pārvaṇaḥ ।। dugdhā seyam acetanena jaratī dugdhasyatā gardabhī kaṣṭaṃ yat khalu dīrghayā dhana-tṛṣā nīco janaḥ sevitaḥ ।। kenāpareṇa kamale bata śikṣitāsi sāraṅga-śṛṅga-kuṭilāni viceṣṭitāni ।।
kasyacit । arthābhāve mṛdutā kāṭhinyaṃ bhavati cārtha-bāhulye । naikatrārtha-mṛdutve prāyaḥ śloke ca loke ca ।। ।। iti nirveda-vrajyā ।।
।। idānīṃ jitam asmābhis tavākiṃcit-karāḥ śarāḥ ।। yad api ca na kṛtaṃ nitambinīnāṃ stana-patanāvadhi jīvitaṃ rataṃ vā ।। ata eva tayoḥ sparśe loko ayaṃ śithilādaraḥ ।।
ko atrāparādhyati vidhiś ca śaṭhaḥ kuṭhārayogyaḥ kaṭhora-hṛdayaḥ kusumāyudhaś ca ।। svasti sukhebhyaḥ saṃprati salilāñjalir eṣa manmatha-kathāyāḥ । tā api mām ativayasaṃ tarala-dṛśaḥ saralam īkṣante ।। kasyacit ।
nirvāsyataḥ pradīpasya śikheva jaratāṃ matiḥ ।। bhaiṣajyam iva manyante yad anyamanasaḥ striyaḥ ।। keśā api virajyante jarayā kim utāṅganāḥ ।। kasyacit ।
no vedmi māṃ palita-varṇaka-bhājam etaṃ nāṭyena kena naṭayiṣyati dīrgham āyuḥ ।। viviktav ānatav eva daridrāv iva garhitau ।। ।। iti vārdhakya-vrajyā ।। ।।
sadyas taptaṃ śavasya jvalad iva piśitaṃ bhūri jagdhvārdha-dagdhaṃ paśyāntaḥ pluṣyamāṇaḥ praviśati salilaṃ satvaraṃ gṛdhra-saṅghaḥ ।। kasyacit । ulkālokaiḥ sphuradbhirnija-vadana-guhotsarpibhir vīkṣitebhyaś cyotat-sāndraṃ vasāmbhaḥ kvathita-śava-vapur-maṇḍalebhyaḥ pibanti ।। pāṇineḥ ।
ātta-srnāyvyv-antra-netraḥ prakaṭita-daśanaḥ preta-raṅgaḥ karaṅkād aṅka-sthād asthi-saṃstha-sthapuṭa-gatam api kravyam avyagram atti ।। vidyut-puñja-nikāśa-keśa-nayana-bhrū-śmaśru-jālair nabho lakṣyālakṣya-viśuṣka-dīrgha-vapuṣām ulkā-mukhānāṃ mukhaiḥ ।। etāḥ śoṇita-paṅka-kuṅkuma-kuṣaḥ saṃbhūya kāntaiḥ pibanty asthi-sneha-surāḥ kapāla-caṣakaiḥ prītāḥ piśācāṅganāḥ ।। kharjūra-druma-dadhna-jaṅghama-sita-tvaṅ-naddha-viṣvaktatasnāyu-granthi-ghanāsthi-pañjara-jarat-kaṅkālam ālokyate ।।
antaḥ-śīrṇa-karaṅka-karkara-tarat-saṃrodhi-kūlaṅkaṣasroto-nirgama-ghora-gharghara-ravā pāre-śmaśānaṃ sarit ।। saṃdaśyauṣṭha-piṭena bhugna-vadanaḥ pretaś citāgni-drutaṃ sūtkārair nalakāsthi-koṭara-gataṃ majjānam ākarṣati ।। vaktrodvāntāḥ patantyaś chimiti-śikhi-śikhā-śreṇayo asmin śivānāṃ asra-srotasy ajasra-sruta-bahala-vasā vāsa-visre svananti ।। patanty ete gṛdhrāḥ śava-piśita-lolānana-guhāgalal-lālā-kleda-snapita-nija-cañcū-bhaya-puṭāḥ ।।
tataḥ styānāḥ kaścid bhuvi nipatitāḥ śoṇita-kaṇāḥ kṣaṇād ucca-grīvo rasayati lasad-dirgha-rasanaḥ ।। śiro nāraṃ pretaḥ kavalayati tṛṣṇā-vaśa-valatkarālāsyaḥ pluṣyad-vadana-kuharas tūdgirati ca ।। sarvaiḥ krāmadbhir ulkānana-kavala-rasa-vyātta-vaktra-prabhābhir vyaktais taiḥ saṃvaladbhiḥ kṣaṇam aparam iva vyomni vṛttaṃ śmaśānam ।। hasta-nyasta-kapāla-kandara-darī-muktābhra-dhārāḥ pibann unmukta-dhvani-bhinna-karṇa-kuharaḥ kravyād ayaṃ nṛtyati ।।
।। iti śmaśāna-vrajyā ।। ।। tato vīra-vrajyā ।। abhyasyanti tathaiva citra-phalake laṅkā-pates tat punar vaidehī-kuca-patra-valli-valanā-vaidagdhyam ardhe karāḥ ।।
yācñā-dainya-parāñci yasya kalahāyante mithas tvaṃ vṛṇu tvaṃ vṛṇv ity abhito mukhāni sa daśagrīvaḥ kathaṃ kathyate ।। tal loka-pāla-sahitaḥ saha lakṣmaṇena cāpaṃ gṛhāṇa sadṛśaṃ kṣaṇam astu yuddham ।। lakpāvasāna-pavanollasitasya sindhor ambho ruṇaddhi kim u saikata-setubandhaḥ ।। etau saṅghaśriyaḥ ।।
asmeraṃ galitāśru-gadgada-padaṃ bhinna-bhruvā yady abhūd vaktreṣv ekam api svayaṃ sa bhagavān tan me pramāṇaṃ śivaḥ ।। draṣṭavyo asy amum eva bhārgava-baṭaḥ kaṇṭhe kuṭhāraṃ vahan paulastyasya puraḥ praṇāma-racita-pratyagra-sevāñjaliḥ ।। so ahaṃ durjaya-bāhu-daṇḍa-sacivo laṅkeśvaras tasya me kā ślāghā ghuṇa-jarjareṇa dhanuṣā kṛṣṭena bhagnena vā ।। kasyacit ।
śakrebha-kumbha-taṭa-khaṇḍana-caṇḍa-dhāmā yenaiṣa me na gaṇito yudhi candrahāsaḥ ।। āropya pracalāṅgulī-kisalaye mlānaṃ guṇāsphālane sphārākarṣaṇa-bhagna-parvaṇi punaḥ siṃhāsane mūrcchitam ।। rājaśekharasya । dik-kuñjarāḥ kuruta tat-tritaye didhīrṣāṃ rāmaḥ karotu hara-kārmukam ātatajyam ।।
