uttīrṇo ambu-nidhir dṛśaiva viṣadais tenāṭṭahāsormibhir laṅkeśasya ca laṅghito diśi diśi krūraḥ pratāpānalaḥ ।। yady acchinnaṃ daśamukha-śiras tasya tasyaiva kāntau saṃkrāmantyām atiśayavatī śeṣa-vaktreṣu lakṣmīḥ ।। itthaṃ jalpati saṃbhramolbaṇa-mukhe sugrīva-rāje muhus tenākekaram īkṣitaṃ daśa śanair bāṇān ṛjūkurvatā ।। ajagaram api cāhaṃ muṣṭi-niṣpiṣṭa-vaktraṃ nija-bhuja-taru-mūlasyālavālaṃ karomi ।।
yasyoraḥ-sthala-śoṇitāsavam ahaṃ pātuṃ pratijñātavān so ayaṃ mad-bhuja-pañjare nipatitaḥ saṃrakṣyatāṃ kauravāḥ ।। muhuḥ paśyan śrutvā rajani-cara-senā-kalakalaṃ jaṭā-jūṭa-granthiṃ draḍhayati raghūṇāṃ parivṛḍhaḥ ।। harir alasa-vilocanaḥ sagarvaṃ balam avalokya punar jagāma nidrām । adhigata-pati-vikramāsta-bhītis tu dayitāpi vilokayāñcakāra ।।
kiṃ cākāṇḍa-kṛtodyamas tripathagāsañcārinaukā-gaṇoaḥ gīrvāṇendra-phaṇīndrayor api dadau śaṅkāṃ viśaṅko api yaḥ ।। tārkṣyaḥ so api samaṃ nijena vibhunā jānāti māṃ rāvaṇaṃ vijñātaṃ sa jaṭāyur eṣa jarasā kliṣṭo vadhaṃ vāñchati ।। tatrādhāra-nibandhano yadi bhaved ādheya-dharmodayasḥ tad bhoḥ skanda gṛhāṇa kārmukam idaṃ nirṇīyatām antaram ।। bhartuḥnr nandana-devatā-viracita-srag-dāmni bhūmeḥ sutā vīra-śrīr iva yasya vakṣasi jagad-vīrasya viśrāmyatu ।।
।। ।। tataḥ praśasti-vrajyā ।। ambho gambhīra-nābhī-kuhara-kavalanomukta-paryasta-lolatkallolābaddha-mugdha-dhvani-cakita-kaṇat-kukkubhaṃ kāminībhiḥ ।।
kṛcchrāt pātāla-mūlāvila-bahula-nirālamba-jambāla-niṣṭhaḥ pṛṣṭhāṣṭhīla-pratiṣṭhām avanim avanamat karparaḥ kūrmarājaḥ ।। saṃsīdac-cakra-śalyākula-taraṇikarot pīḍitāśvīya-dattadvitrāvaskanda-mandaḥ katham api calati syandano bhānavīyaḥ ।। bhava-bhūteḥ । pratyūpyamāna-maṇi-kīlaka-gāḍha-bandhaprāṇaḥ phaṇapatir vasudhāṃ dadhāti ।।
laṅkāṅka trikakut-pratidhvani-ghanāḥ paryanta-yātrā-jaye yasya bhremuramandamandara-ravair āśā-rudho ghoṣaṇāḥ ।। kasyacit । itthaṃ śriyā kupitayeva ripūn vrajantyā saṃjaghnire samara-keli-sukhāni yasya ।। sarva-kṣatra-bhujoṣma-śātana-kalā-duḥśīla-doḥ-śālino vaṃśe tasya babhūvur adbhuta-guṇā dhārā-dharitrī-bhujaḥ ।।
kiṃ cāmībhir api sphuran-maṇitayā caṇḍāṃśukoṭi-bhramaṃ bibhrāṇair udapādi rāhu-bhuvane bhūyān subhikṣotsavaḥ ।। kasyacit । arthibhyo vasu varṣatā punar asau saṃrūḍha-ratnāṅkuraśreṇi-smera-śiraḥ-sahasra-śikharaḥ saṃvardhito rohaṇaḥ ।। karas tasyātyarthaṃ vahati śatakoṭi-praṇayitāṃ sa sarvasvaṃ dātā tṛṇam iva sureśaṃ vijayate ।।
muktā tena kṣameti tvaritam ari-gaṇair uttamāṅgaiḥ pratīṣṭhā pañcatvaṃ dveṣi-sainye sthitam avani-patir nāpa saṃkhyāntaraṃ saḥ ।। teṣu prauḍha-phalopamardavi-namac-chākhā-mukhārohibhis tyāgādvaitam aharniśaṃ sukṛtino yasyāmarair gīyate ।। lokān vācayati sma vikrama-mayim ākhyāyikām ātmanaḥ kvāpi kvāpy anugacchad-arjuna-kathā-saṃbhāra-lambhāvatīm ।। murāreḥ ।r etau
hastenāsima-yūkha-darbha-latikā-baddhena yuddhotsavaiḥ rājñā yena salīlam utkala-pater lakṣmīḥ punar-bhūḥ kṛtā ।। ।। iti praśasti-vrajyā ।। ।। etasmin pracalākināṃ pracalatām udvejitāḥ kūjitair udvellanti purāṇa-rohaṇa-taru-skandheṣu kumbhī-nasāḥ ।।
yeṣām unmada-jāgarūka-śikhini prasthe nameru-sthitāḥ śyāmām eva gabhīra-gadgada-giraḥ skandanti koyaṣṭayaḥ ।। ādhārīkṛta-kūrma-pṛṣṭha-kaṣaṇa-kṣīṇoru-mūlo adhunā jānīmaḥ parataḥ payodhi-mathanād uccaistaro ayaṃ giriḥ ।। etenaiva durātmanā jalanidher utthāpya pāpām imāṃ lakṣmīm īśvara-durgata-vyavahṛti-vyastaṃ jagan nirmitam ।। yasyopāntopasarpat-tapana-kara-dhṛtasyāpi padmasya mudrāṃ uddāmāno diśanti tripura-hara-śiraś-candralekhā-mayūkhāḥ ।।
amuṣmin āruhya sphaṭika-maya-sarvāṅga-subhage nirīkṣante yakṣāḥ phaṇi-pati-purasyāpi caritam ।। jala-gṛhaka-vitardikāsukhāni sphaṭika-girir giriśasya nirmimīte ।। gaurī-hasta-guṇa-pravṛddha-vapuṣaḥ puṣyanti dhātreyakabhrātṛ-sneha-sahoḍha-ṣaṇmukha-śiśu-krīḍā-sukhāḥ śākhinaḥ ।। yatrākṛṣṭa-kucāṃśuke mayi ruṣā vastrāya patrāṇi te cinvatyo vana-devatās taru-latām uccair vyadhuḥ kautukāt ।।
itthaṃ vṛddha-paramparā-pariṇatair yasmin vacobhir munīn adyāpy unmanayanti kānana-śukāḥ so ayaṃ girir mālyavān ।। kari-kavalana-śiṣṭaiḥ śākhi-śākhāgra-patrair aruṇa-saraṇayo amī sarvato bhīṣayante agrakuñjaiḥ । calita-śabara-senā-datta-go-śṛṅga-caṇḍa-dhvani-cakita-varāha-vyākulā vindhya-pādāḥ ।। kamalāyudhasya ।
latā-kuñje yāsām upanadi rata-klānta-śabarīkapola-svedāmbhaḥ-kaṇa-caya-nudo vānti marutaḥ ।। dakṣasya । ete tīrthāśrama-giri-sarid-garta-kāntāra-miśrāḥ saṃdṛśyante paricaya-bhuvo daṇḍakāvindhya-pādāḥ ।। bhavabhūteḥ ।
sīmānaḥ pradarodareṣu vivareṣv alpāmbhaso yāsv ayaṃ tṛṣyadbhiḥ pratisūryakair ajagara-sveda-dravaḥ pīyate ।। śiśira-kaṭu-kaṣāyaḥ styāyate śallakīnām ibha-dalita-vikīrṇa-granthi-niṣyanda-gandhaḥ ।। phala-bhara-pariṇāma-śyāma-jambū-nikuñjaskhalana-mukhara-bhūri-srotaso nirjhariṇyaḥ ।। vyāvalgad-bala-vairi-vāraṇa-vara-pratyagra-dantāhatiśvabhra-prasravad-abhra-sindhu-savana-prasnigdha-deva-drumāḥ ।।
kasyacit । ।। iti parvata-vrajyā ।। ।। mano manda-spandaṃ viharati cirāyābhivimṛśan na jāne kasyaiṣā pariṇatir udārasya tapasaḥ ।।
mudita-vihaga-śreṇī-citra-dhvani-pratināditā manasi na mudaṃ kasyā dadhyuḥ śivā vana-bhūmayaḥ ।। pāraṃ gatvā śrutaughasya dhanyā vanam upāsate ।। sīmantinī-viṣa-latā-gahanaṃ vyudasya ye avasthitāḥ śama-phaleṣu tapo-vaneṣu ।। krīḍā mugdha-mṛgair vayāṃsi suhṛdo naktaṃ pradīpaḥ śaśī svādhīne api dhane tathāpi kṛpaṇā yācanta ity adbhutam ।।
kasyacit । idānīm asmākaṃ jaraṭha-kamaṭhī-pṛṣṭha-kaṭhinā mano-vṛttis tat kiṃ vyasanini mudhaiva kṣapayasi ।। kasyacit । mātar jare maraṇam antikam ānayantyāpy antas tvayā vayam amī paritoṣitāḥ smaḥ ।
nānā-sukha-vyasana-bhaṅgura-parva-pūrvaṃ dhig yauvanaṃ yad apanīya tavāvatāraḥ ।। anyad vā sura-sindhu-saikata-taṭī-darbhāṣṭaka-srastarasthāne brahma-padaṃ samāhita-dhiyo dhyāyanta evāsmahe ।। kāle bāla-tṛṇāni khādasi sukhaṃ nidrāsi nidrāgame tan me brūhi kuraṅga kutra bhavatā kiṃ nāma taptaṃ tapaḥ ।। iti dhyātvā hṛṣyan kṣaṇam atha vighūrṇan kṣaṇam aho na jāne saṃsāraḥ kim amṛta-mayaḥ kiṃ viṣamayaḥ ।।
na prāptāni purā na saṃprati na ca prāptau dṛḍha-pratyayoaḥ vāñchā-mātra-parigrahāṇy api vayaṃ tyaktuṃ na tāni kṣamāḥ ।। yady asty evaṃ kuru bhava-rase lampaṭatvaṃ tadānīṃ no cec cetaḥ praviśa sahasā nirvikalpe samādhau ।। utpala-rājasya । niḥśaṅka-supta-hariṇī-kula-saṃkulāsu cetaḥ paraṃ valati śaila-vana-sthalīṣu ।।
manasi tattva-vidāṃ tu vivecake kva viṣayāḥ kva sukhaṃ kva parigrahaḥ ।। kasyacit । kiṃ tu mattāṅganāpāṅgabhaṅgi-lokaṃ hi jīvitam ।। taṃ vidvāṃsam iha stumaḥ kara-puṭībhikṣālpa-śāke api vā mugdhāvaktra-mṛṇālinī-madhuni vā yasyāviśeṣo rasaḥ ।।
vallaṇasya । hātavyo ayam asaṃstavāya visaraḥ saṃsāra ity ādikaṃ sarvasyaiva hi vāci cetasi punaḥ puṇyātmanaḥ kasyacit ।। silhaṇasya । idānīm asmākaṃ paṭutara-vivekāñjana-juṣāṃ samībhūtā dṛṣṭis tribhuvanam api brahma manute ।।
kasyacit । sadyaḥ-syūta-palāśa-patra-puṭikā-pātrī-pavitrī-kṛtaiḥ bhikṣā-saktubhir eva saṃprati vayaṃ vṛttiṃ samīhāmahe ।। tvattoyānta-śilā-niṣaṇṇa-vapuṣas tvad-vīcibhiḥ preṅkhatas tvan-nāma smaratas tad-arpita-dṛśaḥ prāṇāḥ prayāsyanti me ।। vākkūṭasya ।
iti vyaktodgāraṃ caṭula-vacasaḥ śūnya-manaso vayaṃ vīta-vrīḍāḥ śuka iva paṭhāmaḥ param amī ।। kasyacit । iti cira-sukha-prāptaḥ kiṃcin-nimīlita-locano vrajati nitarāṃ tuṣṭiṃ puṣṭaḥ śmaśāna-gataḥ śavaḥ ।। sāṅga-glāni sa-vepitaṃ sa-cakitaṃ sāntar-nidāgha-jvaraṃ vaktuṃ na tv aham utsaheya kṛpaṇaṃ dehīty avadyaṃ vacaḥ ।।
vrajantaḥ svātantryād atula-paritāpāya manasaḥ svayaṃ tyaktā hy ete śama-sukham anantaṃ vidadhati ।। kasyacit । yeṣāṃ dhūma-samūha-baddha-vapuṣaḥ sindhor amī bandhavo nirvyājaṃ paripālayanti jagatīr ambhobhir ambhomucaḥ ।। itthaṃ khaṭvāṅga-koṭau prakaṭita-daśanaṃ mañju-guñjat-samīraṃ rāgāndhānām ivoccair upahasitam aho moha-jālaṃ kapālam ।।
gato moho asmākaṃ smara-śabara-bāṇa-vyatikarajvara-jvālā śāntā tad api na varākī viramati ।। jñāna-śivasya । lasanto aṅke mātuḥ kuvalaya-dṛśāṃ puṇya-saritāṃ pibanti svacchandaṃ stanam adharam ambhaḥ sukṛtinaḥ ।। iha hi patatāṃ nāsty ālambo na vāpi nivartanaṃ tad api mahatāṃ ko ayaṃ moho yad evam anākulāḥ ।।
bhāryā me putro me dravyaṃ sakalaṃ ca bandhu-vargo me । iti me me kurvantaṃ paśum iva baddhvā nayati kālaḥ ।। kadaitat saṃpūrṇaṃ mama hṛdaya-vṛtter abhimataṃ bhaviṣyaty atyugraṃ parama-paritoṣopacitaye ।। āpāta-ramyā viṣayāḥ paryanta-paritāpinaḥ ।।
niśāntād asvantāt katham api viniṣkrānta-madhunā mano asmākaṃ dīrghām abhilaṣati yuṣmat-paricitim ।। śreyārthino hi puruṣāḥ para-tuṣṭi-hetor duḥkhārjitāny api dhanāni parityajanti ।। sura-patim api śvā pārśva-sthaṃ sa-śaṅkitam īkṣate gaṇayati na hi kṣudro lokaḥ parigraha-phalgutām ।। sa kiṃ dharmo yatra sphurati na para-droha-viratiḥ śrutaṃ tat kiṃ sākṣād upaśama-padaṃ yan na nayati ।।
kasyacit । kiṃ tair bhāvyaṃ mama sudivasair yatra te nirviśaṅkāḥ saṃprāpsyante jaraṭha-hariṇāḥ śṛṅga-kaṇḍū-vinodam ।। saṃpraty apistimita-vastram ivāṅga-lagnam etaj jihāsur api hātum anīśvaro asmi ।। kasyacit ।
dhyātaṃ vittam aharniśaṃ na ca punas tattvāntaraṃ śāśvataṃ tat tat karma kṛtaṃ yad eva munibhis tais taiḥ phalair vañcitam ।। kasyacit । vāsaś ca kīrṇa-paṭa-khaṇḍa-nibaddha-kanthā hā hā tathāpi viṣayān na jahāti cetaḥ ।। kasyacit ।
jānann apy avaśo viveka-virahān majjann avidyāmbudhau śṛṅgārīyati putra-kāmyati bata kṣetrīyati strīyati ।। kasyacit । ataḥ saṃyoge asmin paravati viyoge ca sahaje kim ādhāraḥ premā kim adhikaraṇāḥ santu ca śucaḥ ।। svāṃ saṃpadaṃ sakala-sattva-kṛtopakārān no dṛṣṭavān yad asi tac chava vañcito asi ।।
taiḥ śeṣe kṛta-kṛtyatām upagatair audāsyam ālambitaṃ saṃpraty eṣa vidher niyoga-vaśagaḥ karmāntarair badhyate ।। ।। iti śānti-vrajyā ।। ।। śarat-payoda-stha-sitārdha-tārakāpatha-pratispārdhi vapur dhinotu vaḥ ।।
tat khaṭvāṅga-rathāṅga-saṅga-vikaṭaṃ śrī-kaṇṭha-vaikuṇṭhayor vande nandimahokṣatārkṣya-pariṣan-nānāṅkam ekaṃ vapuḥ ।। kasyacit । anyāpi kiṃ na sakhi bhājanam īdṛśīnāṃ vairī na ced bhavati vepathur antarāyaḥ ।। keśaṭasya ।
yasyāḥ śvāsa-samīra-saurabha-patad-bhṛṅgāvalī-vāraṇakrīḍā-pāṇi-vidhūti-kaṅkaṇa-raṇatkāro muhur mūrcchati ।। kasyacit । tato yāval-līlā-kalaha-kupitāsmi priyatame sapatnīva prācī dig iyam abhavat tāvad aruṇā ।। kasyacit ।
vitata-kare apy anurāgiṇi mitre koṣaṃ sadaiva mudrayataḥ । ucitānabhijña-kairava kairava-hasitaṃ na te caritam ।। pṛthukārta-svara-pātraṃ bhūṣita-niḥśeṣa-parijanaṃ deva । vilasat-kareṇu-gahanaṃ saṃprati samam āvayor bhavanam ।।
gurur api galati vivekaḥ skhalati ca cittaṃ vinaśyati prajñā । patati puruṣasya dhairyaṃ viṣaya-viṣāghūrṇite manasi ।। rājani vidvan-madhye vara-surata-samāgame vara-strīṇām । sādhvasa-dūṣita-hṛdayo vāk-paṭur api kātarī-bhavati ।।
adātari samṛddhe api kiṃ kuryur anujīvinaḥ ।। hṛdaya-saṃgatam eva susaṃgataṃ na tanu-saṃgatam ārya susaṃgatam ।। dhanyā sā rajanī tad eva sudinaṃ dhanyaḥ sa eva kṣaṇo yatrājhāta-caraś-cirān nayanayoḥ sīmānam eti priyaḥ ।। kasyacit ।
gāḍhaṃ mekhalayā balān niyamitaḥ karṇotpalais tāḍitaḥ kṣiptaḥ pāda-tale tad-eka-śaraṇo manye ciraṃ sthāsyasi ।। yenodyat-pulakaiḥ prakampa-vikalair aṅgaiḥ kva karṇotpalaṃ kutrātmā kva ca mekhaleti galati prāyaḥ sa māna-grahaḥ ।। turuṣka-bhojadevayoḥ । unnīyānya-yuvāsya-kālima-karīṃ tāruṇya-ramyām imāṃ dhanyaṃ janma sahāmunaika-samayaṃ na prāpya taptaṃ hṛdā ।।
sītkāraṃ śikṣayati vraṇayaty adharaṃ tanoti romāñcam । nāgarakaḥ kim u milito na hi na hi sakhi haimanaḥ pavanaḥ ।। prāpte caiva samāgame sarabhasaṃ yac cumbanāliṅganāny etat-kāma-phalaṃ tad eva surataṃ śeṣaḥ paśūnām iva ।। kasyāpi ।
daṃṣṭrā-koṭi-visaṃkaṭāsya-kuharaḥ kurvan saṭām utkaṭāṃ utkarṇaḥ kurute kramaṃ kari-patau krūrākṛtiḥ keśarī ।। līlonmūlita-nartita-pratihata-vyāvartita-preritatyakta-svīkṛta-nihnuta-pracalita-proddhūta-tīra-drumāḥ ।। kasyāpi । paścāt kṣīṇa-dhanāṃ bahir nija-daśāṃ dṛṣṭvā mṛṇāla-cchalād arthibhyaḥ pradadau navendu-viśadāny asthīni padmākaraḥ ।।
kasyacit । sarvathā svahitam ācaraṇīyaṃ kiṃ kariṣyati jano bahu-jalpaḥ ।। yasmāl labhante lakṣāṇi nirguṇā api mārgaṇāḥ ।। kṛtvāpi koṣa-pānaṃ bhramara-yuvā purata eva kamalinyāḥ ।
abhilaṣati bakula-kalikāṃ madhulihi maline kutaḥ satyam ।। tenodgīya khalena garjati ghane smṛtvā priyā yat-kṛtaṃ tenādyāpi karaṅka-daṇḍa-patanāśaṅkī janas tiṣṭhati ।। kasyacit । ātape dhṛtimatā saha vadhvā yāminī-virahiṇā vihagena ।
sehire na kiraṇā hima-raśmer duḥkhite manasi sarvam asahyam ।। viśva-śvitra-mataṅginī-ghana-rasa-syandiny amanda-dhvanir gaṅgā-sāgara-saṃgamaḥ punar ivāpūrvaḥ samunmīlati ।। tat-pallī-pati-putri kuñjara-kulaṃ jīvābhayābhyarthanā dīnaṃ tvām anunāthati stana-yugaṃ patrāvṛtaṃ mā kṛthāḥ ।। vallaṇasya ।
sakhīṣu smerāsu prakaṭayati vailakṣyam adhikaṃ priyā prāyeṇāste hṛdaya-nihitātaṅka-vidhurā ।। atirabhasa-kṛtānāṃ karmaṇām ā vipatter bhavati hṛdaya-dāhī śalya-tulyo vipākaḥ ।। cittonmāda-karo vasanta-samayo grīṣmo api caṇḍātapaḥ kālaḥ kāla iti prahṛṣyati janaḥ kālasya kā ramyatā ।। aratnāloka-saṃhāryam avāryaṃ sūrya-raśmibhiḥ ।।
kālaḥ kalir jagad idaṃ na kṛtajñam ajñe sthitvā haniṣyati tavaiva mukhasya śobhām ।। dagdha-mandira-sāre api kasya vahnāv anādaraḥ ।। ajānānas teṣām api niyata-karma svaka-phalaṃ graha-grāma-grastā vayam iti jano ayaṃ pralapati ।। na sa virauti na cāpi na śobhate bhavati yojayitur vacanīyatā ।।
phalaṃ karmāyattaṃ yadi kim aparaiḥ kiṃ ca vidhinā namaḥ sat-karmabhyo vidhir api na yebhyaḥ prabhavati ।। sthitaḥ samīkṣyobhayatā parīkṣakaḥ karoty avajñopahataṃ pṛthag janam ।। ananta-nāma yad rūpaṃ tat tvayā vāmanī-kṛtam ।। manaḥ-khedas tv evaṃ katham akṛta-saṃketa-vidhayo mahā-mārge asmin no nayana-patham eṣyanti suhṛdaḥ ।।
bhrū-cāpākṛṣṭa-muktāḥ śravaṇa-patha-gatā nīla-pakṣmāṇa ete yāval līlāvatīnāṃ na hṛdi dhṛti-muṣo dṛṣṭi-bāṇāḥ patanti ।। ity evaṃ pathikaḥ karoti hṛdaye yāvat taror mūrdhani prodghuṣṭaṃ para-puṣṭayā tava tavety uccair vaco anekaśaḥ ।। āsthānī-bhavanaṃ vasanta-nṛpater devasya ceto-bhuvaḥ satrāgāram anuttaraṃ madhulihām ekaṃ prapā-maṇḍapam ।। madana-jvaram apanetuṃ kuru saṃprati satatam auṣadha-dvitayam ।
bālā-dhara-madhu-pānaṃ kuca-pīḍana-muṣṭi-yogaṃ ca ।। niraṅkuśa ivārūḍho matta-dvirada-mūrdhani ।। śakyaṃ darśayituṃ na pūga-phalavat kṛtvā dvidhedaṃ vapur yat satyaṃ sakhi vīkṣitaḥ khalu mayā nūnaṃ caturthyāḥ śaśī ।। yugaṃ naiva skandhe vahati nitarāṃ yāti dharaṇīṃ varaṃ śūnyā śālā na ca punar ayaṃ duṣṭa-vṛṣabhaḥ ।।
śoka-kṣobhe ca hṛdayaṃ pralāpair avadhāryate ।। na vedmi tad vastu yad atra loke sutāṅga-dhūler upamāna-pātram ।। nānya-janma-gata-tikta-vipākaṃ dṛṣṭa-saukhyam api karma vidhatte ।। upary upari paśyantaḥ sarva eva daridrati ।।
timiram idam indu-bimbāt pūtir gandho ayam amburahakoṣāt amburuha-koṣāt । ninditam abhijāta-mukhād yad alīkaṃ vacanam uccarati ।। tad dānāsava-pāna-matta-madhupa vyālola-gaṇḍaṃ gajaṃ sotkaṇṭhaṃ sabhayaṃ ca paśyati śanair dūre sthitas tāpasaḥ ।। kasyacit ।
vaicitryāpunar ukta-lāñchana-bhṛtaḥ khaṇḍena vākyena vā vyākṣepaṃ kathayanti pakṣmala-dṛśo lekhākṣara-śreṇayaḥ ।। yad bandhanaṃ bisalatātanutantavaś ca kasyāścid eṣa galitas tad anaṅga-lekhaḥ ।। rājaśekharasya । mṛṇālam etad valayī-kṛtaṃ tayā tadīya evaiṣa vataṃsa-pallavaḥ ।
idaṃ ca tasyāḥ kadalī-dalāṃśukaṃ yad atra saṃkrānta iva smara-jvaraḥ ।। vrajatv ambā mugdhe kṣaṇam iha vilambasva yadi vā sphuṭas tāvaj jātaḥ piśuna-vacasām eṣa viṣayaḥ ।। kutaḥ prāpya prītiṃ tuhina-giri-garbha-sthiti-juṣo apy asahyaḥ sahyeta priya-viraha-dāha-vyatikaraḥ ।। viṣṇor māyā-sahasrasya iyam ekā garīyasī ।।
vraṇaiḥ pūya-klinnaiḥ krimi-kula-citair ācita-tanuḥ śunīm abhyeti śvā hatam api nihanty eva madanaḥ ।। praviśyāntarlīnaṃ kim api suvivecyoddharati yaś ciraṃ ruddha-śvāsaḥ sa khalu punar eteṣu viralaḥ ।। ।। iti saṃkīrṇa-vrajyā ।। ।।
viśuddhoktiḥ śūraḥ prakṛti-subhagā bhāva-vigiras tathāpy antar modaṃ kam api bhavabhūtir vitanute ।। kasyacit । revā vindhya-pulīndra-pāmara-vadhū-jhañjhānila-preṣitaprāye arthe vacanāni pallavayituṃ jānāti yogeśvaraḥ ।। abhinandasya ।
bhoktuṃ svādu phalaṃ ca jīvita-taror yady asti te kautukaṃ tad bhrātaḥ śṛṇu rājaśekhara-kaveḥ sūktīḥ sudhā-syandanīḥ ।। śaṅkara-varmaṇaḥ । ābdhar laṅghita eva vānara-bhaṭaiḥ kiṃ tv asya gambhīratām āpātāla-vilagna-pīvara-vapur jānāti manthācalaḥ ।। murāreḥ ।
vālmīki-vāg-amṛta-kūpa-nipāta-lakṣmīm etāni bibhrati murāri-kaver vacāṃsi ।। romṇāṃ nṛtya-bhuvo vilocana-payaḥ-pūrābdhi-candrodayāḥ sāhitya-pratigaṇḍa-garva-galanaṃ glāni-kriyā-hetavaḥ ।। vallaṇasya । rathyā-garta-vigāhanādbhuta-kṛtair gāhyaḥ kva ratnākaro yasyāntaḥ-śapharāvamānana-taṭī-majjad-girīndrāḥ śriyaḥ ।।
yathā kiṃcit kiṃcit pavana-cala-cīnāṃśukatayā stanābhogaḥ strīṇāṃ harati na tathonmudrita-tanuḥ ।। astaṃgata-bhāra-viravi kāla-vaśāt kāli-dāsa-vidhu-vidhuram । nirvāṇa-bāṇa-dīpaṃ jagad idam adyoti ratnena ।। kasyacit ।
kaviḥ kumāra-dāso vā rāvaṇo vā yadi kṣamaḥ ।। asty anyas tu sa saṃniveśa-śiśiraḥ śabdārthayoḥ saṃgamo yenāmī sva-vaśena dagdha-kavayo mathnanti cetāṃsi naḥ ।। jayati kavi-kaṇṭha-haraḥ śrī-raghu-kāraḥ prameya-kedāre । yan-mati-dātra-vilūne śiloñcham iva kurvate kavayaḥ ।।
śaktyeva pāṇḍu-putrāṇāṃ gatayā karṇa-gocaram ।। samudrasya paraṃ pāraṃ kapiseneva setunā ।। utpādakā na bahavaḥ kavayaḥ śarabhā iva ।। parvate paramāṇau ca vastutvam ubhayor api ।।
saubhāgyaika-niveśa peśala-girām ādhāra dhairyāmbudhe dharmādri-druma rājaśekhara-sakhe dṛṣṭo asi yāmo vayam ।। kasyacit । idaṃ kāvyaṃ tattvaṃ sphurati tu yad atrāṇu paramaṃ tad antar-buddhīnāṃ sphuṭam atha ca vācām aviṣayaḥ ।। lasad bhūyo bhāvā mṛdur api vimardocita-tanuḥ kavīndra tvad-vāṇī harati hariṇākṣīva hṛdayam ।।
kasyacit । jihvā-durvyasanair upadrava-rujaḥ kurvanti ye duḥsutāḥ tān dṛṣṭvārtham itas tato nikhanati svaṃ niḥsvam ātanvatī ।। avidita-guṇāpi sat-kavi-bhaṇitiḥ karṇeṣu vamati madhu-dhārām । anadhigata-parimalāpi hi harati dṛśaṃ mālatī-mālā ।।
punaḥ sthito yo bhava-bhūti-rekhayā sa vartate saṃprati rājaśekharaḥ ।। kiṃ punar vikaṭāṭopapada-bandhā sarasvatī ।। yal lagnaṃ hṛdi puṃsāṃ bhūyo bhūyaḥ śiro na ghūrṇayati । tad api kaveḥ kim u kāvyaṃ kāṇḍo vā dhanvināṃ kim asau ।।
avagāḍheva gambhīramasṛṇaughā sarasvatī ।। na hy ekasmin atiśayavatāṃ saṃnipāto guṇānāṃ ekaḥ sūte kanakam upalas tat-parīkṣā-kṣamo anyaḥ ।। agamyāyām anyair diśi pariṇateś cārtha-vacasor mataṃ ced asmākaṃ kavir amara-siṃho vijayate ।। śālikasya ।
avandhyā ca khyātā bhuvi katham agamyā kavi-vṛṣaiḥ kathaṃ vā pīyūṣaṃ sravati bahu dugdhāpi bahubhiḥ ।। śabdārṇavasya । vāg arthau ca tulādhṛtāv iva tathāpy asman-nibandhānayaṃ loko dūṣayituṃ prasārita-mukhas tubhyaṃ pratiṣṭhe namaḥ ।। dharmakīrteḥ ।
tasyāpy arthi-janaikarohaṇa-girer lakṣmīr vṛthaivābhavad dakṣasyāsya na yena sundara-giraḥ karṇāvataṃsī-kṛtāḥ ।। yasya yathā vijñānaṃ tādṛk tasyeha hṛdaya-sad-bhāvaḥ । unmīlati kavi-puṅga-vacane ca purāṇa-puruṣe ca ।। bhavati viditaṃ pūrva-vyūḍho adhunā khilatāṃ gataḥ sa khalu bahulo vāmaḥ panthā mayā sphuṭam urjitaḥ ।।
tāṃ cārthine praṇaya-peśalam apradāya dhik taṃ manuṣya-padam ātmani yaḥ prayuṅkte ।। utpatsyate tu mama ko api samāna-dharmā kālo hy ayaṃ niravadhir vipulā ca lakṣmīḥ ।। kalā-saṃpad-ratna-vratati-viṭapānāṃ sura-taruḥ prakṛtyā gambhīraḥ kavir iha sa-śabdo vijayate ।। yaḥ śrī-vākpatirāja-pāda-rajasāṃ saṃparka-pūtaś ciraṃ diṣṭyā ślāghya-guṇasya kasyacid asau mārgaḥ samunmīlati ।।
paramādbhuta-rasa-dhāmany utsalite jagati vallanāmbhodhau । viśrānto rasa-bhāgas timitayati yathā gabhīrimā ko api ।। jihvāntaḥ kṛṣyamāṇeva na kavitve pragalbhate ।। kāvyaṃ ced avataṃsa-bhūpam abhajad dharmāyaṇaṃ karṇayos tātaḥ kiṃ bahu varṇyate sa bhagavān vaidarbha-garbheśvaraḥ ।।
yāvac ca prati-sāma-sāraṇa-vidhi-vyagrau karau brahmaṇaḥ stheyāsuḥ śruti-śukti-lehya-madhavas tāvat satāṃ sūktayaḥ ।। jagrantha durlabha-subhāṣita-ratna-koṣaṃ vidyākaraḥ sukṛti-kaṇṭha-vibhūṣaṇāya ।। ।। iti kavi-varṇana-vrajyā samāptā ।। ।।
samāpto ayaṃ subhāṣita-ratna-koṣa iti ।। paṇḍita-śrī-bhīmārjuna-somasya ।।
